## 7. The Calorie Bank (Full Engine, Cards, Settings, Every Number)

---

The Calorie Bank turns a rigid daily calorie limit into a flexible weekly budget. Eat under target on quiet days and bank the difference. Banked calories raise your targets later in the week. Eat over and the bank absorbs it by trimming the remaining days. It is one of the two flagship differentiators that move TrackKcal from "logger" to "AI nutritionist." It is premium only and shipped (current behavior as of v1.2.9).

The entire feature flows from one pure function. `calculateCurrentCycle` in `src/utils/calorieBankEngine.ts` is recomputed on every render that needs banking data. There are no stored running totals to drift. Edit a past meal and the bank reflects it instantly because it derives everything from local daily summaries plus config plus goals.

### Core concept

| Term | Definition | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Base daily target | The user's normal daily calorie goal (`goals.calories`, default 2000 if unset) | engine L128 |
| Weekly budget | `baseDailyTarget × daysInCycle` (14,000 on a 2,000 target full week) | engine L285 |
| Banked | Calories saved by eating under target on a past day, capped | engine `settleDay` |
| Spent / Surplus | Calories used by eating over target on a past day, capped for the bank | engine `settleDay` |
| Bank balance | `totalBanked − totalSpent`, floored at 0 | engine L219-220 |
| Adjusted target | A future/today target after redistribution | engine pass 2 |
| Cycle | A 7-day window. Resets, does not roll over. Unspent banked calories expire | engine + service |
| Utilization | `spent / banked × 100`, capped at 100, 0 if nothing banked | engine `calculateBankUtilization` |

### The engine: `calculateCurrentCycle`

Inputs: `config` (CalorieBankConfig), `summariesByDate` (Record of actual intake), `goals` (ExtendedGoalData), `now` (defaults to `new Date()`).

#### Cycle boundaries

- `getCycleStartDate(cycleStartDay, today)`: most recent occurrence of the configured start day on or before today. `cycleStartDay`: 0=Sun, 1=Mon, ..., 6=Sat. Algorithm: `daysBack = todayDow − cycleStartDay; if (daysBack < 0) daysBack += 7`.
- `getCycleEndDate(start)` = `start + 6 days`. Always a 7-day aligned window.
- `enabledDate` (ISO date the bank was turned on) clamps the start. `effectiveCycleStart = max(enabledDate, rawCycleStart)`. This is the partial first cycle (see below). The cycle end stays 7-day aligned to the raw start.
- `daysInCycle = differenceInDays(cycleEnd, effectiveCycleStart) + 1`. Equals 7 for a full week, fewer for a partial first cycle.

#### Caps and safety bounds (computed once per cycle)

| Bound | Formula | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| Daily banking cap | `baseDailyTarget × (dailyCapPercent / 100)` | `dailyCapPercent` ∈ {15, 20, 25} |
| Spending cap | `baseDailyTarget × (spendingCapPercent / 100)` | `spendingCapPercent` ∈ {15, 20, 25} |
| Gender floor | 1200 if `goals.gender === 'female'`, else 1500 | engine L146 |
| Target floor | `max(baseDailyTarget × 0.70, genderFloor)` | adjusted target never drops below this |
| Target ceiling | `baseDailyTarget + spendingCap` | adjusted target never rises above this |

On a 2,000 base with a 20% cap: daily cap = 400, spending cap = 400, floor = max(1400, 1500) = 1500, ceiling = 2400. Per the daily docs the headline is "the highest target you'll ever see is 2,400" and "never below 1,500 men / 1,200 women."

#### Per-day settlement (`settleDay`)

Shared by the live engine (past days only) and the archival path so the two can never drift. `difference = baseDailyTarget − actual`.

**Lose or maintain goal:**

| Condition | Result |
|---|---|
| `difference > 0` (ate under) | `banked = min(difference, dailyCap)`; `capHit = difference > dailyCap` |
| `difference < 0` (ate over) | `spent = min(abs(difference), spendingCap)`; `spendCapHit = abs(difference) > spendingCap` |
| `difference === 0` | nothing banked or spent |

**Gain goal (axis flips):**

| Condition | Result |
|---|---|
| `difference > 0` (ate under target = behind on surplus) | `spent = min(difference, spendingCap)`; `spendCapHit = difference > spendingCap` |
| `difference < 0` (ate over target = building surplus) | `banked = min(abs(difference), dailyCap)`; `capHit = abs(difference) > dailyCap` |

So for gain, eating over target banks the extra surplus; eating under spends it. The same engine serves lose, maintain, and gain.

#### Pass 1: per-day actuals and banking

For each day `i` from 0 to `daysInCycle − 1`:

- `logged = summary exists AND (summary.entryCount > 0 OR summary.totalCalories > 0)`.
- **Future day or today:** `actual = isToday ? (summary.totalCalories || 0) : 0`. No banking, no spending. Today shows live logged intake but is never settled.
- **Past day, not logged:** `actual = baseDailyTarget`. Assumed "ate exactly target." No bank, no penalty. The bank never punishes a forgotten log and never hands out free banked calories for an empty day.
- **Past day, logged:** `actual = summary.totalCalories`.
- Banking/spending via `settleDay` runs **only for past completed days** (`!isFuture && !isToday`). This is the architecture non-negotiable: the engine never settles today.
- `weeklyActual` accumulates `actual` for all non-future days including today. `weeklyLoggedActual` accumulates only days the user actually logged (an unlogged day's assumed base does not fill the "Used" bar).

#### Bank balance

`bankBalance = totalBanked − totalSpent`, floored at 0 (engine L219-220). Displayed value.

#### Pass 2: redistribution into adjusted targets (the deliberate asymmetry)

This is the integrity core. The redistribution is intentionally **not symmetric**. Define over past completed days: `pastDaysExpected = pastDays.length × base`, `pastDaysActual = sum of actuals`, `rawOverspend = pastDaysActual − pastDaysExpected` (positive = overate). `remainingDays` = future days plus today.

| Goal | Direction | adjustmentPerDay |
|---|---|---|
| lose / maintain | Overate (`rawOverspend > 0`) | `−rawOverspend / remainingDays` (full overspend, **uncapped**) |
| lose / maintain | Underate (`rawOverspend ≤ 0`) | `+bankBalance / remainingDays` (**capped** bank only) |
| gain | Behind on surplus (`rawOverspend < 0`) | `−rawOverspend / remainingDays` (full shortfall, **uncapped**, pushes targets up) |
| gain | Ahead on surplus (`rawOverspend ≥ 0`) | `−bankBalance / remainingDays` (**capped** bank, eases off) |

Translation: it is easy to lose banked headroom (overeating cuts future days by the full amount) and hard to game (undereating only credits the capped bank). The math always leans toward the goal, never away from it. This is what stops the bank from becoming a license to overeat.

Each future/today day gets `adjustedTarget = round(clamp(base + adjustmentPerDay, floor, ceiling))`. Past days keep `adjustedTarget = base` for display.

#### Today's adjusted target and macros

`adjustedTodayTarget` = today's `adjustedTarget` (or base if no today row). Macros scale proportionally: `macroRatio = adjustedTodayTarget / base`, then `protein/carbs/fat = round(goalGrams × macroRatio)`. Percentages stay constant; grams move with the adjusted calorie target.

#### Remaining budget

`weeklyBudget = base × daysInCycle`. `remainingBudget = max(0, weeklyBudget − weeklyActual)`.

### Returned `CalorieBankCycle` shape

`cycleStartDate`, `cycleEndDate`, `baseDailyTarget`, `weeklyBudget`, `daysInCycle`, `perDayData[]` (each: date, baseTarget, adjustedTarget, actual, banked, spent, logged, isFuture, isToday, capHit, spendCapHit), `bankBalance`, `remainingBudget`, `remainingDays`, `weeklyActual`, `weeklyLoggedActual`, `adjustedTodayTarget`, `todayMacros {protein, carbs, fat}`, `goalType`.

### Config: `CalorieBankConfig` (dataStorage.ts L38-48)

| Field | Type | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `enabled` | boolean | Feature on/off |
| `cycleStartDay` | 0\|1\|2\|3\|4\|5\|6 | 0=Sun .. 6=Sat |
| `dailyCapPercent` | 15\|20\|25 | Max % of base bankable per day |
| `spendingCapPercent` | 15\|20\|25 | Max % of base spendable per day |
| `enabledDate` | ISO date string | When the feature was first turned on; clamps the first cycle |
| `pendingDailyCapPercent?` | 15\|20\|25 | Staged cap, promoted at next rollover |
| `pendingSpendingCapPercent?` | 15\|20\|25 | Staged cap, promoted at next rollover |

Defaults on a fresh enable: `cycleStartDay = 1` (Monday), `dailyCapPercent = 20`, `spendingCapPercent = 20`.

### Archival and resets (`calorieBankService.ts`)

#### `calculateCompletedCycle` (engine)

The archival twin of `calculateCurrentCycle`. Every day is treated as completed (none is "today"), so the final day of the cycle gets banked or spent instead of being left live. `lastDay = min(settleThrough, cycleEnd)`. `effectiveStart = max(enabledDate, cycleStart)`. Unlogged days still assume base. The live engine never settles today, which would otherwise drop the final day of every archived cycle, so this separate path exists to close the gap.

#### `checkAndResetCycle`

Called on app open, on AppState foreground, and at midnight crossing. If the bank is off or still inside the first cycle, no-op. Otherwise it **archives every cycle that completed since the bank was enabled**, not just the most recent, by stepping a cursor in 7-day increments from `enabledCycleStart` up to (but not including) the current cycle start. This catches cycles the app was closed through (gap cycles). Already-archived cycles (matched by `startDate`) are skipped. Each archived cycle is saved via `buildCompletedCycleRecord`.

#### Cap changes are pending and apply from the next cycle

`updateCalorieBankSettings` never rewrites a day that already settled. If the current cycle already has completed days (`effectiveStart < today`), a cap change is staged into `pendingDailyCapPercent` / `pendingSpendingCapPercent`. Otherwise (just enabled, or today is the start day) it applies immediately. On the next rollover, `checkAndResetCycle` promotes the pending caps to active **after** archiving the completed cycles with their old (correct) cap. The Settings UI sets both `dailyCapPercent` and `spendingCapPercent` to the same value in a single tap (one cap controls both bank and spend).

#### Start-day change archives the in-progress week

`archiveInProgressCycle` settles the current cycle through yesterday (`settleThrough = today − 1`; today is live and not settled) and saves it before the cycle is restructured. Then `updateCalorieBankSettings` with a new `cycleStartDay` resets `enabledDate` to today, starting a fresh cycle from today, and any pending cap is promoted immediately (no past days in the new cycle to rewrite). In Settings, changing the start day is confirmed via an Alert: "This starts a new week today. The days so far this week are saved to your history."

#### `handlePlanChange`

When the user changes their calorie goals, the bank resets by setting `enabledDate = today`. The engine treats this as a new partial cycle, so the remaining days use the new daily target. A new plan means a fresh start. (Dynamic Adjustments suggestions, by contrast, wait until the next reset; they do not call this.)

#### Enable / disable

`enableCalorieBank` preserves an existing config's saved start day and caps (only a brand-new config falls back to defaults), but always sets `enabledDate = today` since the bank was off until now. `disableCalorieBank` sets `enabled = false` but preserves config, so re-enabling later picks up the saved settings.

#### Persistence and sync (dataStorage.ts)

- `saveCalorieBankConfig` / `loadCalorieBankConfig`: AsyncStorage first, then fire-and-forget Supabase upsert.
- `saveCompletedCycle`: appends, then `slice(-52)` (keeps the last 52 cycles, roughly a year), then background upsert.
- `loadCompletedCycles`.
- `isCycleResetSeen(date)` / `setCycleResetSeen(date)`: tracks whether the user dismissed the reset card for a given cycle start.
- On background pull, the calorie bank config is **seed-only**: it is written from the remote copy only when there is no local config at all (fresh device or evicted cache). Never overwrites an existing local config, since the user toggles it by hand and it has no `updatedAt`.

### `CalorieBankCompletedCycle` (the archive record)

Built by `buildCompletedCycleRecord`:

| Field | Computation |
|---|---|
| `startDate`, `endDate` | from the cycle |
| `weeklyBudget`, `weeklyActual` | from the cycle |
| `bankUtilization` | `min(100, round(totalSpent / totalBanked × 100))`, 0 if nothing banked |
| `expiredCalories` | `max(0, totalBanked − totalSpent)` (banked but unspent; do not roll over) |
| `daysLogged` | count of `logged && !isFuture` days |
| `daysInCycle` | 7 or fewer for partial first cycle |
| `peakBankBalance` | round of the running max balance across the cycle (floored at 0 along the way) |
| `capHitDays` | count of days where the banking cap was reached |
| `spendCapHitDays` | count of days where the spending cap was reached |
| `goalType` | lose / gain / maintain |

### The cards and surfaces

#### Home calorie card, BANK ON mode (`Macros2Card.tsx`)

This was simplified in v1.2.9. When `calorieBankActive` is true the card shows a small green **BANK ON** badge (`#22C55E`, fontSize 10, weight 600) next to the title. The three columns are unchanged: **Food** (calories eaten), **Exercise**, **Remaining**. The bank's effect is baked into Remaining, which is measured against the adjusted today target (`bankAdjustedCalories`), not the base. There is no separate live "Banked/Surplus" column on this card anymore. Rationale in the code: the today card stays about today and never shows a live "banked" projection that is just a relabel of Remaining until you overeat. Remaining color: `#EF4444` if ≤ 0, `#F59E0B` if under 20% of the daily target, else `#10B981`.

Note: the PRD and `calorie-bank-feature.md` still describe an older 4-column Food / Banked / Surplus / Remaining layout. The shipped card per `Macros2Card.tsx` is Food / Exercise / Remaining + badge. Trust the code.

#### Weekly bank card (`CalorieBankWeeklyCard.tsx`)

Reached by swiping the home stat cards. When the bank is active the card order becomes `['macros2', 'weekly', 'macros']` (vs `['macros2', 'macros']` when off); if the bank turns off while Weekly is showing, it falls back to `macros2` so the area never renders blank. The Weekly card shows:

- Header: calendar icon, "Weekly", and "Day {dayOfCycle} of {daysInCycle}" where `dayOfCycle = daysInCycle − remainingDays + 1`.
- Progress bar: `progressPct = min(100, weeklyActual / weeklyBudget × 100)`, green `#22C55E`.
- Three columns:

| Column | Value | Color |
|---|---|---|
| Used | `round(weeklyActual)` (passed as `weeklyLoggedActual` from Home) | textPrimary |
| In Bank | `round(bankBalance)` | `#22C55E` if > 0 else textTertiary |
| Left | `max(0, weeklyBudget − weeklyActual)` | `#EF4444` if over budget, else `#10B981` |

Values animate via `NumberTicker` (800ms). The Home screen passes `weeklyActual = weeklyLoggedActual` so the bar reflects logged days only.

#### `CalorieBankCard.tsx` (richer card, exists in the codebase)

A fuller card variant: header with "Day X of Y", a weekly progress bar (red `#EF4444` if over 100%, else primary), a 3-stat row (Banked/Surplus, Today = `adjustedTodayTarget`, Remaining), and a 7-bar mini-week. Bar colors per day: `#22C55E` on/under adjusted target, `#F59E0B` over but within spending cap, `#EF4444` over spending cap (`spendCapHit`). The "Banked" label flips to "Surplus" for a gain goal. This component is imported in HomeScreen.

#### Use-it-before-you-lose-it nudge (HomeScreen L2700-2715)

Banked calories expire at reset, so when the bank is full and the week is nearly over the app points it out. Shown only when: `calorieBankActive`, selected date is today, `bankBalance ≥ 200`, and `remainingDays` is 1 or 2. Green gift-icon banner. Copy: "You have {bankBalance} kcal banked and {today is the last day | N days left}. Enjoy a bigger meal before your week resets."

#### Cycle reset / recap card (`CycleResetCard.tsx`)

Shown once at the start of a new cycle (gated by `isCycleResetSeen` / `setCycleResetSeen`, dismiss persists per cycle start date). Titled "Weekly Summary." Shows:

- Main: "You used {weeklyActual} of {weeklyBudget} kcal."
- If `expiredCalories > 0`: "{expiredCalories} kcal went unused."
- If over budget: "{overUnder} kcal over budget" in red.
- Three details: Bank used (`bankUtilization%`), Days logged (`daysLogged/daysInCycle`), Budget used (`round(weeklyActual/weeklyBudget×100)%`).
- A forward-looking coach line keyed off the week:
  - Over budget: "You ran over budget. Plan your heavier days earlier so the bank can absorb them."
  - Else if `bankUtilization < 30 && expiredCalories > 200`: "You banked plenty but barely spent it. Use that room next week, the flexibility is the point."
  - Else if `daysLogged < daysInCycle`: "A few days went unlogged. Logging every day makes the bank work for you."
  - Else: "Balanced week. Keep the rhythm going."
- Footer: "Your new cycle starts today."

#### Nutrition Analysis insights (`NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx`)

When `calorieBankData.enabled`, a Calorie Bank insight section shows: weekly budget progress bar (`weeklyActual / weeklyBudget`, red if over, else green), Banked (`+bankBalance`), Utilization (`bankUtilization%`), and `capHitDays`. Below it a **Bank Distribution** day-by-day chart: green bars for days under target (banked), amber for days over (spent), bar scaled against `dailyCapPercent/100 × base`. The weekly AI insight aligns to the cycle start day (e.g., Wednesday to Tuesday) rather than always resetting Monday.

### Settings (SettingsScreen.tsx, slide-up `calorieBank`)

Premium gated. When `plan === 'premium' && isSignedIn` the row is tappable with subtitle "On · Resets every {day}" or "Flexible weekly calorie budgeting." For free or signed-out users the row renders at `opacity: 0.5` with a `shield-lock-outline` icon and no chevron; the bank UI and math do not run. The slide-up header carries a gold crown badge.

Controls (visible only when enabled):

- **Toggle** (Enabled/Disabled). Optimistic update so the switch does not bounce; on enable it calls `enableCalorieBank()` (preserves saved settings, defaults Monday/20/20).
- **Cycle Start Day**: chips in order `[1,2,3,4,5,6,0]` (Mon-first). Changing it confirms via Alert, archives the in-progress week, then restructures from today. Helper: "Your weekly budget resets every {day}. Any unused banked calories expire at reset."
- **Daily Banking Cap**: 15 / 20 / 25 chips, each showing `~{round(base × pct/100)} kcal`. Sets both daily and spending caps to the same value. The selected chip reflects the **pending** cap if one was just chosen. If pending differs from active: "New cap applies from your next cycle ({day}). This week keeps its current cap." Helper: "The maximum you can bank or spend beyond your daily target in a single day. This prevents extreme restriction or overeating."
- **How it works** explainer plus Banked/Surplus definition cards and a tabbed Example (Lose / Maintain / Gain). The Lose example: 2,000 target, 14,000 budget, Monday 1,650 → 350 banked → remaining 6 days each +~58, Saturday dinner 2,350 → 350 surplus covered, weekly total 13,900, under budget.

### Premium gating (load-bearing)

`calorieBankActive = !!(isPremium && calorieBankConfig?.enabled && calorieBankCycle)`. `bankAdjustedCalories` and `bankAdjustedMacros` only resolve to bank values when `isPremium && calorieBankCycle && calorieBankConfig?.enabled`; otherwise they fall back to the plain goal. `isPremium` requires a `premium` plan AND a signed-in account with email, with `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` granting premium to every signed-in user during launch. The cycle effect re-gates on `isPremium` (HomeScreen L729), so the bank card stays hidden for non-premium and recomputes once the flag flips. Goals must exist; with no goals there is no base target and the bank cannot run.

### Edge cases and invariants (for anyone extending this)

- **Today is never settled.** Live for display, never banked or spent. The only path that settles a final day is `calculateCompletedCycle` at archive time.
- **Unlogged past day = assumed base.** No bank, no penalty. Same in live and archival engines.
- **Bank balance floored at 0.** Spending more than banked cannot make the displayed balance negative; the redistribution penalty (full uncapped overspend) is what actually punishes overeating.
- **Asymmetry is intentional.** Overeating reduces future by the full overspend; undereating raises future only by the capped bank.
- **Expiry is by design.** No multi-week rollover. Unspent banked calories expire at reset and are recorded as `expiredCalories`.
- **Pure engine, derived state.** No stored running totals. Editing a past meal recomputes everything.
- **Gap cycles.** App closed for weeks → every completed cycle in the gap is archived on next open, not just the latest.

---

Section completeness notes (per CLAUDE.md): I documented shipped behavior only and flagged the one place the prose docs (PRD, calorie-bank-feature.md) lag the code: they still describe a 4-column Food/Banked/Surplus/Remaining home card, but `Macros2Card.tsx` (v1.2.9) ships Food/Exercise/Remaining plus a BANK ON badge. Two distinct card components exist (`CalorieBankCard.tsx` is the richer 7-bar variant; `CalorieBankWeeklyCard.tsx` is the swipe-to-weekly card). I did not visually test any UI. Relevant files: `src/utils/calorieBankEngine.ts`, `src/services/calorieBankService.ts`, `src/services/dataStorage.ts` (L38-64, L3742-3797), `src/components/{Macros2Card,CalorieBankCard,CalorieBankWeeklyCard,CycleResetCard,SwipeableCards,StatCardsSection}.tsx`, `src/screens/SettingsScreen.tsx` (L1067-1300), `src/screens/HomeScreen.tsx` (L240-246, L2685-2715, L2871-2883), `src/screens/NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx` (L1835-1935), `docs/product/PRD-calorie-bank.md`, `docs/calorie-bank-feature.md`.

---

## 8. Nutrition Analysis Screen: Every Tab, Chart and Insight

---

The Nutrition Analysis Screen (`src/screens/NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx`, 2754 lines) is a full-screen modal opened from HomeScreen. It dismisses via a downward chevron, a swipe-down gesture (`PanResponder`, triggers `handleClose` when `dy > 100` or `vy > 0.5`), or by tapping the backdrop. Header right has an info button opening an "About Nutrition Analysis" page-sheet modal.

### Props and data sources

| Prop | Type | Role |
|---|---|---|
| `mealsByDate` | `Record<string, Meal[]>` | Raw meals keyed by `yyyy-MM-dd`. Source for meal-timing, top-foods, sugar-load (uses `meal.timestamp`, `meal.foods[].calories/sugar/added_sugars`). |
| `summariesByDate` | `Record<string, DailySummary>` | Preferred source for the per-day calorie/macro totals. Also the input to `MicronutrientCard`. |
| `targetCalories/Protein/Carbs/Fat` | `number` | Goal targets. Each is treated as "set" only if `> 0`, else `undefined`. |
| `isPremium` | `boolean` | Gates the entire Insights tab. |
| `calorieBankData` | object or `null` | Drives the two calorie-bank cards and shifts the AI insight week boundary. |
| `insightUnlocks` | `InsightUnlocks` | Per-insight unlock records; checked by `isInsightUnlocked`. |
| `initialTab` | `'Calories' \| 'Macros' \| 'Insights'` | Initial tab. |
| `scrollToInsight` | `InsightId \| null` | Auto-jumps to a specific insight card (the `scrollToInsight` mechanism noted in CLAUDE.md). |

`nutritionData` is built (memoized) by preferring `summariesByDate` (mapping `totalCalories/Protein/Fat/Carbs`); only if that map is empty does it fall back to aggregating `mealsByDate` by summing each food's macros. Sorted oldest-first.

### Tabs

Three tabs render in a segmented control. The Calories and Macros tabs always show. The **Insights** tab (labeled `✨ Insights`) renders only when `isPremium === true`. The tab bar itself only appears once `hasLoggedMeals` is true.

| Tab | Premium | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| Calories | Free | Calorie line chart, week-over-week, history table. |
| Macros | Free | Protein/carbs/fat line chart, macro insight box, history table. |
| Insights | Premium only | All unlock-gated insight cards + AI Weekly Insight. |

### Time ranges

`type TimeRange = '1D' | '1W' | '1M' | '3M' | '6M' | '1Y' | '2Y'`. The pill selector (`renderTimeRangePills`, rendered on all three tabs) exposes only six: `['1D','1W','1M','3M','6M','1Y']` (`2Y` exists in the type and in `MicronutrientCard`'s `RANGE_DAYS` but is not user-selectable here). Default range is `1W`.

Range start (from `startOfDay(new Date())`, in `getFilteredData`):

| Range | rangeStart | X-axis label format (`formatXLabel`) |
|---|---|---|
| 1D | `subDays(now, 1)` | `ha` (e.g. "9AM") |
| 1W | `subDays(now, 6)` | `EEE` (e.g. "Mon") |
| 1M | `subMonths(now, 1)` | `d MMM` |
| 3M | `subMonths(now, 3)` | `d MMM` |
| 6M | `subMonths(now, 6)` | `d MMM` |
| 1Y | `subYears(now, 1)` | `MMM yyyy` |
| 2Y | `subYears(now, 2)` | `MMM yyyy` |

`getFilteredData` zero-fills **every** calendar day from `rangeStart` to today so the chart x-axis scales correctly. Days with no log become `{calories:0, protein:0, fat:0, carbs:0}`. X-axis shows at most 5 evenly spaced labels (`getXAxisLabelIndices`, `maxLabels=5`).

### Averages and `daysWithData`

This is the load-bearing distinction. `graphData` (zero-filled) is used for the chart shape. `daysWithData` filters `graphData` to days where `calories>0 || protein>0 || carbs>0 || fat>0`. **All averages divide by `daysWithData.length`, not by the number of calendar days in the range.** So a week with 3 logged days averages over 3, not 7.

- `averageCalories = Math.round(sum(calories over daysWithData) / daysWithData.length)`, or `null` if no logged days.
- `averageProtein/Carbs/Fat` = same pattern, returned unrounded (`null` if empty).
- `hasLoggedMeals = daysWithData.length > 0`.

### Empty / insufficient / set-goals states

| Condition | Render |
|---|---|
| `!hasLoggedMeals` | "Log your first meal" empty-state card with a "Log Meal" button (`onRequestLogMeal`). Tab bar and charts are hidden. |
| Hero with no average | Shows `--`. |
| `targetCalories` undefined (≤0 or absent) | TARGET hero shows a "Set Goal" link → `handleSetGoalPress` (`onRequestSetGoals`, else `onBack`). |
| Macros tab, no macro targets | Info box: "Set macro goals to get personalized insights on your nutrition." + "Set Goals" link. |
| Insight unlocked but no goals set | `NeedsGoalsCard`: "Set your goals to use this insight" (used by Goal Adherence and Nutrition Balance). |
| Insight locked | `LockedInsightCard`: dim card (opacity 0.5), lock icon, name, and `requirementText`. |

### Hero summary cards (top of every tab)

**Calories tab** renders up to three hero cards:

1. **AVERAGE** — `averageCalories` Kcal (or `--`).
2. **TARGET** — `targetCalories` Kcal, or a "Set Goal" link.
3. **Deficit/Surplus** — only when both target and average exist. `diff = averageCalories - targetCalories`. Logic:

| Condition | Label | Value | Color |
|---|---|---|---|
| `Math.abs(diff) <= 50` | `ON TRACK` | `0` | `#10B981` green |
| `diff < 0` | `DEFICIT` | `${diff}` (negative) | `#3B82F6` blue |
| else | `SURPLUS` | `+${diff}` | `#EF4444` red |

**Macros tab** renders three hero cards: PROTEIN (`#3B82F6`), CARBS (`#F59E0B`), FAT (`#8B5CF6`), each showing `value.toFixed(0)` g or `--`.

### Macro colors (used everywhere)

Protein `#3B82F6`, Carbs `#F59E0B`, Fat `#8B5CF6`. Calories line uses `theme.colors.primary`. Target lines: calories `#EF4444` (dashed `4,4`, opacity 0.5), protein `#3B82F6` (dashed). Banked green `#22C55E`, spent amber `#F59E0B`.

---

## Calories tab

**Calorie line chart.** Smooth bezier (Catmull-Rom control points, `cp = ±dx/6`), `graphHeight=280`, animated draw over 1800ms plus a 350ms fade-in. Y-axis: 6 grid lines, scaled to `Math.ceil((maxCalories + caloriesPadding)/100)*100` down to `Math.max(0, floor((minCalories - caloriesPadding)/100)*100)` where `caloriesPadding = (max-min)*0.1`. Red dashed target line if target set. Hollow data dots are drawn only when `caloriesData.length < 20`. Scrubbing: drag finger across the chart; nearest point snaps and a tooltip shows `MMM d` + `{calories} Kcal` with a vertical guide line and filled dot.

**Week-over-week comparison.** `weekOverWeek` compares last 7 days vs the prior 7 days (days 7–14 ago), averaging over whatever entries exist in each window. `pctChange = round((curr-prev)/prev*100)`, `0` if prev is 0. Shown as a chip; for calories, `>0` is red (`#EF4444`, eating more), `<0` is green (`#10B981`), `0` is neutral. Returns `null` if either window has zero entries.

**History table.** Newest-first list of every day in range: `d MMM yyyy` + `{calories} Kcal`, with an edit (`edit-2`) icon → `onRequestLogMealForDate(date)`.

---

## Macros tab

**Macro line chart.** Three overlaid bezier lines (protein/carbs/fat). Shared Y-axis max `maxValue = Math.ceil(Math.max(maxProtein, maxCarbs, maxFat, 50)/25)*25` (round up to nearest 25, floor 50), where each `maxX = Math.max(...graphData values, targetX ?? 0)`. Only the protein target line is drawn (carbs/fat target lines are intentionally omitted, per inline comment). Same 1800ms/350ms animation. Scrubbing tooltip shows P/C/F in grams, with three colored dots on the lines.

**Week-over-week macro chips.** P/C/F each: `>0` shown in the macro color, `<0` green (`#10B981`), `0` neutral.

**Dynamic macro insight box.** Per macro with a target and average, `pct = ((avg - target)/target)*100`. Status: `low` if `pct < -15`, `high` if `pct > 15`, else `on_track`. If all on-track: green check, "All macros are within target range...". Otherwise it picks the most off-track macro (largest `|pct|`) and emits a macro-specific copy string (e.g. protein low: "Protein is {deficit}% below target. Try adding eggs, Greek yogurt, or chicken...").

**Macros history table.** Newest-first: Date | Protein | Carbs | Fat (g each) + edit icon.

---

## Insights tab (premium)

If `!isPremium`, the whole tab body is a lock placeholder: "Premium Feature — Unlock advanced analytics, AI-powered insights, and weekly trend reports." Otherwise every card is wrapped in an `InsightSlot` (registers its scroll Y for `scrollToInsight`) and gated by `isInsightUnlocked(id, insightUnlocks)`. A locked card renders `LockedInsightCard`; an unlocked card with missing goals renders `NeedsGoalsCard`.

### Unlock thresholds (`src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts`)

The unlock `check` runs against `InsightStats` (computed elsewhere, e.g. HomeScreen). `loggedDays` = days with ≥1 food entry. Insight cards on this screen:

| Insight | id | `requirementText` | Unlock condition | Premium |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Goal Adherence | `goal-adherence` | Log 2 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 2` | Premium |
| Macro Split | `macro-split` | Log 2 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 2` | Premium |
| Calorie Trend | `calorie-trend` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` | Premium |
| Meal Timing | `meal-timing` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` | Premium |
| Sugar Load | `sugar-load` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` | Premium |
| Calorie Bank | `calorie-bank` | Log 3 days with the calorie bank on | `loggedDays >= 3 && calorieBankEnabled` | Premium |
| Top Foods | `top-foods` | Log 4 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 4` | Premium |
| Weekly Pattern | `weekly-pattern` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` | Premium |
| Nutrition Balance | `nutrition-balance` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` | Premium |
| Micronutrients | `micronutrient-balance` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` | Premium |
| AI Weekly Insight | `ai-weekly-insight` | Log 7 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 7` | Premium |

Note: `isInsightUnlocked` simply checks whether a record exists in `insightUnlocks` (the unlock event is recorded persistently once the `check` first passes), so cards stay unlocked even if `loggedDays` later drops. The Calorie Bank slot additionally renders only when `calorieBankData?.enabled`.

The Insights tab renders cards in this visual order: time-range pills → AI Weekly Insight → Calorie Bank (×2 cards) → Goal Adherence → Calorie Trend → Macro Split → Micronutrients → Nutrition Balance → Weekly Pattern → Meal Timing → Top Foods → Sugar Load.

### Card-by-card detail

**AI Weekly Insight** (`ai-weekly-insight`). Collapsible card. Calls `generateWeeklyInsights` (`openaiService.ts`, `gpt-4o-mini`, `temperature 0.4`, `max_tokens 600`, free-text — no JSON schema). The prompt writes exactly 3 short paragraphs, each forced to lead with the user's actual numbers (calories, grams, food names, days), explain the consequence, and end with one specific action; it covers calorie accuracy, macro imbalance, day patterns, food variety, meal timing, logging gaps, and bank usage when present.

The payload (`weeklySummary`) is sanitized via `sanitizeObjectForAI` and includes: `averageCalories/Protein/Carbs/Fat`, `targets` (calories + macro grams), `totalDaysLogged` (= `graphData.length`), a 7-day `dailyBreakdown` (`EEE` day, cal/protein/carbs/fat), `dayOfWeekAvg` (computed over the last 14 days bucketed by weekday), `mealTimingDistribution` (counts of meals in morning 4–12, afternoon 12–17, evening otherwise, over the last 7 days), `topFoods` (top 5 by frequency over last 7 days, formatted `name (Nx)`), and `calorieBank` when bank data exists.

Caching: keyed by `INSIGHT_CACHE_KEY = '@trackkal:weeklyInsightCache'`, week key = `startOfWeek(now, { weekStartsOn })` formatted `yyyy-MM-dd`. `weekStartsOn` = the bank's `cycleStartDayNum` when the bank is enabled, otherwise `1` (Monday). On a cache hit for the current week key the cached text is shown (no "NEW" badge). On miss it generates, shows the **NEW** badge, and caches `{weekKey, text, generatedAt}`. A `insightRequestInFlight` ref prevents duplicate calls. The header reads "Refreshes every {Monday or the bank's cycleStartDay}". Failures fall back to: "We need a bit more data to generate your weekly insight. Keep logging!"

**Calorie Bank** (`calorie-bank`) — two cards, only if `calorieBankData.enabled`.

- *Bank Utilization card.* Header chip "ACTIVE". Weekly budget progress bar = `min(100, weeklyActual/weeklyBudget*100)`%, colored red `#EF4444` if `weeklyActual > weeklyBudget` else green `#22C55E`. Three stat tiles: **Banked** `+round(bankBalance)` (green), **Utilization** `bankUtilization%`, **Cap days** `capHitDays`. Values are pass-through from `calorieBankData` (computed by the bank engine, never for today).
- *Bank Distribution card.* One horizontal bar per day in `perDayBreakdown`. `maxBar = dailyCapPercent/100 * day.base`; `bankedPct = min(1, day.banked/maxBar)`, `spentPct = min(1, day.spent/maxBar)`. Banked segment green `#22C55E`, spent segment amber `#F59E0B`. Future days (`actual===0 && !isToday`) render "—". Day label shows banked `+N`, spent `-N`, or `0`. Today is bolded. Legend: Banked / Spent.

**Goal Adherence** (`goal-adherence`). Ring per macro that has a target (Protein, Carbs, Fat, and Calories if `targetCalories` set). Each ring: `pct = min(1, avg/target)`, SVG circle radius 32, `circumference = 2π·32`, `strokeDashoffset = circumference*(1-pct)`, rotated −90°. Center shows `round(pct*100)%`; subtitle shows `round(avg)/target` (with "g" suffix except Calories). Requires at least one macro target, else `NeedsGoalsCard`. Subtitle "Average vs. target".

**Calorie Trend** (`calorie-trend`). Renders only when also `graphData.length >= 2`. Mini area+line chart, height 140. `maxV = max(...calories, targetCalories ?? 0, 100)`, `minV = 0`. Gradient area fill (primary, 0.2→0 opacity). Dashed avg line labeled "avg" at `averageCalories`. Red dashed target line labeled "target" if target set. Data dots drawn only when ≤14 points. Header right shows `averageCalories` "avg Kcal/day".

**Macro Split** (`macro-split`). Stacked bar split by **calorie** contribution: `pCal = protein*4`, `cCal = carbs*4`, `fCal = fat*9`, each segment width = its share of `totalCal`. Three labels show the calorie-percent (`round(pct)%`) and `round(grams)g/day`. (Note: gram percentages are computed but the displayed % is the calorie-based one.) Subtitle "Average daily ratio".

**Micronutrients** (`micronutrient-balance`). Renders `MicronutrientCard` (`src/components/MicronutrientCard.tsx`) only if `summariesByDate` exists, passing the current `timeRange`. See dedicated subsection below.

**Nutrition Balance** (`nutrition-balance`). Radar chart (`renderRadarChart`). Requires all three macro targets (else `radarData` empty → `NeedsGoalsCard`). 4 axes — Protein, Carbs, Fat, Calories. Each value = `min(1.2, avg/target)` (calories: `min(1.2, averageCalories/targetCalories)`, else 0). Drawn radius clamps to `min(value, 1.1)*65`. Background webs at scales 0.25/0.5/0.75/1; data polygon fill `rgba(59,130,246,0.2)`, stroke `theme.colors.primary`. Subtitle "Target vs. actual performance".

**Weekly Pattern** (`weekly-pattern`). Renders when also `graphData.length >= 3`. Bar chart of average calories per weekday (Mon→Sun ordering). Each weekday bucket sums `graphData` calories and divides by its count (`0` if none). Bars scale to the max day average; today's bar is solid primary, others `primary40`. Value label drawn above non-zero bars. Subtitle "Average calories by day of week".

**Meal Timing** (`meal-timing`). Uses raw `mealsByDate` filtered to the current range (`rangeDays` = 1/7/30/90/180/365 by range; `1Y`+ map to 365). Buckets by hour: Morning 4–12, Afternoon 12–17, Evening otherwise (5PM–4AM). For each: `pct = bucket.cals / totalRangeCals`, and `avgCals = round(bucket.cals / daysWithData)`. Shown as three rows with icon (sunrise/sun/moon), time label, `(pct*100)%`, and `~{avgCals} Kcal` plus a progress bar. Subtitle "When are you eating?"

**Top Foods** (`top-foods`). From `mealsByDate` within range, counts food occurrences by lowercased trimmed name and sums their calories. Top 5 by count. Each row: rank, name (capitalized), `{count}x · {round(cals/count)} Kcal avg`, and a bar = `count/maxCount`. Empty state: "Log more meals to see your top foods." Subtitle "Most logged items".

**Sugar Load** (`sugar-load`). From `mealsByDate` within range, sums `f.sugar` (total) and `f.added_sugars`. `avgTotal = round(totalSugar/days)`, `avgAdded = round(addedSugar/days)`, `avgNatural = max(0, avgTotal - avgAdded)`. Three stats: Added (`#FB7185`), Natural (`#4ADE80`), Total. Stacked bar with `maxBar = max(avgTotal, dailyLimit*1.2)` and a vertical marker at the `dailyLimit = 50g` line ("Limit 50g"). Subtitle "Natural vs. added sugars (daily avg)".

---

### MicronutrientCard detail (`MicronutrientCard.tsx`)

Loads goals via `dataStorage.loadGoals()` then `getMicroTargets({ age, sex: gender, proteinGramsOverride: proteinGrams })`. Tracks 15 nutrients in this fixed order, each mapped to a `DailySummary` field:

| Nutrient | key | summaryKey | Kind |
|---|---|---|---|
| Sodium | `sodium_mg` | `totalSodium` | limit |
| Added sugar | `added_sugars` | `totalAddedSugars` | limit |
| Saturated fat | `saturated_fat` | `totalSaturatedFat` | limit |
| Cholesterol | `cholesterol_mg` | `totalCholesterol` | limit |
| Calcium | `calcium_mg` | `totalCalcium` | target |
| Iron | `iron_mg` | `totalIron` | target |
| Magnesium | `magnesium_mg` | `totalMagnesium` | target |
| Zinc | `zinc_mg` | `totalZinc` | target |
| Potassium | `potassium_mg` | `totalPotassium` | target |
| Fiber | `dietary_fiber` | `totalFiber` | target |
| Omega-3 | `omega_3_g` | `totalOmega3` | target |
| Vitamin A | `vitamin_a_mcg` | `totalVitaminA` | target |
| Vitamin C | `vitamin_c_mg` | `totalVitaminC` | target |
| Vitamin D | `vitamin_d_mcg` | `totalVitaminD` | target |
| Vitamin B12 | `vitamin_b12_mcg` | `totalVitaminB12` | target |

**Range math.** `RANGE_DAYS = {1D:1, 1W:7, 1M:30, 3M:90, 6M:180, 1Y:365, 2Y:730}`. For `1D` it uses today's summary only (counted if `entryCount > 0`). For longer ranges it builds the last `rangeDays` calendar dates, filters to those with `entryCount > 0` (`daysWithData`), sums each nutrient over those, and divides by `max(1, daysWithData.length)` — i.e. a **daily average over logged days**. `loggedDaysInRange` drives the subtitle: "Today's intake vs your targets" (1D), "No food logged in the {range} yet" (0 logged), "Daily average across your N logged days in the {range}" (sparse), or "Daily average across the {range}".

**Status + colors** (`microTargets.ts` `statusFor`, `percentOfTarget` clamped 0–999):

- Target nutrients: `<50%` **deficient** (`#EF4444`), `50–80%` **low** (`#F59E0B`), `80–120%` **on_track** (`#10B981`), `120–200%` **over** (`#F59E0B`), `>200%` **way_over** (`#EF4444`).
- Limit nutrients: `<80%` **on_track** (green), `80–120%` **over** (amber), `≥120%` **way_over** (red). Over-limit rows append "% of limit".

Bar fill width is `min(100, pct)`. Each row shows `actual / target {unit}` and the percent. Footer disclaimer: "Estimates from your food log. For medical concerns, talk to a doctor."

**Personalized targets** (`getMicroTargets`, defaults age 30 / male if unknown; `prefer_not_to_say` → male):

| Nutrient | Value | Source/notes |
|---|---|---|
| Fiber | M ≤50: 38g, M 51+: 30g; F ≤50: 25g, F 51+: 21g | IOM |
| Added sugars | 50g (limit) | FDA Daily Value |
| Saturated fat | 20g (limit) | FDA DV |
| Sodium | 2300mg (limit) | FDA upper |
| Potassium | M 3400mg / F 2600mg | |
| Calcium | 1000mg base; 1300 if ≤18; 1200 for women 51+, men 71+ | |
| Iron | 18mg women 19–50, else 8mg | |
| Magnesium | M ≤30: 400, M 31+: 420; F ≤30: 310, F 31+: 320; teen M 410 / F 360 | |
| Zinc | M 11mg / F 8mg | |
| Cholesterol | 300mg (limit) | historic FDA |
| Omega-3 | M 1.6g / F 1.1g | AI/AMDR |
| Vitamin A | M 900 / F 700 mcg | |
| Vitamin C | M 90 / F 75 mg | |
| Vitamin D | 20mcg if ≥71, else 15mcg | |
| Vitamin B12 | 2.4mcg | |
| Protein (mirrored) | `proteinGramsOverride` if >0, else `round(70*0.8)=56g` | |

### Note on `insightService.ts`

`insightService.ts` is a separate deterministic rule engine (`generateInsights`) that produces the `Insight[]` warnings/patterns surfaced elsewhere (e.g. Home), not the cards on this screen. For completeness its 5 rules: low protein (`totalProtein < goal*0.85` on ≥5 of 7 days, confidence 0.9), weekend calorie spikes (`isWeekend && totalCalories > goal*1.15` on ≥2 days, 0.85), low fiber if `weakNutrients` includes fiber (0.8), weight plateau (`consistencyScore>80`, `periodDays>=7`, `|change|<0.3kg`, goal=lose, 0.85), and high consistency achievement (`consistencyScore>90`, 0.95). It dedupes against titles from the last 7 days, prioritizes warning(5) > pattern(3) > suggestion(2) > achievement(1), and returns max 2 per run. `getActionForInsight` maps each title to a one-tap action suggestion.

## 9. The Progressive Insight Unlock System

---

The progressive insight unlock system is the app's core engagement loop for the two analysis screens. Every chart starts locked behind a data threshold. As the user logs food and weight, thresholds are crossed, insights unlock, and the Home screen announces each new unlock with a tappable card that deep links straight to the chart. The whole system is premium gated: only premium users compute and persist new unlocks.

The engine itself lives in [src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts](src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts) as pure functions with no side effects and no storage calls. Stats in, unlocked IDs out. Persistence, premium gating, and announcement state live in `HomeScreen.tsx` and `dataStorage.ts`.

### Where each piece lives

| Concern | Location |
| --- | --- |
| Insight definitions, thresholds, pure check functions | `src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts` |
| Unlock detection + announcement orchestration | `checkInsightUnlocks` in `src/screens/HomeScreen.tsx` (lines 738-822) |
| Announcement card UI | `src/components/InsightUnlockCard.tsx` |
| Locked placeholder + unlocked content rendering, scroll landing | `InsightSlot` / `LockedInsightCard` in `NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx` and `WeightTrackerScreen.tsx` |
| Local persistence (AsyncStorage) + background Supabase sync | `loadInsightUnlocks` / `saveInsightUnlocks` / `markInsightSeen` in `src/services/dataStorage.ts` (lines 3712-3738) |
| Storage key | `@trackkal:insightUnlocks` (`STORAGE_KEYS.INSIGHT_UNLOCKS`) |

### Premium gating

Insight unlocks are premium. In `checkInsightUnlocks`, existing unlocks are always loaded into state so the render-time gate handles visibility, but new unlocks are only computed and saved when `plan === 'premium' && !!account?.email` (HomeScreen line 749). Non premium users still get the announcement for any already unseen unlock, but no new unlocks are minted for them. The announcement card on Home is additionally render gated behind `pendingUnlockAnnouncement && isPremium` (HomeScreen line 2745).

### The full insight catalog

There are 21 insights total, split 11 nutrition / 10 weight. (Note: the `InsightId` union and `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` array are the single source of truth; `micronutrient-balance` and `sugar-load` are both nutrition, giving 11 nutrition entries.) Each insight has an `id`, `name`, `description` (the announcement one liner), `screen`, a Feather `icon`, a `requirementText` (shown on the locked placeholder), and a `check(stats)` predicate. The table below is verbatim from `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS`.

#### Nutrition Analysis insights (`screen: 'nutrition'`)

| id | Name | Icon | Requirement text (locked copy) | Exact unlock check |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `goal-adherence` | Goal Adherence | `target` | Log 2 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 2` |
| `macro-split` | Macro Split | `pie-chart` | Log 2 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 2` |
| `calorie-trend` | Calorie Trend | `trending-up` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` |
| `meal-timing` | Meal Timing | `clock` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` |
| `top-foods` | Top Foods | `award` | Log 4 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 4` |
| `weekly-pattern` | Weekly Pattern | `bar-chart-2` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` |
| `nutrition-balance` | Nutrition Balance | `compass` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` |
| `micronutrient-balance` | Micronutrients | `zap` | Log 5 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 5` |
| `sugar-load` | Sugar Load | `droplet` | Log 3 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 3` |
| `calorie-bank` | Calorie Bank | `credit-card` | Log 3 days with the calorie bank on | `loggedDays >= 3 && !!calorieBankEnabled` |
| `ai-weekly-insight` | AI Weekly Insight | `cpu` | Log 7 days to unlock | `loggedDays >= 7` |

#### Weight Tracker insights (`screen: 'weight'`)

| id | Name | Icon | Requirement text (locked copy) | Exact unlock check |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `logging-consistency` | Logging Consistency | `check-circle` | Log 1 weight entry to unlock | `weightEntries >= 1` |
| `bmi` | Body Mass Index | `activity` | Log 1 weight entry and set your height | `weightEntries >= 1 && hasHeight` |
| `weight-fluctuation` | Weight Fluctuation | `git-branch` | Log 3 weight entries to unlock | `weightEntries >= 3` |
| `goal-progress` | Goal Progress | `flag` | Log 3 weight entries and set a target weight | `weightEntries >= 3 && hasTargetWeight` |
| `weekly-rate` | Weekly Rate of Change | `zap` | Log 5 weight entries over 2+ weeks | `weightEntries >= 5 && weightEntrySpanDays >= 14` |
| `weight-vs-calories` | Weight vs Calories | `layers` | Log 5 days with both weight and food data | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 5` |
| `estimated-goal-date` | Estimated Goal Date | `calendar` | Log 7 weight entries over 3+ weeks | `weightEntries >= 7 && weightEntrySpanDays >= 21` |
| `monthly-comparison` | Monthly Comparison | `columns` | Log weight in 2 different months | `monthsWithWeightData >= 2` |
| `deficit-surplus-ai` | Deficit & Surplus Impact | `cpu` | Log 7 days with both weight and food data | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 7` |
| `milestones-records` | Milestones & Records | `award` | Log 10 weight entries to unlock | `weightEntries >= 10` |

Note the ordering vs definition order: in `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` the weight block is declared `logging-consistency` before `bmi`, but the `InsightId` union lists `bmi` first. Order in the array matters because `getFirstUnseenUnlock` and the locked render order both iterate `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` top to bottom.

Two announcement one liners (`description`) worth noting because they appear in the Home unlock card: e.g. Calorie Bank is "Your weekly budget, banked calories, and bank utilization"; Micronutrients is "Vitamins, minerals, and omega-3 vs your personalized targets". All 21 descriptions are in the array.

### InsightStats: the inputs to every check

`InsightStats` is the only argument to every `check`. The interface:

| Field | Type | Meaning | How HomeScreen computes it |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `loggedDays` | number | Days with at least 1 food entry | `Object.values(summaries).filter(s => s.entryCount > 0).length` |
| `uniqueFoods` | number | Count of distinct foods logged | Hardcoded `0` in HomeScreen (`// not critical for unlock checks that don't use it`). No current insight check reads it. |
| `weightEntries` | number | Total weight entries | `(weightEntries || []).length` |
| `weightEntrySpanDays` | number | Days between first and last weight entry | `Math.round` of `abs(last - first) / 86_400_000`; `0` if fewer than 2 entries |
| `hasTargetWeight` | boolean | User set a target weight | `!!(goals?.targetWeightKg)` |
| `hasHeight` | boolean | User set height | `!!(goals?.heightCm || goals?.heightFeet)` |
| `calorieAndWeightDays` | number | Days with both calorie and weight data | Intersection of the food date set and the weight date set, counted day by day |
| `monthsWithWeightData` | number | Distinct calendar months containing a weight entry | `Set` of `${year}-${month}` over weight entries, then `.size` |
| `calorieBankEnabled` | boolean (optional) | Whether the weekly calorie bank is on | `!!bankConfig?.enabled` |

Important caveats baked into the current implementation:

- `loggedDays` counts days present in the summaries map with `entryCount > 0`. It is a count of distinct logged days, not consecutive days. There is no streak requirement; gaps do not reset progress.
- `calorieAndWeightDays` keys both sides on local `YYYY-MM-DD` strings (food side uses `summaries` keys directly; weight side rebuilds the key from `new Date(e.date)` with `getFullYear/getMonth/getDate`). Same day pairing is required for the count to increment.
- `uniqueFoods` is currently dead input. The comment in HomeScreen flags it as an approximation that real foods would need meal data to compute. No insight gates on it today, so the `0` is harmless, but any new insight using `uniqueFoods` would need real wiring first.

### Detecting and announcing new unlocks

The flow runs inside `checkInsightUnlocks(summaries)` (HomeScreen 738-822), called after data loads (`loadAllData`, line 1085) and after summaries change (line 715), always fire and forget (`.catch(() => {})`).

1. Load existing unlocks from AsyncStorage (`dataStorage.loadInsightUnlocks`) and push into React state via `setInsightUnlocks`. This is unconditional so the analysis screens always have the current map even before the `isPremium` memo settles (avoids a stale isPremium race on cold start).
2. Premium check. If not premium, surface any existing unseen announcement via `getFirstUnseenUnlock` and return without minting anything.
3. Build `InsightStats` from summaries, weight entries, goals, and bank config.
4. `getNewlyUnlockedInsights(stats, existingUnlocks)` returns the definitions whose `check` now passes but which have no record in `existingUnlocks`. It is `getUnlockedInsightIds(stats)` filtered to IDs not already present.
5. For each newly unlocked insight, write `updatedUnlocks[def.id] = { unlockedAt: now }` (ISO string, no `seenAt` yet), persist with `saveInsightUnlocks`, and update state.
6. Pick the announcement: `getFirstUnseenUnlock(updatedUnlocks)` walks `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` in array order and returns the first record that exists but has no `seenAt`. That definition becomes `pendingUnlockAnnouncement`.
7. If nothing newly unlocked, it still checks `existingUnlocks` for a leftover unseen announcement so a previously missed unlock can still surface.

`InsightUnlockRecord` is `{ unlockedAt: string; seenAt?: string }`. `unlockedAt` is stamped when the insight first crosses its threshold. `seenAt` is stamped only when the user interacts with the announcement card. `isInsightUnlocked(id, unlocks)` is simply `!!unlocks[id]` — presence of a record means unlocked, independent of seen state, which is why the analysis screens can render the chart immediately even if the Home card was never tapped.

### The Home announcement card

When `pendingUnlockAnnouncement` is set and the user is premium, Home renders `InsightUnlockCard` (HomeScreen 2744-2773). The card shows a primary tinted icon box (`${primary}15` background) with the insight's Feather icon, the literal label "New Insight Unlocked", a green `#10B981` "NEW" pill, the insight `name`, its `description`, an X dismiss button, and a "Tap to view" footer with a chevron.

Two interactions, both defined in `InsightUnlockCard.tsx` as `onDismiss` and `onPress` props and wired in HomeScreen:

- Dismiss (X): `markInsightSeen(id)` stamps `seenAt`, reloads unlocks into state, then advances to the next unseen via `getFirstUnseenUnlock`. The card either shows the next queued unlock or disappears.
- Tap (the card body): same `markInsightSeen` + advance, then it deep links. It sets `scrollToInsightId` to the tapped insight's id and opens the right screen on its Insights tab. Nutrition: `setOpenNutritionOnInsights(true)` + `setShowNutritionAnalysis(true)`. Weight: `setOpenWeightOnInsights(true)` + `setShowWeightTracker(true)`.

Because announcements queue, multiple simultaneous unlocks (e.g. crossing day 5 unlocks `weekly-pattern`, `nutrition-balance`, and `micronutrient-balance` at once) surface one at a time in `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` order, each requiring a dismiss or tap before the next appears.

### Locked placeholder vs unlocked content (InsightSlot pattern)

Both analysis screens render every insight inside an `InsightSlot`, regardless of unlock state, so the layout is stable and positions can be measured:

```tsx
const InsightSlot = ({ id, children }) => (
  <View onLayout={registerInsightPosition(id)}>{children}</View>
);
```

`registerInsightPosition(id)` stores the slot's `nativeEvent.layout.y` into a `useRef` map `insightPositions.current[id]`. This is how the scroll target is known later.

Inside each slot the screen branches on `isUnlocked(id)` (which calls `isInsightUnlocked(id, insightUnlocks)`):

- Locked: renders `LockedInsightCard`, a dimmed card (`opacity: 0.5`) with a lock icon, the insight `name`, and the `requirementText` from the definition. This is what nudges the user toward the threshold.
- Unlocked: renders the actual chart. There is a third state for insights that need goals or enough data. If unlocked but goals are missing, the nutrition screen shows `NeedsGoalsCard` ("Set your goals to use this insight", taps through to set goals) instead of an empty gap. Example: `goal-adherence` shows the chart only when `(targetProtein || targetCarbs || targetFat)` exists; otherwise `NeedsGoalsCard`. Some charts also require enough plotted data (e.g. `calorie-trend` needs `graphData.length >= 2`, `weekly-pattern` needs `>= 3`).

So a single slot can be in four visible states: locked placeholder, unlocked-but-needs-goals, unlocked-but-insufficient-data, or fully rendered chart.

### scrollToInsight landing

When Home deep links, it passes the tapped id down as the `scrollToInsight` prop to both analysis screens, along with `initialTab` set to `Insights` and an `onScrollToInsightConsumed` callback that clears `scrollToInsightId` back to `null` in HomeScreen.

The screen's effect (NutritionAnalysisScreen 140-151, mirrored in WeightTracker) does:

1. Force `setActiveTab('Insights')` so the right tab is showing.
2. After a `450ms` `setTimeout` (giving the tab and `onLayout` measurements time to settle), read `insightPositions.current[scrollToInsight]` and `insightsScrollRef.current.scrollTo({ y: Math.max(0, y - 16), animated: true })`. The `- 16` leaves a small top margin so the card is not flush to the header.
3. Call `onScrollToInsightConsumed?.()` so Home resets the prop and the effect does not re fire.

This is the fix for the past bug where an unlocked chart "did not show" because the tap landed on the wrong tab. The combination of forcing the Insights tab plus scrolling to the exact registered y position guarantees the user lands on the specific chart they were told unlocked.

### Persistence and sync

`saveInsightUnlocks` writes the full map to AsyncStorage under `@trackkal:insightUnlocks`, then, if there is a cached account with `supabaseUserId`, fires `supabaseDataService.upsertInsightUnlocks` in the background (`void ... .catch`). This follows the local first rule: the write returns immediately, Supabase sync is best effort and never blocks. `loadInsightUnlocks` reads AsyncStorage and returns `{}` on any miss or parse error. On account hydration, unlocks are also fetched from Supabase (`fetchInsightUnlocks`) and merged on sync (dataStorage 588, 709). `markInsightSeen(id)` loads, stamps `seenAt` if the record exists, and re saves (which re triggers the same background sync).

### Building a new insight (the contract)

To add an insight an LLM must touch exactly these points, all in `insightUnlockEngine.ts` plus the rendering screen:

1. Add the id to the `InsightId` union.
2. Add an `InsightDefinition` entry to `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` with `name`, `description`, `screen`, Feather `icon`, `requirementText`, and a `check`. Array position controls announcement and render order.
3. If the `check` needs a new signal, add it to `InsightStats` and compute it in `checkInsightUnlocks` (HomeScreen ~784). Reusing existing fields avoids this step.
4. Wrap the chart in an `InsightSlot id="..."` on the relevant screen, with the `!isUnlocked(id)` → `LockedInsightCard` / `isUnlocked(id)` → chart branch, plus a needs-goals or needs-data fallback if applicable.

Because checks are pure and centralized, the requirement copy on the locked card and the announcement always stay consistent with the actual gate. There is no separate place to keep in sync.

---

## 10. Weight Tracker: Charts, Smart Adjustments, BMI

The Weight Tracker is a modal screen (`src/screens/WeightTrackerScreen.tsx`, ~2549 lines) opened from `HomeScreen` via `handleWeightTracker`. It has two tabs: **Tracker** (free) and **Insights** (premium only). All weight is stored internally in **kilograms**; pounds is a display-only conversion. The Smart Adjustment system lives outside this screen — its engine is in `dataStorage.ts` and its UI (banner + modal) renders on `HomeScreen`.

### Data model

Weight entries are `{ id?, date: Date, weight: number /* kg */, updatedAt?: string, seeded?: boolean }`. Entries seed from `UserContext.weightEntries` synchronously on mount (no async delay). If context is empty but an onboarding `initialCurrentWeightKg` exists, a single `seeded: true` entry is created for today.

**The seed is display-only and never persisted.** Persisting it would turn it into a real today-dated weigh-in, which then blocks daily logging on the PWA. The persistence effect (`useEffect` on `weightEntries`) filters out seeded entries: `const real = weightEntries.filter(e => !e.seeded)`. If only the seed exists, nothing is written.

**Deduplication by day.** `deduplicateByDate` keys entries by `yyyy-MM-dd` and keeps the one with the latest `updatedAt`. Re-sorts ascending by date.

### Weight logging

| Behavior | Detail |
|---|---|
| Entry point | "Log Weight" button at bottom of Tracker tab; opens `showLogModal` |
| Once-a-day guard | Before opening the modal, checks `weightEntries.some(e => !e.seeded && format(e.date,'yyyy-MM-dd') === todayKey)`. If already logged today, shows alert `"You've already logged today's weight.\nYou can edit it anytime if you need to make a change."` and does **not** open the modal. |
| Same-day replace | In `handleLogWeight`, if an entry exists for `logDate`'s day key, it is replaced in place (keeps/assigns `id`, sets `seeded: false`, new `updatedAt`), not duplicated. |
| Validation | `parseFloat(logWeight)`; rejects `NaN` or `<= 0` with alert `"Invalid Weight" / "Please enter a valid weight."` |
| Unit conversion | Input is in display unit; stored via `convertWeightFromDisplay(weight, weightUnit)`. lbs→kg uses `* 0.453592`. |
| Analytics | `analyticsService.trackWeightEntryLogged(logDate)` on save. |
| Default date | `logDate` resets to `new Date()` each time the modal opens (logs are effectively "today" only via the UI; there is no date picker in the log modal). |

**History table** (`historyEntries`, newest-first): each row supports inline **edit** (pencil) and **delete** (trash). Edit uses `convertWeightToDisplay(...).toFixed(1)` in the field and `convertWeightFromDisplay` on save (validation: reject `NaN`/`<=0`). Delete confirms via `Alert` (`"Delete weight entry for {d MMM yyyy}?"`, destructive). `handleClose` (drag-down or chevron) force-saves `weightEntries` before `onBack`.

### Units (kg / lb)

Conversion lives in `PreferencesContext`. Source of truth is kg.

| Direction | Factor |
|---|---|
| kg → lbs (display) | `weightKg * 2.20462` |
| lbs → kg (storage) | `weight * 0.453592` |
| Label | `weightUnit === 'kg' ? 'kg' : 'lbs'` |

All charts, insights, and hero cards run displayed numbers through `convertWeightToDisplay(...)` and label with `getWeightUnitLabel()`. Default unit is `'kg'`.

### Hero cards (above tabs, shown when `hasEntries`)

| Card | Value | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| CURRENT | last entry weight | `--` if none |
| {Drop/Gain/Change} | `currentWeight - startingWeight` | Label derived from actual direction: `>0` → "Gain", `<0` → "Drop", `0` → "Change". Defaults to goal-based ("Gain" if gain goal else "Drop") when no change exists. Trend-up icon shows when change `>0.05`, trend-down when `<-0.05`; icon color flips by goal (`isGainGoal` makes up=green/down=red). |
| TARGET | `targetWeight` | If `targetWeightValue <= 0`, renders a "Set Goal" link calling `onRequestSetGoals`. |

### The weight chart

| Property | Value / Source |
|---|---|
| Library | `react-native-svg` (`Path`, `Circle`, `Line`, `Text`) |
| Dimensions | `graphWidth = screenWidth - 32 - 36`; `graphHeight = 260`; `graphPadding = 20`; `paddingLeft = 45` (Y-axis label room) |
| Time ranges | `1W, 1M, 3M, 6M, 1Y` (default `1Y`). 1W=`subDays(now,7)`, 1M/3M/6M=`subMonths`, 1Y=`subYears(now,1)`. Filter compares at `startOfDay`. |
| Y-axis | Auto-scaled. `axisPad = max(range*0.1, 1)`; `minAxis = floor(min - pad)`, `maxAxis = ceil(max + pad)`; if equal, ±1. Integer tick step `max(1, round(range/5))`. Labels rendered via `convertWeightToDisplay(value).toFixed(0)`. |
| Path | Catmull-Rom-style smooth bezier (`generateSmoothPath`); control points use `dx/6, dy/6`. 1 point → `M` only; 2 points → straight `L`. |
| Dots | Only drawn when `graphData.length < 20` (radius 4, card fill, primary stroke). |
| Animation | On every `graphData` change: `chartOpacity` 0.15→1 over 350ms; line-draw via `strokeDashoffset` 1800ms. |
| Scrubbing | Horizontal-only `PanResponder` (claims gesture only when `|dx| > |dy|` and `|dx| > 5`, so vertical scroll still works). Snaps to nearest point by x-distance; shows a tooltip (`MMM d, yyyy` + `weight unit`) and a dashed cursor line + enlarged dot. |
| Empty axis | When no data: min 0, max 5, ticks `[0..5]`. |
| Date range label | `{d MMM yyyy} - {d MMM yyyy}` from filtered (or all) data. |

### Daily trend insight (Tracker tab, free)

A non-AI heuristic insight box below the chart. Generated **once per day** (`insightGeneratedDate === today` guard), persisted to `@trackkal:weightInsight` as `{ insight, date }`, reloaded only if `date === today`. Resets and regenerates when the time range changes (`handleTimeRangeChange` clears it). Requires `graphData.length >= 2`.

Logic (over `graphData` first→last):

| Condition (in order) | Icon | Color | Copy |
|---|---|---|---|
| `variability > 0.02` (CoV = stdDev/avg) | `activity` | warning | "Your weight is fluctuating. Consider tracking hydration and sleep patterns to identify patterns." |
| `abs(change) < 0.5` | `check-circle` | success | "Your weight has been stable. Great consistency! Keep maintaining your current routine." |
| `change > 0.5` | `trending-up` | gain-goal→success else error | "You've gained {x} {unit} over this period." |
| `change < -0.5` | `trending-down` | gain-goal→error else success | "You've lost {x} {unit} over this period. Keep up the great progress!" |
| else | `minus-circle` | secondary | "Your weight shows minimal change. Small fluctuations are normal and expected." |

### Insights tab (premium-gated)

The Insights tab button only renders when `isPremium === true` (line ~1122). Every card is wrapped in an `InsightSlot` that registers its scroll Y so `scrollToInsight` can land on the exact card (450ms delay, scrolls to `y - 16`). Each card checks `isUnlocked(id)` = `isInsightUnlocked(id, insightUnlocks)` = `!!unlocks[id]`. Unlocked-but-no-data cards simply don't render; cards that fail the unlock check render a `LockedInsightCard` (lock icon + name + `requirementText`). At the bottom, a second pass renders `renderLockedCard(...)` static placeholders for any card whose data is missing.

**Unlock thresholds** (from `insightUnlockEngine.ts` `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS`; all `screen: 'weight'`). Unlock status is computed centrally from `InsightStats` and passed in as the `insightUnlocks` prop:

| Insight | id | Unlock requirement (`check`) | requirementText |
|---|---|---|---|
| Logging Consistency | `logging-consistency` | `weightEntries >= 1` | Log 1 weight entry to unlock |
| Body Mass Index | `bmi` | `weightEntries >= 1 && hasHeight` | Log 1 weight entry and set your height |
| Weight Fluctuation | `weight-fluctuation` | `weightEntries >= 3` | Log 3 weight entries to unlock |
| Goal Progress | `goal-progress` | `weightEntries >= 3 && hasTargetWeight` | Log 3 weight entries and set a target weight |
| Weekly Rate of Change | `weekly-rate` | `weightEntries >= 5 && weightEntrySpanDays >= 14` | Log 5 weight entries over 2+ weeks |
| Weight vs Calories | `weight-vs-calories` | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 5` | Log 5 days with both weight and food data |
| Estimated Goal Date | `estimated-goal-date` | `weightEntries >= 7 && weightEntrySpanDays >= 21` | Log 7 weight entries over 3+ weeks |
| Monthly Comparison | `monthly-comparison` | `monthsWithWeightData >= 2` | Log weight in 2 different months |
| Deficit & Surplus Impact | `deficit-surplus-ai` | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 7` | Log 7 days with both weight and food data |
| Milestones & Records | `milestones-records` | `weightEntries >= 10` | Log 10 weight entries to unlock |

> Note: the locked-placeholder `requirementText` strings shown at the bottom of the rendered card list differ slightly from the engine's `requirementText` (they describe data-availability rather than the unlock gate). E.g. Estimated Goal Date placeholder says "Requires a target weight and at least 3 days of weigh-ins." while the engine gate is 7 entries over 21 days. The engine's `check` is authoritative for whether the card unlocks; the data computation (below) independently determines whether the card has anything to show.

#### Card data computations (memoized in the screen)

**BMI** (`bmiData`): requires `currentWeight` and `heightCm > 0`. `heightCm` derived from `goals.heightCm`, or `(heightFeet*12 + heightInches) * 2.54`.
- Formula: `bmi = currentWeight / (heightM^2)` where `heightM = heightCm/100`.
- Categories: `<18.5` Underweight (blue `#3B82F6`); `<25` Normal (green `#10B981`); `<30` Overweight (amber `#F59E0B`); else Obese (red `#EF4444`).
- Gauge position: `clamp01((bmi - 15) / (40 - 15))` over a 15–40 scale. Bar segments flex 3.5 / 6.5 / 5 / 10. Legend ranges shown: `<18.5`, `18.5–24.9`, `25–29.9`, `30+`.

**Goal Progress** (`goalProgressData`): requires `currentWeight`, `targetWeight`, `startingWeight`.
- Maintain goal: `diff = |current - target|`; status `On Target` if `diff < 1` (green) else `Off Target` (amber); percentage forced to 100. (Maintain cards are rendered only when `!isMaintain`, so they don't show the bar.)
- Lose/Gain: `totalRequired = |target - start|`; `achieved = isGain ? current-start : start-current`; `remaining = isGain ? target-current : current-target`; `ratio = clamp01(achieved/totalRequired)`; `percentage = round(ratio*100)`. Status: `Goal Reached` if `remaining<=0`, else `On Track` if `achieved>0` (green) else `Off Track` (amber).

**Weekly Rate of Change** (`weeklyRateData`): needs `>= 2` entries spanning `>= 3` days.
- `weeks = daysDiff/7`; `weeklyRate = (lastWeight - firstWeight)/weeks` (positive = gaining).
- Direction: `gaining` if `>0.01`, `losing` if `<-0.01`, else `maintaining`.
- Color: aligned with goal → green; misaligned → amber; maintaining → gray `#71717A`; no goal → blue if gaining / amber if losing. Info copy states a healthy loss rate is "0.5 to 1 kg per week."

**Estimated Goal Date** (`estimatedGoalData`): needs `weeklyRateData`, `currentWeight`, `targetWeight`, non-maintain goal.
- Already at/past goal → `{reached:true, message:'Goal reached!'}` (green).
- `|rate| < 0.01` → "Not enough change to project a date" (gray).
- Moving wrong direction → "Currently moving away from goal" (amber).
- Else `weeksLeft = |remaining / rate|`; `goalDate = today + round(weeksLeft*7) days`. Display: `<1 week` → days; `>=52` → years (`/52`, 1 decimal); else weeks.

**Logging Consistency** (`loggingConsistency`): needs `>= 1` entry.
- Week = Monday-based (`mondayOffset = day===0 ? 6 : day-1`). `daysInWeekSoFar = mondayOffset + 1`.
- `count` = distinct logged days this week; `ratio = count/daysInWeekSoFar`. Color: `>=0.8` green, `>=0.5` amber, else red `#EF4444`.
- Message: `count===7` → "Perfect week!"; `count===daysInWeekSoFar` → "On track for a perfect week!"; `count===0` → "No weigh-ins yet this week."; else null.
- Renders 7 day-dots (M T W T F S S); logged=green, future=faded border, today=outlined.

**Weight Fluctuation** (`fluctuationData`): needs `>= 2` entries in the last 7 days.
- `range = max - min`; `isNormal = range < 2` (kg). Normal → green text + "— that's normal."; else amber + "— consider tracking hydration and sodium."

**Monthly Comparison** (`monthlyComparison`): per-month change = last − first entry of that calendar month (needs `>= 2` entries in a month, else `null`). Renders this-month vs last-month deltas. Loss colored green `#10B981`, gain blue `#3B82F6`, no-data tertiary.

**Milestones & Records** (`milestoneData`): needs `>= 1` entry.
- Lowest/highest = min/max weight entries with dates. `totalChange = |current - start|`.
- Milestone strings from goal percentage: `>=100` "You reached your goal!"; `>=75` "You're 75% of the way there!"; `>=50` "Halfway to your goal!"; `>=25` "You're 25% of the way there!". Plus, if `totalChange >= 5`: "You've changed {x} {unit} total".

**Weight vs Calories** (`calorieCorrelation`): needs `>= 3` weight entries and non-empty `dailySummaries`. Looks back **14 days**, keeps days that have both an entry and `summary.totalCalories > 0`; requires `>= 3` such days. Renders blue calorie bars + green weight line/dots on a 120px SVG; legend shows `avg` calories.

**Deficit & Surplus Impact** (AI). Needs `>= 7` weight entries and non-empty `dailySummaries`. Refreshed **weekly on Mondays** (keyed by Monday's `yyyy-MM-dd`, cached at `@trackkal:deficitInsight`). Collects up to **4 prior weeks** of `{week, avgCalories, weightChange}` (each week needs `>= 2` entries); requires `>= 2` weeks of data. Calls `invokeAI`:
- `model: 'gpt-4o-mini'`, `temperature: 0.7`, `max_tokens: 100`.
- System: "You are a concise nutrition coach. Analyze the weekly calorie and weight data. Give ONE short insight (2 sentences max)... Be encouraging. Use specific numbers from the data. Do not use emojis."
- This is a free-text prompt (no JSON schema), consistent with the architecture note that Deficit/Surplus prompts don't need schemas.

### Smart Adjustment system

Detects when measured weight has drifted enough from a baseline to warrant re-tuning the daily calorie/macro targets. The detection engine is `dataStorage.checkAndGenerateAdjustment()`; UI is `SmartAdjustmentBanner` + `SmartAdjustmentModal`, both rendered on `HomeScreen` (not in the Weight Tracker screen).

**When it triggers.** `checkAndGenerateAdjustment` is called on `HomeScreen` in two places: inside `loadAllData` (line ~969) and in a `useEffect` that fires whenever the Weight Tracker closes (`!showWeightTracker`, line ~358). If it returns a `pending` record, `setAdjustmentAvailable` shows the banner.

**Preconditions** (any failure → returns `null`):
1. `prefs.dynamicAdjustmentEnabled` must be true. Default in `dataStorage` defaults is **`true`** ("Enable by default for visibility").
2. Goals and `>= 1` weight entry must exist.
3. Baseline = `prefs.lastAdjustmentWeight` if set; otherwise (first time) the **oldest** weight entry, which requires `>= 2` entries.
4. Skip if `baselineWeight === currentWeight`.

**Trigger math.**
```
percentChange   = (currentWeight - baselineWeight) / baselineWeight
thresholdDecimal = prefs.dynamicAdjustmentThreshold / 100
fire if           |percentChange| >= thresholdDecimal
```
`dynamicAdjustmentThreshold` is a percentage (`3, 4, or 5` per the type comment) but the shipped default is **`2`** ("Lower threshold to 2% for easier testing"). So by default an adjustment fires once measured weight moves ≥2% from baseline.

**Adjustment amount** (by pace via `goals.activityRate`):

| `activityRate` | Pace | kcal step |
|---|---|---|
| `<= 0.25` | Mild | 100 |
| `<= 0.5` | Normal | 200 |
| `> 0.5` | Fast | 300 |
| unset | (default) | 200 |

**New target.** `gain` goal → `newCalories = goals.calories + step`; otherwise (`lose`/`maintain`) → `goals.calories - step`. Hard floor: `if (newCalories < 1200) newCalories = 1200`.

**New macros** are recomputed from the goal's macro split percentages applied to `newCalories`:
```
protein = round((newCalories * proteinPercentage/100) / 4)
carbs   = round((newCalories * carbsPercentage/100)   / 4)
fats    = round((newCalories * fatPercentage/100)      / 9)
```
The record also stores `previousMacros` (current `proteinGrams/carbsGrams/fatGrams`) for the strikethrough display.

**Record shape** (`AdjustmentRecord`): `{ id, date (YYYY-MM-DD), previousCalories, newCalories, previousWeight, currentWeight, threshold, status: 'applied'|'dismissed'|'pending', previousMacros, macros }`.

#### SmartAdjustmentBanner

Static blue card: title "Smart Plan Update Available", subtitle "Prevent plateaus with new targets", activity icon. Visible only when `adjustmentAvailable` is set. Tapping opens the modal; the X dismisses (calls `handleDismissAdjustment`).

#### SmartAdjustmentModal

| Element | Detail |
|---|---|
| Header | "Smart Adjustment" + collapsible blurb ("Smart Update automatically fine-tunes your nutrition targets based on your weight progress." / "This prevents plateaus and ensures your goals stay realistic and effective.") with Read more/Show less. |
| Weight Change row | `{previousWeight}kg → {currentWeight}kg` (rendered in kg literally, not unit-converted). |
| Daily Goal | `previousCalories` (strikethrough) → editable `newCalories` kcal. Pencil toggles edit mode. |
| Macro split | Protein (blue `#3B82F6`), Carbs (green `#10B981`), Fats (amber `#F59E0B`). View mode shows old value strikethrough + new; edit mode is inline number inputs. |
| Actions | "Not Now" (dismiss) / "Update My Plan" (apply). |

**In-modal edit math (bi-directional):**
- Edit calories → macros recompute from saved ratios: `protein = round(cals*ratio.p/4)`, `carbs = round(cals*ratio.c/4)`, `fats = round(cals*ratio.f/9)`. Initial ratios derived from suggested macros: `p=(protein*4)/cal, c=(carbs*4)/cal, f=(fats*9)/cal`.
- Edit a macro → calories recompute: `total = p*4 + c*4 + f*9`, and ratios update from the new total.
- **Floor guard:** `minAllowed = previousCalories - 300`; if edited calories `< minAllowed` → `isTooLow`. Shows red border + "Max reduction: 300 kcal (Min: {minAllowed})"; "Update My Plan" is disabled. (Rule: max single reduction is 300 kcal below the previous target.)

**Apply / dismiss outcomes** (`dataStorage`):
- `applyAdjustment(record)`: writes new `calories`/`proteinGrams`/`carbsGrams`/`fatGrams` into goals; sets `prefs.lastAdjustmentWeight = record.currentWeight` (new baseline); prepends `{...record, status:'applied'}` to adjustment history. HomeScreen then `loadAllData()` and shows `"Your plan has been updated! 🚀"`.
- `dismissAdjustment(record)`: prepends `{...record, status:'dismissed'}` to history **and still updates `lastAdjustmentWeight = currentWeight`** so the same drift does not immediately re-prompt.

Note: `smartSuggestEnabled` is a separate (newer) preference flag and is not what gates this engine; the engine gates strictly on `dynamicAdjustmentEnabled`.

### Premium vs free summary

| Surface | Free | Premium |
|---|---|---|
| Tracker tab (chart, hero cards, daily trend insight, history, logging) | ✅ | ✅ |
| Insights tab button | ❌ (not rendered) | ✅ (`isPremium === true`) |
| All 10 insight cards | ❌ | ✅ (further gated per-card by unlock thresholds) |
| Smart Adjustment banner/modal | ✅ (gated on `dynamicAdjustmentEnabled` only, not premium) | ✅ |

### What I could not fully verify / caveats

- **`isPremium` here is the prop passed by the parent**, not recomputed in this screen. Whether `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` grants the Insights tab depends on how `HomeScreen` derives the `isPremium` prop it passes down (out of scope for this file). The canonical `isPremium = premium plan AND signed-in-with-email` check lives in `HomeScreen`.
- The Weight Change row in `SmartAdjustmentModal` prints raw `kg` and does not honor the user's lb preference — a likely display bug for lb users.
- `dynamicAdjustmentThreshold` default is **2** in code despite the type comment saying "3, 4, or 5"; treat 2% as the shipped trigger until changed.
- UI/animation behavior (scrubbing, draw animation, modal collapse) is described from code and has not been visually tested here.

---

## 11. Micronutrients: Targets, Card, Deficiency Logic

---

### Overview

TrackKcal tracks **15 micronutrients and detailed macros** beyond the headline calories/protein/carbs/fat. Each is compared against a **personalized daily target** derived from the user's age and sex. The system has two files:

- `src/utils/microTargets.ts` — pure logic: target derivation, percent-of-target math, and status bucketing.
- `src/components/MicronutrientCard.tsx` — the UI: one card with a labeled progress bar per nutrient, in 1D or multi-day average mode.

Targets cite **NIH Office of Dietary Supplements DRI tables, AHA sodium guidance, AI/AMDR for omega-3, and US RDA / FDA Daily Values**. The header comment notes these are "the same numbers used by Apple Health." General-population values only: **pregnancy, lactation, and clinical conditions are NOT factored in**, and the UI is required to show a "talk to a doctor" disclaimer wherever surfaced.

### Gating: premium vs free

| Aspect | Status |
| --- | --- |
| Premium gate | **None.** The Micronutrients card is not premium-gated. It is an insight-unlock card, not an `isPremium` feature. |
| Unlock requirement | `loggedDays >= 5` (insight id `micronutrient-balance` in `insightUnlockEngine.ts`). Below 5 logged days a `LockedInsightCard` shows "Log 5 days to unlock". |
| Render location | `NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx` line ~2153, wrapped in `<InsightSlot id="micronutrient-balance">`. Renders only when `isUnlocked('micronutrient-balance')` and `summariesByDate` is present. |
