| Insight metadata | name "Micronutrients", icon `zap`, screen `nutrition`, description "Vitamins, minerals, and omega-3 vs your personalized targets". |

### The two target kinds

Every target is one of two kinds (`TargetKind`), which flips the entire color/status logic:

| Kind | Meaning | Applies to |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `target` | Aim to reach this amount **or more** | vitamins, minerals, fiber, omega-3, protein |
| `limit` | Stay **under** this amount | sodium, added sugars, saturated fat, cholesterol |

### Full tracked-nutrient list with units, kind, and DailySummary source key

`getMicroTargets(inputs)` returns a `MicroTargetSet` with these fields. The card reads the actual intake from the matching `DailySummary` key (all optional; older summaries may lack them). Card display order is defined by `ORDER` in `MicronutrientCard.tsx` and differs from the type-declaration order.

| Display order | Label | Target field (`MicroTargetSet`) | DailySummary key | Unit | Kind |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Sodium | `sodium_mg` | `totalSodium` | mg | limit |
| 2 | Added sugar | `added_sugars` | `totalAddedSugars` | g | limit |
| 3 | Saturated fat | `saturated_fat` | `totalSaturatedFat` | g | limit |
| 4 | Cholesterol | `cholesterol_mg` | `totalCholesterol` | mg | limit |
| 5 | Calcium | `calcium_mg` | `totalCalcium` | mg | target |
| 6 | Iron | `iron_mg` | `totalIron` | mg | target |
| 7 | Magnesium | `magnesium_mg` | `totalMagnesium` | mg | target |
| 8 | Zinc | `zinc_mg` | `totalZinc` | mg | target |
| 9 | Potassium | `potassium_mg` | `totalPotassium` | mg | target |
| 10 | Fiber | `dietary_fiber` | `totalFiber` | g | target |
| 11 | Omega-3 | `omega_3_g` | `totalOmega3` | g | target |
| 12 | Vitamin A | `vitamin_a_mcg` | `totalVitaminA` | mcg | target |
| 13 | Vitamin C | `vitamin_c_mg` | `totalVitaminC` | mg | target |
| 14 | Vitamin D | `vitamin_d_mcg` | `totalVitaminD` | mcg | target |
| 15 | Vitamin B12 | `vitamin_b12_mcg` | `totalVitaminB12` | mcg | target |

Two more fields exist in `MicroTargetSet` but are **not** rendered by the card:
- `protein_g` (g, target) — mirrored here "for completeness"; protein is shown elsewhere via its own card.
- The type also declares `totalSugar` (natural+total sugar) in `DailySummary`, surfaced by the separate `sugar-load` insight, not this card.

### Target derivation logic

Inputs come from `dataStorage.loadGoals()`: `age`, `gender` (mapped to `sex`), and `proteinGrams` (the protein override from the user's custom plan).

**Defaults and fallbacks.** Age defaults to **30** when missing or non-positive. Sex resolves to `'female'` only when explicitly `'female'`; **`'male'` and `'prefer_not_to_say'` both fall back to male defaults.** Derived age buckets: `isAdult = age >= 19`, `isElder = age >= 51`, `isTeen = age in [14,18]`.

**Sex/age-dependent targets** (the ones that vary):

| Nutrient | Rule | Resulting values |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Dietary fiber | Male: 38 (age ≤50) / 30 (≥51). Female: 25 (≤50) / 21 (≥51) | 21–38 g |
| Calcium | 1300 if age ≤18; else 1000 for men ≤70 and women ≤50; else 1200 (women 51+, men 71+) | 1000 / 1200 / 1300 mg |
| Iron | 18 if female AND age 19–50; else 8 | 8 or 18 mg |
| Magnesium | Male: 400 (≤30) / 420 (>30). Female: 310 (≤30) / 320 (>30). Teen override: 410 male / 360 female | 310–420 mg |
| Zinc | Male 11, female 8 | 8 or 11 mg |
| Potassium | Male 3400, female 2600 | 2600 or 3400 mg |
| Omega-3 (ALA+EPA+DHA, AI) | Male 1.6, female 1.1 | 1.1 or 1.6 g |
| Vitamin A | Male 900, female 700 | 700 or 900 mcg |
| Vitamin C | Male 90, female 75 | 75 or 90 mg |
| Vitamin D | 20 if age ≥71, else 15 | 15 or 20 mcg |
| Vitamin B12 | Flat | 2.4 mcg |
| Protein | `proteinGramsOverride` if > 0, else `round(70 kg × 0.8 g/kg)` = 56 g | from plan or 56 g |

**Fixed limits** (do not vary by age/sex):

| Nutrient | Value | Kind | Source note in code |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Added sugars | 50 g | limit | FDA Daily Value (AHA is stricter: 36 g men / 25 g women) |
| Saturated fat | 20 g | limit | FDA Daily Value (10% of 2000 kcal ÷ 9 ≈ 22 g, rounded to 20) |
| Sodium | 2300 mg | limit | FDA upper limit |
| Cholesterol | 300 mg | limit | historic FDA limit, kept as a soft ceiling |

### Percent-of-target math

`percentOfTarget(actual, target)` = `round((actual / target.value) × 100)`, **clamped to 0–999** (so absurd inputs don't blow up the UI). Returns 0 if the target or its value is falsy.

### Status buckets and color coding

`statusFor(actual, target)` returns a `MicroStatus`. The thresholds differ by kind:

**For `target` kind** (want to reach it):

| Status | Condition (pct of target) | Color | Hex |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `deficient` | < 50% | red | `#EF4444` |
| `low` | 50–79% | amber | `#F59E0B` |
| `on_track` | 80–120% (inclusive) | green | `#10B981` |
| `over` | 121–200% | amber | `#F59E0B` |
| `way_over` | > 200% | red | `#EF4444` |

**For `limit` kind** (want to stay under):

| Status | Condition (pct of limit) | Color | Hex |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `on_track` | < 80% | green | `#10B981` |
| `over` | 80–119% | amber | `#F59E0B` |
| `way_over` | ≥ 120% | red | `#EF4444` |

If `target` is undefined, status defaults to `on_track`. The `STATUS_COLORS` map in the card is the single source for bar/label color. The code comment notes `way_over` "mainly matters for sodium and vitamin A."

### The card UI

Each nutrient renders as a row: **label (fixed 100px) | progress bar (flex) | value block (fixed 90px)**.

- **Bar fill width**: `min(100, pct)` percent. The bar caps visually at 100% even when intake exceeds target, but the numeric percent below can read higher.
- **Bar/percent color**: the status color from `STATUS_COLORS`.
- **Value text**: `{actual} / {target}{unit}` using `formatValue` — grams below 10 show one decimal (`toFixed(1)`), everything else is rounded to a whole number.
- **Percent label**: bold, status-colored. For a `limit` nutrient over 100%, it reads `"{pct}% of limit"`; otherwise just `"{pct}%"`.
- **Disclaimer** (always shown, italic, tertiary color): "Estimates from your food log. For medical concerns, talk to a doctor."
- **Info tooltip** (`info` icon → `Alert.alert`): explains green/yellow/red, that the range follows the top filter, that 1D shows today and longer ranges show the daily average across logged days, and that values are AI estimates.

### 1D vs multi-day modes

The card takes a `timeRange: MicroTimeRange` prop (`'1D' | '1W' | '1M' | '3M' | '6M' | '1Y' | '2Y'`) that follows the screen's top filter. `RANGE_DAYS` maps these to window sizes:

| Range | Days | Subtitle label |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1D | 1 | today |
| 1W | 7 | past 7 days |
| 1M | 30 | past 30 days |
| 3M | 90 | past 90 days |
| 6M | 180 | past 6 months |
| 1Y | 365 | past year |
| 2Y | 730 | past 2 years |

**1D mode**: reads only today's summary (`today.toISOString().split('T')[0]`). A day counts as logged only if `entryCount > 0`. Values are today's raw totals. Subtitle: "Today's intake vs your targets".

**Multi-day mode**: iterates back `rangeDays` from today, collects each date key, filters to days where `summariesByDate[k].entryCount > 0`, and computes a **daily average**: `sum(over logged days) / max(1, loggedDaysCount)`. Key detail — the denominator is the number of **logged** days, not calendar days, so skipped days do not dilute the average. Subtitle variants:

- `loggedDaysInRange === 0` → "No food logged in the {label} yet".
- **Sparse** (some but not full coverage, `0 < loggedDays < expectedDays`) → "Daily average across your {n} logged day(s) in the {label}".
- Full → "Daily average across the {label}".

The card returns `null` until targets load from `loadGoals()`.

### Omega-3, vitamin, and mineral coverage summary

- **Omega-3**: total ALA + EPA + DHA combined into one `omega_3_g` target (1.6 g male / 1.1 g female, AI/AMDR guidance). Not split by fatty-acid type.
- **Vitamins covered (4)**: A, C, D, B12. **Not tracked**: E, K, and the full B-complex beyond B12 (no thiamin, riboflavin, niacin, B6, folate, etc.).
- **Minerals covered (6)**: calcium, iron, magnesium, zinc, potassium, sodium. **Not tracked**: phosphorus, selenium, copper, manganese, iodine, chromium.
- **Other detailed macros covered**: dietary fiber, added sugars, saturated fat, cholesterol (and protein, mirrored but rendered elsewhere).

### Notes for an LLM extending this

1. The actual intake values originate upstream from AI food analysis (`dataStorage.ts` rolls them into `DailySummary` via `round0`/`round1` at ~line 2886+). A new nutrient needs: a field in `DailySummary`, population in the summary rollup, a `MicroTarget` in `MicroTargetSet` + `getMicroTargets`, and an `ORDER` entry in the card. Missing any one yields a 0 actual or a skipped row.
2. `prefer_not_to_say` silently uses male defaults — this overstates female-specific targets (e.g. iron 8 vs 18). Worth flagging if accuracy matters.
3. The visual bar caps at 100% width, so a 300%-over sodium looks identical in bar length to a 100% sodium; only the numeric "% of limit" label distinguishes them.
4. Targets are recomputed once on mount from `loadGoals()`; changing age/sex/protein in settings will not refresh an already-mounted card without a remount.

**v1.2.9**

---

## 12. Premium, Free Tier, Paywall and Monetization

---

### The `isPremium` definition (the single source of truth)

Premium is never gated on plan alone. The canonical memo lives in `src/screens/HomeScreen.tsx` (lines 172-184) and resolves in this exact order:

```ts
const isSignedIn = !!accountInfo?.email;
const isPremium = React.useMemo(() => {
  if (!accountInfo?.email) return false;        // (1) MUST be signed in with an email
  if (FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH) return true;          // (2) launch flag grants premium to all signed-in users
  if (userPlan === 'premium') return true;       // (3) explicit premium plan
  if (accountInfo?.premiumUntil) {               // (4) time-boxed premium (trial / referral grant)
    return new Date(accountInfo.premiumUntil) > new Date();
  }
  return false;
}, [userPlan, accountInfo]);
```

| Condition | Source | Effect |
|---|---|---|
| Signed-out (no `accountInfo.email`) | `HomeScreen.tsx:175` | `isPremium = false` always. No premium feature can be reached. This is the hard floor. |
| `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH === true` | `src/config/featureFlags.ts:11` | Every signed-in user is premium. This is the **current launch state.** |
| `userPlan === 'premium'` | `dataStorage.loadUserPlan()` | Premium when the launch flag is off. |
| `accountInfo.premiumUntil` in the future | `AccountInfo` field | Time-limited premium (trial / referral). |

`FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` is set to `true` today. The downstream `isPremium` check still requires a signed-in account with email, so signed-out users get nothing even during launch. The comment in `featureFlags.ts` states it is flipped to `false` "when paid tiers + RevenueCat go live."

Important consequence: with the launch flag on, the practical gate for every premium feature reduces to **"is the user signed in with an email."** The free-vs-premium split below is the design intent for when the flag flips to `false`; right now the only paywall a user can hit is the **account wall** (sign-in), not a payment wall.

#### Where the check is duplicated (and why)
Some flows recompute premium without the launch flag, intentionally, to avoid stale-state races:
- `HomeScreen.tsx:749` and `checkInsightUnlocks` (`HomeScreen.tsx:749`) use `plan === 'premium' && !!account?.email` directly when deciding whether to *compute and persist new* insight unlocks. Render-time visibility still goes through the full `isPremium` memo.
- `SettingsScreen.tsx:96-109` gates premium feature toggles on two separate checks: `!isSignedIn` shows a "Sign In Required" alert; `plan !== 'premium'` opens the subscription screen. It does **not** consult `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH`, so in Settings the premium toggles are gated on the literal stored plan.

This is a known inconsistency surface: the home/analytics screens honor the launch flag, Settings honors the raw plan. Document it as-is.

---

### Feature gating matrix (complete)

Status reflects design intent (launch flag off). With `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH = true`, every "Premium / Yes" row is available to any signed-in user. "Requires Sign-In" means the feature is dead for signed-out users regardless of flag.

| Feature | Free | Premium | Requires sign-in | Code anchor |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Food logging (text/voice/photo) | 3/day (enforcement disabled pre-launch) | Unlimited | No | `HomeScreen.tsx:1421-1424`, `1464-1477` |
| Meal edits | 3/day (per docs) | Unlimited | No | `HomeScreen.tsx:1674-1680`; docs `app-features.md:103` |
| Photo recognition | Yes | Yes | No | — |
| Calorie + macro tracking | Yes | Yes | No | — |
| Goal setting | Yes | Yes | No | `SetGoalsScreen` |
| Weight tracker (raw chart) | Yes | Yes | No | `WeightTrackerScreen.tsx` |
| Weight tracker Insights tab | No | Yes (progressive unlock) | Yes | `WeightTrackerScreen.tsx:1485` (`activeTab === 'Insights' && isPremium`) |
| Exercise logging | Yes | Yes | No | — |
| Health app sync | Yes | Yes | No | `HealthService` |
| Basic meal reminders | Yes | Yes | No | `NotificationSettingsScreen` |
| Smart / pattern-timed reminders + end-of-day summary | No | Yes | Yes | `smartReminderService.ts` |
| Streak tracking + freezes | Yes (2 freezes/month) | Yes | No | `app-features.md:71` |
| Nutrition Analysis Insights tab (all cards) | No | Yes (progressive unlock) | Yes | `NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx:1770` (`!isPremium` → "Premium Feature" lock) |
| Micronutrient balance card | No | Yes (unlocks at 5 logged days) | Yes | `insightUnlockEngine.ts:131-139` |
| Sugar load card | No | Yes (3 days) | Yes | `insightUnlockEngine.ts:140-148` |
| AI Weekly Insight | No | Yes (7 days) | Yes | `insightUnlockEngine.ts:158-166` |
| Calorie Bank (engine + UI + bank insights) | No | Yes | Yes | `HomeScreen.tsx:240-246, 728-735`; PRD `PRD-calorie-bank.md:112` |
| Dynamic / Smart Adjustments | No | Yes | Yes | `SettingsScreen.tsx:96` (`'dynamic'`), `app-features.md:194` |
| Smart Suggest banner | No | Yes (needs 3+ logged days of data) | Yes | `HomeScreen.tsx:2718` (`isPremium && smartSuggestEnabled`), `SmartSuggestBanner.tsx:56` |
| Pattern Detection | No | Yes (the *fix* is blurred for non-premium) | Yes | `HomeScreen.tsx:1055`; `PatternDetectionCard.tsx:139-150` |
| Predictive / over-budget warnings | No | Yes | Yes | docs `TrackKCal-Complete-Documentation.md:1137` |
| AI Chat Coach | No | Yes | Yes | `HomeScreen.tsx:2907` (floating button rendered only when `isPremium`) |
| Grocery Suggestions | No | Yes + a *separate data unlock* | Yes | `featureFlags.ts:14` (admin-gated) + `dataStorage.checkGroceryUnlockEligibility` |
| Advanced analytics (heatmaps, consistency, macro distribution) | No | Yes | Yes | `NutritionAnalysisScreen.tsx` |
| Deficit & Surplus AI (Weight) | No | Yes (7 days with weight+food) | Yes | `insightUnlockEngine.ts:241-249` |
| Referral program | Yes | Yes | Yes (needs account) | `referralService.ts` |
| Ad-free experience | No (ads planned) | Yes | n/a | `SubscriptionScreen.tsx:41,46` |

Two distinct gates stack on premium features, and both must pass:
1. **Premium gate** — `isPremium === true` (controls whether the feature exists at all).
2. **Progressive data unlock** — for every insight card and for grocery suggestions, even a premium user sees a `LockedInsightCard` placeholder until they have logged enough data. See the unlock thresholds section.

---

### AI Chat Coach: limits and data gate

The coach has three separate gates layered on top of each other.

**1. Premium gate.** The floating coach button only renders when `isPremium` (`HomeScreen.tsx:2907`). Non-premium users never reach the coach screen.

**2. Data sufficiency gate.** Inside the coach, `chatCoachService.buildContext` (`chatCoachService.ts:164-209`) marks data `insufficient` unless:
- `loggedDaysCount >= minLoggedDays` (default **14**), AND
- weight is tracked (`weightTrend.current` is non-null and > 0) when `requireWeight` (default `true`).

When `insufficient`, the input box is replaced with an "AI Nutritionist Locked" panel reading: *"Log meals for 14 days and track your weight to unlock the AI Nutritionist."* (`ChatCoachScreen.tsx:248-255`). The system prompt itself also hard-stops with *"Not enough data yet. Log meals for 7 days and track weight."* if it ever receives insufficient data (`chatCoachService.ts:106-110`). Note the user-facing copy says 14 days; the prompt fallback says 7. The actual gate is 14.

A separate unlock notification fires once via `checkUnlockStatus` (`chatCoachService.ts:130-159`) using a looser rule: `commonFoods.length >= 5 || consistencyScore > 10`, AND weight present.

**3. Daily message rate limit.** From `COACH_LIMITS` (`chatCoachService.ts:12-15`):

| Tier | Messages per day | Constant |
|---|---|---|
| Free | 7 | `COACH_LIMITS.FREE` |
| Premium | 10 | `COACH_LIMITS.PREMIUM` |

The count is stored per-day in AsyncStorage under `@trackkal:coach_usage_v2` and resets at the date boundary (`checkDailyLimit` / `incrementUsage`, `chatCoachService.ts:337-372`). On error the limiter fails open with `{ allowed: true, remaining: 3 }`. When the limit is hit, the input is replaced with a "Daily Limit Reached — Refresh tomorrow for more wisdom." panel (`ChatCoachScreen.tsx:256-263`).

Because the coach is premium-only, free users in practice never consume the 7-message free allowance; the FREE limit is dormant infrastructure for when the coach (or a free preview of it) is opened to non-premium users.

---

### Food-logging entry limits

The design is **3 meals/day** and **3 edits/day** for free, unlimited for premium (`app-features.md:8,103,219-220`; `TrackKCal-Complete-Documentation.md:606,1124`).

**Current launch state: the daily logging limit is DISABLED.** The enforcement function is stubbed:

```ts
const canAddEntry = () => {
  // TODO: Re-enable daily limit (3 meals/day for free users) before launch
  return true;   // HomeScreen.tsx:1421-1424
};
```

The gate plumbing is still wired up. When `canAddEntry()` returns `false`, both the text path (`HomeScreen.tsx:1464-1477`) and the photo path (`HomeScreen.tsx:1970-1976`) raise:

> "Daily Limit Reached — Free plan is limited to 3 meals per day. Claim your 10-day Premium trial or upgrade for unlimited logging!"

with a "View Offer" button that opens the subscription screen. The "10-day Premium trial" is referenced only in this copy string; there is no trial-granting code path wired today.

A separate constant, `FREE_ENTRY_LIMIT = 20` (`AccountScreen.tsx:149`), is a *lifetime* free entry allowance tied to the account/referral system (referrals top it up). It is distinct from the 3/day meal cap. The edit limit has its own alert: "Entry Limit Reached — You have reached your free entry limit. Upgrade to Premium for unlimited entries." (`HomeScreen.tsx:1674-1680`).

---

### Progressive insight unlock thresholds

Every insight card is premium-gated (Insights tab) AND additionally locked behind a data threshold. Thresholds are pure `check(stats)` functions in `src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts`. A premium user with insufficient data sees a `LockedInsightCard` with the requirement text.

**Nutrition Analysis**

| Insight | Unlock condition | Requirement copy |
|---|---|---|
| Goal Adherence | `loggedDays >= 2` | Log 2 days to unlock |
| Macro Split | `loggedDays >= 2` | Log 2 days to unlock |
| Calorie Trend | `loggedDays >= 3` | Log 3 days to unlock |
| Meal Timing | `loggedDays >= 3` | Log 3 days to unlock |
| Sugar Load | `loggedDays >= 3` | Log 3 days to unlock |
| Calorie Bank insights | `loggedDays >= 3 && calorieBankEnabled` | Log 3 days with the calorie bank on |
| Top Foods | `loggedDays >= 4` | Log 4 days to unlock |
| Weekly Pattern | `loggedDays >= 5` | Log 5 days to unlock |
| Nutrition Balance | `loggedDays >= 5` | Log 5 days to unlock |
| Micronutrients | `loggedDays >= 5` | Log 5 days to unlock |
| AI Weekly Insight | `loggedDays >= 7` | Log 7 days to unlock |

**Weight Tracker**

| Insight | Unlock condition | Requirement copy |
|---|---|---|
| Logging Consistency | `weightEntries >= 1` | Log 1 weight entry to unlock |
| Body Mass Index | `weightEntries >= 1 && hasHeight` | Log 1 weight entry and set your height |
| Weight Fluctuation | `weightEntries >= 3` | Log 3 weight entries to unlock |
| Goal Progress | `weightEntries >= 3 && hasTargetWeight` | Log 3 weight entries and set a target weight |
| Weekly Rate of Change | `weightEntries >= 5 && spanDays >= 14` | Log 5 weight entries over 2+ weeks |
| Weight vs Calories | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 5` | Log 5 days with both weight and food data |
| Estimated Goal Date | `weightEntries >= 7 && spanDays >= 21` | Log 7 weight entries over 3+ weeks |
| Monthly Comparison | `monthsWithWeightData >= 2` | Log weight in 2 different months |
| Deficit & Surplus Impact (AI) | `calorieAndWeightDays >= 7` | Log 7 days with both weight and food data |
| Milestones & Records | `weightEntries >= 10` | Log 10 weight entries to unlock |

---

### Grocery Suggestions: triple gate

Grocery Suggestions is gated three ways:
1. **Admin allowlist** (`featureFlags.ts:14-25`): `grocerySuggestions.isEnabled` returns `true` only if the user's email is in `ADMIN_EMAILS` (`admin@trackkcal.com`, `hulexo@trackkcal.com`, `test@trackkcal.com`) or their `supabaseUserId` is in `ADMIN_IDS` (`admin-user-id`). Default is `false`. This is effectively a feature flag, not a public release.
2. **Premium** (`isPremium`).
3. **Data unlock** (`dataStorage.checkGroceryUnlockEligibility`, `dataStorage.ts:3661-3690`): `eligible = loggedDays >= 5 && uniqueFoods >= 7`. Once eligible, `setGroceryUnlocked()` persists `@trackkal:groceryUnlocked`, and a one-time unlock card shows.

---

### Paywall: SubscriptionScreen and pricing

`src/screens/SubscriptionScreen.tsx`. Title "Unlock TrackKcal Premium," subtitle "Ad-free. Unlimited entries. Cancel anytime." Three listed benefits: Ad-Free Experience, Unlimited Entries & History, Priority Features & Updates.

| Plan | Display price | Billing detail | Badge | Default selected |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Annual | **AED 7.50/mo** | "Billed AED89.99 annually" | "Best Value" | Yes (`selectedPlan = 'annual'`) |
| Monthly | **AED 24.99/mo** | "Billed monthly" | none | No |

Annual implied effective price: AED 89.99/yr ≈ AED 7.50/mo, a ~70% discount vs the AED 24.99/mo monthly rate. These are hardcoded display strings in the JSX (`SubscriptionScreen.tsx:73-87`); there is no price catalog, no localization, no store product ID, and no currency other than AED.

**No real payment is processed.** `handleSubscribe` (`HomeScreen.tsx:506-511`) simply flips local state to premium and persists it:
```ts
const handleSubscribe = async (plan) => {
  setUserPlan('premium');
  await dataStorage.saveUserPlan('premium');
  setShowSubscription(false);
  setShowSettings(true);
};
```
There is no RevenueCat, StoreKit, or Google Play Billing integration wired. "Restore purchases" (`SubscriptionScreen.tsx:99-101`) is an optional `onRestore` prop that is not passed in from Home, so the button is currently inert. The screen is functionally a UI shell plus an instant local upgrade. `analyticsService.trackSubscriptionScreenOpen()` fires on open (`HomeScreen.tsx:500`); per `METRICS.md:81`, there is no purchase or premium-activated event yet.

There is **no in-app free trial mechanism** beyond the copy string promising a "10-day Premium trial." `premiumUntil` exists as a field the `isPremium` memo respects, but no code path sets it from a trial.

---

### Account wall (the only live "wall")

Because the launch flag makes premium = signed-in, the real conversion gate is the account wall, not the paywall.

- **Trigger** (`HomeScreen.tsx:1126-1131`): if `goalsSet && entryCount >= 5 && !accountInfo?.email`, the account wall (`QuickSignupScreen`) is shown 1.5s after load. So after 5 logged entries with no account, the user is prompted to create one.
- **Settings premium gate** (`SettingsScreen.tsx:96-109`): tapping any premium toggle (`dynamic`, `smartSuggest`, `patternDetection`, `weeklyOverview`, `grocery`, `calorieBank`) when signed out raises "Sign In Required — You need to sign in to access premium features." with a "Sign In" action. When signed in but `plan !== 'premium'`, it opens the subscription screen instead.

---

### Referral monetization

`referralService.ts`. The reward is **+10 free entries** to both referrer and referee (`entriesAwarded: 10`, lines 269/295/306/349), credited the first time the referred user logs a meal (idempotency-guarded). Rate-limited to **max 5 rewards/week, 10/month** per referrer (`referralService.ts:188`).

Note a copy mismatch to flag: `app-features.md:78` claims referrals grant "3 free premium days per referral," but the code grants 10 *entries*, not premium days. The code is the source of truth: the referral reward is entry credits against the `FREE_ENTRY_LIMIT = 20` allowance, not premium time.

---

### Things worth flagging for the LLM building on this

- **Launch flag collapses the model.** With `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH = true`, "free tier" is unreachable for signed-in users and the only friction is the account wall. Any work touching monetization must decide whether it targets the current (flag-on) reality or the post-flag design. Test both.
- **Gating is inconsistent across screens.** Home/analytics honor `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH`; Settings honors raw `plan`. The coach unlock-notification rule (`commonFoods>=5 || consistency>10`) differs from the coach gate (`loggedDays>=14`). The "7 days" prompt fallback contradicts the "14 days" UI copy.
- **No payments exist.** Subscribe = local plan flip. Restore is inert. There is no store SDK, product catalog, receipt validation, or premium-activated analytics event. Hardcoded AED-only pricing in JSX.
- **Two unrelated "limits" share vocabulary.** The 3/day meal cap (disabled) vs the lifetime `FREE_ENTRY_LIMIT = 20` (referral-toppable) are different systems with overlapping "entry limit" copy.
- **Doc vs code drift:** referral reward (10 entries in code vs "3 premium days" in docs); 3/day enforcement (documented as active, actually stubbed `return true`).

---

## 13. Streaks, Freezes, Referrals and Growth Loops

---

This section documents TrackKcal's gamification and growth systems: logging streaks, streak freezes (branded "recovery days"), the referral program, the account wall, and the first-log nudge. Every number, threshold, and copy string below is cited to the actual source.

### Streaks

A streak counts **consecutive calendar days that have at least one logged meal**, optionally extended by streak-freeze days. The core logic lives in `src/utils/streakUtils.ts` (`calculateStreak`).

#### How a day "counts"

A date is an **active date** if either:

- `summariesByDate[dateKey].entryCount > 0` (at least one meal logged that day), or
- the date appears in `frozenDates` (a freeze was applied to it).

Source: `streakUtils.ts` lines 16-21. `calculateStreak(summariesByDate, frozenDates = [])` builds `activeDates = new Set([...datesWithMeals, ...frozenDates])`.

#### Counting algorithm

| Step | Rule | Code |
|---|---|---|
| Empty case | If `activeDates.size === 0`, streak is `0`. | line 23 |
| Liveness gate | If neither **today** nor **yesterday** is active, streak is `0` (the streak is considered dead). | lines 29-31 |
| Start point | Start counting at **today** if today is active, otherwise at **yesterday**. | lines 34-39 |
| Walk back | Increment streak for each consecutive active day walking backward one calendar day at a time; stop at the first gap. | lines 41-48 |

Key consequences:

- **Today not logged yet does not break the streak.** As long as yesterday is active, the streak survives and is counted from yesterday. The user has until end of "today" to keep it alive.
- **A single fully-missed day (no log, no freeze) breaks the streak to 0** on the following day, unless a freeze covered the gap.
- Streak is recomputed from stored daily summaries on load. It is not an incrementing counter, so it self-heals if summaries change.
- Date keys are local `yyyy-MM-dd` via `date-fns` `format`. There is no timezone normalization beyond device local time.

#### What breaks a streak (summary)

| Event | Streak outcome |
|---|---|
| Log a meal today | Streak continues / starts |
| No log today, logged yesterday | Streak alive, counted from yesterday |
| No log today AND no log yesterday | Streak = 0 |
| One missed day with a freeze available + premium | Freeze auto-applied, streak preserved (see below) |
| One missed day, no freeze (or not premium) | Streak broken |

### Streak freezes ("Recovery Days")

Freezes are stored in `StreakFreezeData` (`dataStorage.ts` lines 301-305):

```
freezesAvailable: number;   // 0-2
lastResetDate: string;      // 'yyyy-MM-01' of current month
usedOnDates: string[];      // 'yyyy-MM-dd' dates a freeze preserved
```

#### Quota and reset

| Property | Value | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Freezes per month | **2** | `HomeScreen.tsx` line 953, `UserContext.tsx` line 82, `streakFreezeData` comment line 302 |
| Reset cadence | Monthly. On load, if `lastResetDate !== format(now, 'yyyy-MM-01')`, `freezesAvailable` resets to 2 and `lastResetDate` updates. | `HomeScreen.tsx` lines 947-958, `UserContext.tsx` lines 76-87 |
| History on reset | `usedOnDates` is **preserved** across the monthly reset; only the counter resets. | `HomeScreen.tsx` line 955 |
| Earned, not purchasable | Freezes are granted (2/month), not bought, not earned through actions. There is no code path that increases `freezesAvailable` above 2. | — |

#### How a freeze is used (auto-apply only)

There is **no manual "use freeze" button**. Freezes apply automatically and retroactively on app load. The branding to the user is "Recovery Day," never "freeze" (`HomeScreen.tsx` line 2612).

The auto-freeze rule (`checkMissedDaysAndFreeze`) protects **yesterday only**:

1. If **yesterday** has no logged meals AND is not already in `usedOnDates`, and
2. **The day before yesterday** was active (logged or frozen) — i.e. there was a real streak to protect, and
3. `freezesAvailable > 0`,

then it consumes one freeze: `freezesAvailable -= 1` and pushes yesterday's date into `usedOnDates`, then persists.

Sources: `HomeScreen.tsx` lines 848-896 and the duplicate `streakLogic.ts` lines 8-56.

| Constraint | Detail |
|---|---|
| Window | Protects **only the immediately previous day** (D-1). It does not recursively repair older gaps. Comment at `streakLogic.ts` lines 47-49 calls this "Yesterday Protection." |
| Streak-exists check | Requires D-2 to be active so a freeze is not "wasted" on a non-streak. `HomeScreen.tsx` lines 871-877. |
| Premium gating | **In `HomeScreen.tsx` the auto-freeze only runs for `plan === 'premium'`** (line 854). The `UserContext`/`streakLogic.ts` copy of the function has **no premium gate** (it runs for any user with freeze data). This is a divergence between the two implementations — see "Known divergences." |
| One per day | A date already in `usedOnDates` is skipped, so the same gap cannot consume two freezes. |

#### Freeze UI feedback

- When a freeze is applied during load, `setJustFrozeToday(true)` is set (`HomeScreen.tsx` line 888). This renders a one-shot banner: heading **"Recovery Day Used"** with body **"We've got you covered. A recovery day was used to save your streak. Reset and ready when you are."** plus a ❄️ emoji (`HomeScreen.tsx` lines 2597-2622).
- The top bar and `StreakWidgetCard` show the streak as "frozen" when `streakFreeze.usedOnDates.includes(currentDateKey) || justFrozeToday` (lines 2559, 3122). Frozen state swaps the flame to a snowflake: `flameEmoji = frozen ? '❄️' : '🔥'`, `flameColor = frozen ? '#38BDF8' : '#F97316'` (`StreakWidgetCard.tsx` lines 84-85).

#### Streak widget (`StreakWidgetCard.tsx`)

A modal that slides from the top (opened via `showStreakWidget`). Contents:

| Element | Detail | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Streak count | `{streak} {streak === 1 ? 'day' : 'days'}`, label "Logging streak" | lines 116-121 |
| Calorie line | `{round(caloriesConsumed)} / {round(caloriesTarget)} kcal` | lines 126-131 |
| Progress bar | `progress = min(1, consumed / target)`; fill is `warning` color when `progress >= 1`, else `success` | lines 83, 138-140 |
| Weekly dots | Monday-start week (`weekStartsOn: 1`), labels `['Mo','Tu','We','Th','Fr','Sa','Su']`. A dot is filled (success color) if `entryCount > 0` OR the date is in `frozenDates`. Future days render dim (opacity 0.4); today renders as a ring (`borderWidth: 2`) when not yet logged. | lines 32, 73-81, 145-168 |

#### Streak reminder notification — status

There is **no dedicated streak-reminder notification** in the codebase. `smartReminderService.ts` schedules meal-slot, macro, calorie, and end-of-day reminders only. Its message set (`GENERIC_MESSAGES`, lines 34-37) is:

| Slot | Title | Body |
|---|---|---|
| breakfast | "Good morning!" | "Don't forget to log your breakfast!" |
| lunch | "Lunchtime!" | "Time to log your lunch!" |
| dinner | "Dinner time!" | "Don't forget to log your dinner!" |

No copy references the streak, "don't break your streak," or the flame. If a streak-reminder is intended, it is **not yet built**. The only streak-saving mechanism currently is the silent retroactive freeze on app open.

### Referral system

Code: `src/services/referralService.ts`, screen `src/screens/ReferralScreen.tsx`. Three stored entities (`dataStorage.ts` lines 258-286): `ReferralCode`, `ReferralRedemption`, `ReferralReward`.

#### Codes

| Property | Value | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Charset | `ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789` (uppercase A-Z + 0-9) | `referralService.ts` line 13 |
| Length | Random **8-10** characters (`8 + floor(random()*3)`) | line 14 |
| Uniqueness | Up to **10** generation attempts checking storage; on failure, fallback is 6 random chars + 4-char base36 timestamp suffix | lines 15-36 |
| Validation regex | `/^[A-Z0-9]{8,10}$/` (uppercased before test) | lines 77-78 |
| One per user | `getOrCreateReferralCode` returns the existing code if present, else generates and saves; `userId` is the owner's email | lines 44-71 |

#### Redemption flow

1. **Validation before redeem** (`validateReferralCodeForRedemption`, lines 112-147), in order:
   - Format must match the regex → else "Invalid code format".
   - Code must exist in storage → else "Referral code not found".
   - **No self-referral**: `referralCode.userId.toLowerCase() !== userEmail.toLowerCase()` → else "You cannot use your own referral code".
   - **One redemption per referee**: `checkIfUserHasUsedReferralCode(userEmail)` must be false → else "You have already used a referral code".
2. **Create redemption** (`createReferralRedemption`, lines 152-185): status `'pending'`, `mealsLogged: 0`, `deviceId = Device.modelName || 'unknown'`. Fraud check runs here and **blocks** if suspicious (throws).
3. **Progress** (`processMealLoggingProgress`, lines 227-358): called after each meal log for a referee with a pending redemption. Increments `mealsLogged`. Reward triggers at **5 meals**.

#### Reward thresholds and amounts

| Threshold | Value | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Meals the referee must log to complete | **5** | `referralService.ts` line 247, type comment line 274 |
| Reward to **referee** | `entriesAwarded: 10`, reason `'referee_reward'` | lines 269, 291-299 |
| Reward to **referrer** | `entriesAwarded: 10`, reason `'referrer_reward'` | lines 302-310 |
| Per-meal progress copy | `"Keep logging meals! ${5 - updatedMealsLogged} more to unlock your referral bonus."` | line 356 |

Idempotency and concurrency guards (lines 248-258): before awarding, it checks `getReferralRewardsForRedemption`; if any reward already exists it returns early ("Rewards already awarded for this referral."). It then marks the redemption `'completed'` **before** writing rewards to prevent concurrent duplicate awards.

On completion it also updates the owner's `ReferralCode`: `totalReferrals += 1`, `totalEarnedEntries += 10` (lines 336-345), and fires a push (`sendReferralRewardNotification`).

#### Abuse guards

| Guard | Rule | Effect | Source |
|---|---|---|---|
| Self-referral | Owner email == referee email | Blocked at validation | lines 127-134 |
| One code per referee | `checkIfUserHasUsedReferralCode` | Blocked at validation | lines 136-144 |
| Device fraud | If the same `deviceId` has **≥ 3** redemptions, flagged suspicious | **Redemption is blocked** (throws "This device has been flagged...") | lines 172-177, 364-382 |
| Referrer weekly cap | **≥ 5** completed referrals in the trailing 7 days | Referrer gets **no** reward this time; referee still gets +10, with message noting the friend hit their limit | lines 198-209, 263-288 |
| Referrer monthly cap | **≥ 10** completed referrals in the trailing 30 days | Same as weekly: referrer skipped, referee still rewarded | lines 213-218 |

Note the rate-limit windows are rolling (`now - 7*24h`, `now - 30*24h`), not calendar week/month (lines 195-196).

#### Referral screen (`ReferralScreen.tsx`)

| Element | Behavior | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Logged-out state | Shows "You need to be logged in to view your referral code" + "Log in" CTA | lines 114-129 |
| Code display | The user's code, large with `letterSpacing: 4`; "loading" placeholder until ready | lines 146-148 |
| Helper copy | **"share this with friends each friend who logs meals unlocks 3 free premium days for both of you"** | line 150 |
| Share | WhatsApp deep link: `whatsapp://send?text=...`, message `"Join me on TrackKcal use my referral code ${referralCode} to get free extra entries"`; falls back to alert if WhatsApp absent | lines 92-99 |
| Copy | `expo-clipboard`, alert "Copied" | lines 83-90 |
| Premium Rewards card | Shows `+{totalEarnedEntriesFromReferrals} Days` | lines 176-189 |
| History table | Columns "Friend" / "Days"; per-row entries = sum of `entriesAwarded` for rewards whose `relatedRedemptionId` matches | lines 67-81, 218-227 |

#### Reward semantics — critical divergence

The reward is stored and surfaced inconsistently across the codebase. **An LLM extending this must resolve this before relying on it.**

| Layer | What it says the reward is |
|---|---|
| `referralService.ts` / `ReferralReward.entriesAwarded` | **+10 "entries"** (free entries) |
| Reward push + in-app alert | "You earned +10 free entries!" (`notificationService.ts` line 239, `HomeScreen.tsx` lines 1587, 2052) |
| `ReferralScreen` copy + Premium Rewards card | **"3 free premium days"** / `+N Days` |
| Docs (`TrackKCal-Complete-Documentation.md` line 751, `app-features.md` line 78) | "you earn 3 free premium days" / "3 free premium days per referral" |

The stored value is `10` regardless. The screen relabels the same `entriesAwarded` sum as "Days." **There is no code that converts a referral reward into actual premium time** (`premiumUntil` is never written by the referral flow), and there is no enforced "free entry" quota the +10 decrements against (`canAddEntry()` in `HomeScreen.tsx` line 1421-1423 currently just `return true`, with a TODO to re-enable the daily limit before launch). So today the referral reward is **a tracked number with no functional payout**. This is unfinished, not intentional.

### Account wall

Component `src/components/AccountWallModal.tsx`, triggered from `HomeScreen.tsx`.

#### When it appears

In `incrementEntryCount` (`HomeScreen.tsx` lines 1403-1419), after persisting the new count:

```
if (next >= 5 && next % 5 === 0 && !accountInfo?.email) {
  setTimeout(() => setShowAccountWall(true), 800);
}
```

| Property | Value |
|---|---|
| First trigger | At the **5th** log |
| Cadence | Every **5th** log thereafter (5, 10, 15, ...) — `next % 5 === 0` |
| Audience | Only accountless users (`!accountInfo?.email`) |
| Delay | 800 ms after the log |
| Dismissible | Yes. It is **not** a hard wall despite the doc label "Mandatory sign-up." `onDismiss` closes it (`X` button), so a user can keep logging and will be re-prompted at the next multiple of 5. |

#### Copy and content (`AccountWallModal.tsx`)

| Element | Text |
|---|---|
| Headline | `You've logged {logCount} times!` (logCount = current entry count) |
| Subhead | "Create an account to keep your data safe and unlock all features" |
| Benefit 1 (cloud) | "Your data backed up securely" |
| Benefit 2 (smartphone) | "Access from any device" |
| Benefit 3 (zap) | "Unlock the AI Nutritionist & insights" |
| Google button | "Sign in with Google — coming soon" — disabled, opacity 0.5 (placeholder) |
| Apple button | "Sign in with Apple — coming soon" — disabled, opacity 0.5 (placeholder) |
| Primary CTA | "Continue with email" → opens AccountScreen in `'signup'` mode, sets `accountFromWall` so Back returns Home (`HomeScreen.tsx` lines 2460-2467) |

OAuth buttons are visual placeholders only; **email is the sole working path**. Accent color is hardcoded `#3B82F6`.

### First-log nudge

A separate, gentler one-time encouragement, distinct from the account wall.

| Property | Value | Source |
|---|---|---|
| Trigger | On the user's **first log ever** (`setShowFirstLogMessage(true)`) | `HomeScreen.tsx` lines 1545-1547, 2015-2017 |
| Copy | `"Most people improve simply by paying attention."` (rendered as a centered quote in a tinted card) | line 2829 |
| Auto-hide | Disappears after **6000 ms** (`setTimeout(... 6000)`) | lines 268-274 |
| Re-show guard | Comment at lines 2042 notes a prior bug where the banner re-showed on every photo; it is intended to be one-time | — |

### Known divergences and gaps (for anyone extending this)

1. **Duplicate freeze logic.** `checkMissedDaysAndFreeze` exists twice: `HomeScreen.tsx` (premium-gated, sets `justFrozeToday`) and `streakLogic.ts` (no premium gate, used via `UserContext`). They can disagree on whether a non-premium user's streak is frozen. Consolidate to one source.
2. **"Premium" freeze gate vs FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH.** The HomeScreen gate checks raw `plan === 'premium'`, not the canonical `isPremium`/`FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` check. During launch every signed-in user is premium via the flag, but the freeze gate does not honor it — a signed-in launch user on the `free` plan would not get auto-freezes from the HomeScreen path.
3. **Referral reward has no payout.** As above: +10 is recorded, relabeled "days" in the UI, but never converts to `premiumUntil` or decrements any entry quota. Pick one model (entries or premium days) and wire it end to end.
4. **No streak reminder.** Despite streaks being the core retention loop, nothing notifies a user that their streak is at risk today. This is the single highest-leverage missing growth mechanic in this section.
5. **Push is local-only.** `sendReferralRewardNotification` schedules a **local** notification on the device that ran the meal-log loop (the referee's device), not a real push to the referrer. The referrer is not actually notified cross-device (comment at `notificationService.ts` lines 222-234 acknowledges this needs a backend).

---

## 14. Notifications and Reminders

### Overview

TrackKcal runs two independent notification systems:

1. **Local scheduled reminders** (`smartReminderService.ts`) — on-device `expo-notifications` that fire on a per-day schedule. No server. These are the meal nudges, macro pacing nudge, and end-of-day summary.
2. **Remote push broadcasts** (`notificationService.ts`) — Expo Push API broadcasts sent from a hidden admin console to every registered device token.

Notification behavior is configured globally at import time in `notificationService.ts` via `Notifications.setNotificationHandler`:

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| `shouldPlaySound` | `true` |
| `shouldSetBadge` | `false` |
| `shouldShowBanner` | `true` |
| `shouldShowList` | `true` |

On Android, a notification channel `default` is created on registration with `importance: AndroidImportance.MAX`, `vibrationPattern: [0, 250, 250, 250]`, `lightColor: '#00FFEC'`.

> Note: streak reminders, insight-unlock notifications, and a coach-unlock notification were requested for this section but do **not** exist as distinct notification code paths in the repo. The only scheduled local notifications are the meal-slot reminders, the macro pacing nudge, and the end-of-day summary defined in `smartReminderService.ts`. The only other one-shot local notification is the referral reward placeholder in `notificationService.ts` (`sendReferralRewardNotification`). No code schedules notifications keyed on streaks, insight unlocks, or coach unlocks. Treat their absence as a real gap, not an omission in this doc.

### Smart reminders (`smartReminderService.ts`)

#### Entry point and lifecycle

`smartReminderService.scheduleAllReminders()` is the single entry point. It is meant to run on every app open / foreground. On each run it:

1. Computes the premium flag self-contained (no closure): `isPremium = !!accountInfo?.email && (FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH || isPlanPremium(plan, accountInfo?.premiumUntil))`. This matches the architectural rule: premium requires email AND (launch flag OR a premium plan).
2. Loads preferences. If `reminderPrefs.enabled` is false OR `prefs.notificationsEnabled` is false, it cancels all reminders and returns `[]`. Both the global notifications toggle and the reminders toggle must be on.
3. Cancels the previous batch (`cancelAllSmartReminders`), then recomputes patterns and schedules a fresh batch for the rest of today only. All triggers are absolute `Date` objects set on the current day; nothing recurs.

Cancellation reads the persisted log of scheduled reminders (`@trackkal:smartReminderLog`), calls `Notifications.cancelScheduledNotificationAsync(id)` for each, swallows per-id errors (already fired/dismissed), then removes the log key.

#### Storage keys

| Key | Holds |
|---|---|
| `@trackkal:smartReminderCache` | `ReminderPatternCache` (computed meal-timing patterns + daily averages) |
| `@trackkal:smartReminderLog` | `ScheduledReminder[]` for the current day's batch (used for cancel + effectiveness) |
| `@trackkal:smartReminderEffectiveness` | `EffectivenessRecord[]`, capped at the last 100 |

#### Default preferences

`DEFAULT_PREFERENCES` (used when none saved):

| Field | Default |
|---|---|
| `enabled` | `true` |
| `reminderMode` | `'smart'` |
| `smartRemindersEnabled` | `true` |
| `mealSlots` | `{ breakfast: true, lunch: true, dinner: true }` |
| `endOfDaySummary` | `true` |
| `quietHoursStart` | `22` (10 PM) |
| `quietHoursEnd` | `7` (7 AM) |

#### Meal-slot classification

A meal's hour maps to a slot (`classifyMealSlot`):

| Hour range | Slot |
|---|---|
| 5–10 | `breakfast` |
| 11–14 | `lunch` |
| 15–20 | `dinner` |
| all others (21–4) | `snack` |

#### Pattern analysis (how reminder times are chosen)

`computeMealTimingPatterns(lookbackDays = 14)` walks the previous 14 days (days `i = 1..14`, today excluded). For each day it pulls `dataStorage.getDailyLog(dateKey)` and bins each meal by `minutesSinceMidnight = hour*60 + minute` into its slot. It also accumulates daily calories/protein/carbs/fat from `loadDailySummaries()` to compute averages.

A slot produces a `MealTimingPattern` only if it has **at least 3 samples** (`times.length >= 3`). For qualifying slots it computes:

- `averageHour = floor(avg / 60)`, `averageMinute = round(avg % 60)` where `avg` is the mean of `minutesSinceMidnight`.
- `stdDevMinutes = round(sqrt(variance))` (population variance over the samples).
- `sampleSize = times.length`.

The cache also stores `averageDailyProtein/Calories/Carbs/Fat` (rounded means over days with data) and `typicalMealCount` (total binned meals / days with data, rounded). The cache is written to `@trackkal:smartReminderCache` and returned. If computation throws, an empty cache is used.

#### Mode resolution (smart vs scheduled)

Per meal slot the effective mode is:

```
mode = reminderPrefs.reminderMode ?? (reminderPrefs.smartRemindersEnabled ? 'smart' : 'scheduled')
useSmart = mode === 'smart' && isPremium && pattern && pattern.stdDevMinutes < 60
```

So **smart timing requires all of**: mode is `smart`, the user is premium, a pattern exists for that slot (≥3 samples), AND the slot's `stdDevMinutes < 60`. Otherwise the slot falls back to scheduled (fixed-time) behavior.

#### Per-slot scheduling rules

Loops over `['breakfast', 'lunch', 'dinner']`. A slot is skipped entirely if:

- its `mealSlots[slot]` toggle is off, OR
- it was already logged today (`loggedSlots.has(slot)` — derived from today's meals via `getLoggedSlotsToday`).

Time selection:

| Branch | Hour / minute chosen | Content source | `isPremium` flag on record | Record `type` |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Smart** (`useSmart`) | `(averageHour*60 + averageMinute) − 10` minutes, clamped to ≥ 0. Fires **10 minutes before** the detected average meal time. | `generateReminderContent` with the pattern (personalized) | `true` | `meal_timing` |
| **Scheduled** | `prefs.mealReminders[slot].hour/minute`, else defaults: breakfast **08:00**, lunch **12:30**, dinner **18:00** | `generateReminderContent` with no pattern (generic) | `false` | `generic_meal` |

In scheduled mode, if `mealReminders[slot].enabled === false` the slot is skipped (respects the per-meal toggle from Settings). Scheduled-mode default minute is 30 only for lunch, 0 otherwise.

A scheduled reminder is then dropped if either:

- its hour is within quiet hours (`isWithinQuietHours(scheduleHour, quietStart, quietEnd)`), OR
- the computed trigger `Date` for today is `<= now` (in the past).

The notification id is `smart_<slot>_<generateId()>`, data payload `{ type: 'smart_reminder', reminderId, mealSlot: slot }`.

#### Quiet hours

`isWithinQuietHours(hour, quietStart, quietEnd)` returns true if `hour >= quietStart || hour < quietEnd`. With defaults (22→7) any reminder hour in 22,23,0–6 is suppressed. Note: both the wrap and non-wrap branches use the same expression, so a non-wrapping window (e.g. start ≤ end) is not handled distinctly — it still evaluates `hour >= start || hour < end`.

#### Macro pacing nudge (premium only, 3:30 PM)

Scheduled only if `isPremium && reminderPrefs.smartRemindersEnabled && goals`. Trigger fixed at **15:30** today, and only if `15:30 > now` and hour 15 is not in quiet hours.

Content from `generateMacroPacingContent` (returns `null` if no actionable nudge, in which case nothing is scheduled). Logic, in order:

| Condition (evaluated against today's running totals) | Title | Body |
|---|---|---|
| `proteinTarget > 0` AND protein remaining ratio `(proteinTarget − currentProtein)/proteinTarget > 0.6` (more than 60% of protein still to go) | `Protein check` | `You're at {round(currentProtein)}g protein with dinner left. Maybe something protein-heavy tonight?` |
| else `calorieTarget > 0` AND `currentCalories/calorieTarget > 0.8` (over 80% of calories used) | `Calorie heads up` | `You've used {round(ratio*100)}% of your daily calories. {round(target−current)} cal left for the rest of the day.` |
| else | — | returns `null`, no notification |

Returns `null` immediately if both `proteinTarget <= 0` and `calorieTarget <= 0`. Record `type: 'macro_pacing'`, `isPremium: true`. Id `smart_macro_<generateId()>`.

#### End-of-day summary (8:30 PM)

Scheduled if `reminderPrefs.endOfDaySummary && goals`, trigger fixed at **20:30** today, only if `20:30 > now` and hour 20 is not in quiet hours. Premium gets personalized numbers; free/no-goal gets generic copy.

| Case | Title | Body |
|---|---|---|
| Not premium OR `goals.calories <= 0` | `End of day` | `Have you logged all your meals today?` |
| Premium, `remaining > 0` | `Daily wrap-up` | `You've logged {currentCalories} of {goals.calories} cal today. {remaining} cal remaining.` |
| Premium, `remaining <= 0` | `Daily wrap-up` | `You've hit your {goals.calories} cal target for today. Nice work!` |

`remaining = round(goals.calories − currentCalories)`. Record `type: 'end_of_day'`, `isPremium` mirrors the user's premium flag. Id `smart_eod_<generateId()>`.

#### Personalized meal content (`generateReminderContent`)

Free or missing pattern → static `GENERIC_MESSAGES` (falls back to the lunch message if slot unknown):

| Slot | Title | Body |
|---|---|---|
| breakfast | `Good morning!` | `Don't forget to log your breakfast!` |
| lunch | `Lunchtime!` | `Time to log your lunch!` |
| dinner | `Dinner time!` | `Don't forget to log your dinner!` |

Premium with a pattern:

| Pattern condition | Title | Body |
|---|---|---|
| `stdDevMinutes < 30` (very consistent) | `{Slot} time?` | `You usually eat {slot} around {h:mm AM/PM}. Everything ok?` |
| `stdDevMinutes >= 30` (still < 60 to reach here) | `{Slot} time?` | `Around this time you often have {slot}. Don't forget to log it!` |

#### Effectiveness tracking

Records use shape `{ reminderId, firedAt, wasOpened, mealLoggedWithin30Min }`, persisted to `@trackkal:smartReminderEffectiveness`, trimmed to the last 100 on save.

- `recordReminderOpened(reminderId)` — call when the user taps a smart-reminder notification. Sets `wasOpened = true` (creating a record if needed) and fires `analyticsService.trackSmartReminderOpened()`.
- `checkMealLoggedAfterReminder()` — call after every meal save. For each reminder in the day's log whose `scheduledFor` has passed and is within the last **30 minutes** (`30 * 60 * 1000` ms), it marks `mealLoggedWithin30Min = true`. If any effective records exist it fires `analyticsService.trackSmartReminderEffective()`.
- On scheduling, if any reminders were scheduled, `analyticsService.trackSmartReminderScheduled(count)` fires.

So the effectiveness signal is binary per reminder: opened (tapped) and/or meal-logged-within-30-min. There is no time-decay model or auto-tuning of future reminder times from effectiveness data; patterns drive timing, effectiveness is analytics-only.

#### Free vs premium summary (smart reminders)

| Capability | Free | Premium |
|---|---|---|
| Global notifications + reminders toggles | Yes | Yes |
| Scheduled-mode meal reminders at user-picked times | Yes | Yes |
| Smart timing (10 min before learned average) | No (falls back to scheduled even if mode = smart) | Yes (needs pattern, `stdDev < 60`) |
| Personalized meal copy (uses learned time) | No (generic) | Yes |
| Macro pacing nudge (3:30 PM) | No | Yes |
| End-of-day summary | Yes (generic copy) | Yes (personalized numbers) |

Premium is gated by the same `isPremium` rule above; under `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH`, every signed-in user with an email is treated as premium, so all of the above is effectively on for signed-in launch users.

### NotificationSettingsScreen controls

Loads `Preferences` from `dataStorage.loadPreferences()`. Saves immediately on every toggle (local-first, no confirm). Controls:

| Section | Control | Backed by | Default |
|---|---|---|---|
| General | **Allow Notifications** switch | `preferences.notificationsEnabled` | `true` |
| Reminders | **Reminders** master switch (subtitle: `Smart timing` / `At set times` / `Off`) | `smartReminderPreferences.enabled` | `true` |
| Reminders | **Smart / Scheduled** segmented toggle | `smartReminderPreferences.reminderMode` | `'smart'` |
| Reminders (scheduled mode only) | **Breakfast / Lunch / Dinner** rows: per-meal enable switch + tap-to-set time via `TimePickerModal` | `preferences.mealReminders[meal].{enabled,hour,minute}` | breakfast 08:00, lunch 12:30, dinner 18:00 |
| Reminders | **End-of-Day Summary** switch (subtitle: `Get a daily nutrition wrap-up at 8:30 PM`) | `smartReminderPreferences.endOfDaySummary` | `true` |

Behavior details:

- The entire Reminders section is hidden when `notificationsEnabled` is false.
- The Smart/Scheduled toggle and meal rows are hidden when `smartPrefs.enabled` is false.
- The three meal time rows render only in `scheduled` mode. In smart mode they are hidden because times are learned, not picked.
- Helper copy under the toggle: smart → "TrackKcal learns when you typically eat and nudges you at the right time. Needs a few days of logging to calibrate." scheduled → "Reminders fire at the times you pick below."
- Tapping a meal row only opens the time picker if that meal's `enabled` is true.
- `reminderMode` falls back to `'smart'` for any user upgrading from a build that lacked the field.
- This screen does **not** call `scheduleAllReminders()` itself; it only persists preferences. Rescheduling happens on the next app open/foreground that invokes the service. Quiet hours (`quietHoursStart`/`End`) are stored in `SmartReminderPreferences` but have **no UI control** on this screen; they only ever take their defaults (22→7) unless set elsewhere.

### Push notifications (remote broadcasts)

#### Registration (`notificationService.registerDeviceAsync`)

| Step | Behavior |
|---|---|
| Physical device check | If `!Device.isDevice`, returns `{ status: 'not_physical' }`. Push does not work on most simulators. |
| Permission | Reads existing permission; if not `granted`, calls `requestPermissionsAsync()`. If still not granted, returns `{ status: 'denied' }`. |
| Project id | Resolved from `expoConfig.extra.eas.projectId` → `easConfig.projectId` → legacy `manifest`/`manifest2`. If missing, returns `{ status: 'error', error: 'Missing projectId in Expo config' }` and skips registration. |
| Token | `getExpoPushTokenAsync({ projectId })`. On success, `dataStorage.addPushToken(token)` persists it locally. |
| Android channel | Creates the `default` channel (see Overview). |
| Result | `{ status: 'granted', token }`. |

Tokens are stored locally via `dataStorage.addPushToken` / read with `loadPushTokens`. Broadcasts target the locally stored token list — there is no server-side email→token mapping. (`sendReferralRewardNotification` explicitly notes this is a placeholder; in production a backend would map emails to tokens.)

#### Broadcast send (`sendBroadcastPush(title, body)`)

- Loads all stored tokens. If none, alerts "No Registered Devices" and returns zeroed result.
- Generates `broadcastId = broadcast_<Date.now()>_<random base36>`.
- Loops tokens, POSTing each individually to the Expo push endpoint `https://exp.host/--/api/v2/push/send` via `sendPushToToken`. Payload: `{ to, sound: 'default', title, body, data: { sentAt, broadcastId } }`.
- A token counts as a failure if the HTTP response is not ok OR the Expo response body has `data.status === 'error'`.
- Writes a `PushBroadcastRecord` to history `{ id, title, message, timestamp, targetCount, successCount, failureCount, clickCount: 0 }` via `dataStorage.addPushHistoryRecord`.
- Alerts a completion summary (success count, and failure count if any).
- `recordPushClick(broadcastId)` increments `clickCount` on the matching history record (no-op on empty id).

#### Referral reward notification (`sendReferralRewardNotification`)

Placeholder. Schedules an **immediate local** notification (`trigger: null`) rather than a real targeted push: title `🎉 Referral Reward Earned!`, body `{refereeName} completed 5 meals! You earned +10 free entries.`, data `{ type: 'referral_reward' }`. Not wired to a per-user push path.

### AdminPushScreen (hidden push console)

A hidden internal screen for the team to send manual broadcasts. Reveal: open the sidebar and tap the "Menu" title **five times**.

Contents:

| Card | What it shows / does |
|---|---|
| Manual Push Broadcast | Title + multiline Message inputs (placeholders `Subscription reminder` / `We added new premium recipes. Tap to explore!`). "Send Push" requires both fields non-empty, else alerts "Missing fields". On send, calls `sendBroadcastPush`, then shows a summary line (`Targeted N · Delivered to M · failures`) with a check or alert-triangle icon, plus an error line if any failed. |
| Registered Devices | Lists every stored push token, or a hint to install on a physical device and accept permissions if none. |
| Delivery History | Per broadcast: title, timestamp (`MMM d, yyyy · h:mm a`), message, and stat chips: **Targets**, **Sent** (success), **Failed**, **Clicks**. |
| How to Test | Static checklist: physical device required, accept permission on first launch, tap "Menu" title five times, send and observe device notification center + Metro logs. |

There is no audience targeting, scheduling, segmentation, or premium/free filtering in the admin console — every broadcast goes to all locally stored tokens. Click attribution depends on the app calling `recordPushClick(broadcastId)` when a push with that `broadcastId` is opened.

### Gaps and blast radius (notifications)

- **No streak / insight-unlock / coach-unlock notifications exist.** If the product spec promises these, they are unbuilt. Adding them would go through `Notifications.scheduleNotificationAsync` (local) and likely a new record type analogous to the smart-reminder records.
- **Reschedule timing is implicit.** Reminders only re-schedule on app open/foreground when something calls `scheduleAllReminders()`. A user who never opens the app gets no reminders for that day, and changing a setting does nothing until the next foreground.
- **All triggers are same-day absolute dates.** Nothing recurs natively; the system relies on the app being opened to repopulate tomorrow. Backgrounded-only users can miss notifications.
- **Quiet hours have no UI.** Stored but unsettable on the settings screen; only defaults apply.
- **Push is fan-out-from-device.** `sendBroadcastPush` iterates tokens client-side with no batching/throttling and no server. Large token lists mean many sequential fetches from whatever device runs the admin console. There is no real targeted/per-user push.
- **Effectiveness data is analytics-only.** It is recorded and capped at 100 records but never feeds back into timing decisions.

I read `smartReminderService.ts`, `notificationService.ts`, `NotificationSettingsScreen.tsx`, and `AdminPushScreen.tsx` in full. The streak/insight-unlock/coach-unlock notifications named in the assignment do not exist as code; I documented that explicitly rather than inventing them.

---

## 15. Data Model, Storage, Sync and Offline

TrackKcal is **local-first**: AsyncStorage is the source of truth and returns immediately on every write; Supabase syncs in the background and never blocks UX. On conflict, **local wins** for settings/derived state and **newer-wins** (by `updatedAt` timestamp) for meals, weights, and summaries. Source files: `src/services/dataStorage.ts` (~3,800 lines, the local + sync layer), `src/services/supabaseDataService.ts` (the Supabase mapping layer), `src/services/realtimeMealsService.ts` (the realtime subscription), and the SQL in `docs/supabase-schema.sql` / `docs/supabase-rls-policies.sql`.

### AsyncStorage keys

All keys are namespaced `@trackkal:` (note: `trackkal`, not `trackkcal`). Defined in the `STORAGE_KEYS` object in `dataStorage.ts`.

| Key | Constant | Shape | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `@trackkal:goals` | `GOALS` | `ExtendedGoalData` | Active nutrition goal + profile snapshot. |
| `@trackkal:meals` | `MEALS` | `Record<date, MealEntry[]>` | **Legacy** single blob. Migrated to per-day shards on first read, then removed. |
| `@trackkal:log:<YYYY-MM-DD>` | `dailyLog(date)` | `MealEntry[]` | Day-sharded food log. One key per logged day. The live store of meals. |
| `@trackkal:exercises` | `EXERCISES` | `Record<date, ExerciseEntry[]>` | Single blob (not sharded). |
| `@trackkal:weightEntries` | `WEIGHT_ENTRIES` | `WeightEntry[]` | Flat array, normalized (id, ISO date, kg, updatedAt). |
| `@trackkal:summaries` | `SUMMARIES` | `Record<date, DailySummary>` | Per-day rollups. Recomputed on every meal write. |
| `@trackkal:entryCount` | `ENTRY_COUNT` | `string` (int) | Free-tier entry usage counter. |
| `@trackkal:userPlan` | `USER_PLAN` | `'free' \| 'premium'` | Plan string only; not the entitlement gate. |
| `@trackkal:deviceInfo` | `DEVICE_INFO` | `any` (json) | Device metadata. |
| `@trackkal:accountInfo` | `ACCOUNT_INFO` | `AccountInfo` | Identity cache: email, `supabaseUserId` (auth.uid), `appUserId`. |
| `@trackkal:preferences` | `PREFERENCES` | `Preferences` | Units, notifications, meal reminders, dynamic adjustment, smart reminders. |
| `@trackkal:pushTokens` | `PUSH_TOKENS` | `string[]` | Expo push tokens. |
| `@trackkal:pushHistory` | `PUSH_HISTORY` | `PushBroadcastRecord[]` | Broadcast records. |
| `@trackkal:referralCodes` | `REFERRAL_CODES` | `ReferralCode[]` | Local cache; codes are global in Supabase. |
| `@trackkal:referralRedemptions` | `REFERRAL_REDEMPTIONS` | `ReferralRedemption[]` | |
| `@trackkal:referralRewards` | `REFERRAL_REWARDS` | `ReferralReward[]` | |
| `@trackkal:savedPrompts` | `SAVED_PROMPTS` | `SavedPrompt[]` | |
| `@trackkal:entryTasks` | `ENTRY_TASKS` | `EntryTasksStatus` | customPlan + registration completion (5 bonus entries each). |
| `@trackkal:syncQueue` | `SYNC_QUEUE` | `SyncOperation[]` | Offline write queue (see Sync engine). |
| `@trackkal:streakFreeze` | `STREAK_FREEZE` | `StreakFreezeData` | 0–2 freezes/month + used dates. |
| `@trackkal:adjustmentHistory` | `ADJUSTMENT_HISTORY` | `AdjustmentRecord[]` | Dynamic calorie adjustment log. Local only (no Supabase sync). |
| `@trackkal:analyticsFeedback` | `ANALYTICS_FEEDBACK` | `AnalyticsFeedback[]` | Local only. |
| `@trackkal:detectedPatterns` | `DETECTED_PATTERNS` | `DetectedPattern[]` | **Premium.** |
| `@trackkal:weeklyActionPlan` | `WEEKLY_ACTION_PLAN` | `WeeklyActionPlan` | **Premium.** Single plan per user. |
| `@trackkal:userMetricsSnapshot` | `USER_METRICS_SNAPSHOT` | `UserMetricsSnapshot` | Generated rollup for AI prompts. Local only. |
| `@trackkal:insights` | `INSIGHTS` | `Insight[]` | Generated insight objects. |
| `@trackkal:coachDismissDate` | `COACH_DISMISS_DATE` | `string` | Coach card dismissal date. |
| `@trackkal:smartReminderCache` | `SMART_REMINDER_CACHE` | `ReminderPatternCache` | Computed meal-timing patterns. |
| `@trackkal:smartReminderLog` | `SMART_REMINDER_LOG` | log | Fired reminders. |
| `@trackkal:smartReminderEffectiveness` | `SMART_REMINDER_EFFECTIVENESS` | metrics | |
| `@trackkal:groceryUnlocked` | `GROCERY_UNLOCKED` | `'true'` | Grocery suggestions unlock flag. |
| `@trackkal:groceryUnlockSeen` | `GROCERY_UNLOCK_SEEN` | `'true'` | Whether the unlock toast was shown. |
| `@trackkal:insightUnlocks` | `INSIGHT_UNLOCKS` | `Record<insightId, {unlockedAt; seenAt?}>` | Drives every insight unlock gate. |
| `@trackkal:calorieBankConfig` | `CALORIE_BANK_CONFIG` | `CalorieBankConfig` | **Premium.** Seed-only from remote (never overwritten). |
| `@trackkal:calorieBankCompletedCycles` | `CALORIE_BANK_COMPLETED_CYCLES` | `CalorieBankCompletedCycle[]` | **Premium.** Trimmed to the last **52** cycles (1 year). |
| `@trackkal:calorieBankCycleResetSeen` | `CALORIE_BANK_CYCLE_RESET_SEEN` | `string` (cycle start date) | Suppresses the reset modal once seen. |
| `@trackkal:lastMealsSyncAt` | `LAST_MEALS_SYNC_AT` | `string` (epoch ms) | Watermark distinguishing "pending local meal" from "deleted on remote." |

There is no key for `pushHistory` sync state, no separate `exercises` shard (exercises remain a single blob), and adjustment history / analytics feedback / the metrics snapshot are **local-only** (never sent to Supabase).

### Day-sharded daily logs

Meals are stored one AsyncStorage key per day: `@trackkal:log:YYYY-MM-DD` → `MealEntry[]`. This avoids rewriting the entire meal history on every save.

`MealEntry`:

| Field | Type | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `id` | `string` | UUID. `ensureUUID` upgrades legacy ids on read. Used as the Supabase primary key. |
| `prompt` | `string` | Raw user text. |
| `summary?` | `string` | AI meal summary. |
| `foods` | `ParsedFood[]` | Per-food macros + micros. |
| `timestamp` | `number` | Epoch ms. Drives `logged_date` and sort order. |
| `imageUri?` | `string` | Local photo URI. |
| `updatedAt?` | `string` | ISO. The conflict-resolution clock for meals. |
| `date?` | `string` | Optional redundant date key. |
| `userId?` | `string` | Optional. |
| `isLoading?` / `loadingState?` | `boolean` / `'analyzing'\|'done'\|'failed'` | **In-memory only.** `saveDailyLog` filters out any meal with `isLoading` or `loadingState==='analyzing'` so a stuck "calculating" skeleton can never be persisted. |

Key sharding methods (`dataStorage`): `getDailyLog(date)`, `saveDailyLog(date, meals)`, `saveMeal(date, meal)` (append one), `deleteDailyLog(date)`, `saveMeals(byDate)` (batched wrapper), `loadMeals()` (reconstructs the full blob — expensive). `migrateLegacyMealsToShards()` splits the legacy `@trackkal:meals` blob into shards then deletes it.

`loadMeals()` is **in-memory cached for 10,000 ms** (`MEALS_CACHE_TTL_MS = 10_000`) and dedupes concurrent calls via a shared `mealsLoadPromise`. The cache is invalidated by `invalidateMealsCache()` on every meal write and by the realtime subscription. Per-key write serialization uses `withWriteLock(key, fn)` — a per-key promise chain so read-modify-write on the same shard (or the `summaries` / `syncQueue` blob) never interleaves.

### Daily summaries

`DailySummary` (per day, recomputed by `recalculateDailySummary` on every meal write, then `updateSummaryForDate` writes the `@trackkal:summaries` blob under the `summaries` write lock):

| Field | Type | Rounding |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `date` | `YYYY-MM-DD` | — |
| `totalCalories` | number | round0 |
| `totalProtein` / `totalCarbs` / `totalFat` | number | round1 |
| `entryCount` | number (meal count) | — |
| `updatedAt` | ISO | — |
| `totalFiber`, `totalSugar`, `totalAddedSugars`, `totalSaturatedFat` | number? | round1 |
| `totalSodium`, `totalPotassium`, `totalCholesterol`, `totalCalcium`, `totalMagnesium`, `totalVitaminA` | number? | round0 |
| `totalIron`, `totalZinc`, `totalOmega3`, `totalVitaminC`, `totalVitaminD`, `totalVitaminB12` | number? | round1 |

Micros are optional (older summaries lack them). `migrateMealsToSummaries()` backfills summaries for all logged days when none exist. Summaries feed the streak engine (`calculateStreak(summaries, freezeUsedDates)`), the consistency score, and the metrics snapshot.

### UserMetricsSnapshot (every field)

Generated by `generateUserMetricsSnapshot()` and stored at `@trackkal:userMetricsSnapshot`. Local only; built for the AI prompts. Requires goals to exist (returns `null` otherwise).

| Field | Type | Derivation |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `generatedAt` | ISO | now |
| `userGoals.calories/protein/carbs/fat/goalType` | numbers + string | from active goals |
| `averages7Day.calories/protein/carbs/fat` | number | mean over **logged** days in last 7 (divides by `dayCount`, the count of days with `entryCount>0`, not by 7) |
| `averages7Day.*` micros | number | `dietary_fiber, sugar, added_sugars, sugar_alcohols, net_carbs, saturated_fat, trans_fat, polyunsaturated_fat, monounsaturated_fat, sodium, potassium, cholesterol, calcium, iron, vitamin_a, vitamin_c, vitamin_d, vitamin_e, vitamin_k, vitamin_b12` — averaged over the last 7 logged days |
| `weightTrend.current` | number\|null | newest weight |
| `weightTrend.startOfPeriod` | number\|null | weight ≥14 days ago, else oldest |
| `weightTrend.change` | number\|null | current − start |
| `weightTrend.periodDays` | number | ~14 |
| `consistencyScore` | 0–100 | `round((consistentDays / max(1, dayCount)) * 100)`; a day is "consistent" if `abs(totalCalories − goal) / goal ≤ 0.15` (within **15%**) |
| `currentStreak` | number | streak engine |
| `weakNutrients` | `string[]` | e.g. `['protein','fiber']` |
| `commonFoods[]` | `{name, frequency, avgP, avgC, avgF, avgKcal}` | top 10 over a **30-day** scan window |
| `recentDailySummaries` | `DailySummary[]` | last 7 days |
| `loggedDaysCount` | number | count of dates with ≥1 meal (from `loadMeals`) |

### Goals, preferences, weight

`ExtendedGoalData` (key `@trackkal:goals`): `calories`, `proteinPercentage/carbsPercentage/fatPercentage`, `proteinGrams/carbsGrams/fatGrams`, `currentWeightKg`, `targetWeightKg`, `age?`, `gender?` (`male|female|prefer_not_to_say`), `heightCm?/heightFeet?/heightInches?`, `goal?` (`lose|maintain|gain`), `activityRate?`, `name?`, `dob?`, `trackingGoal?`, `activityLevel?` (`sedentary|light|moderate|very`). Loaded local-first: if signed in and a local copy exists, **local wins every field and remote only fills gaps** (`{...remoteGoals, ...localGoals}`); remote seeds only when there is no local copy. Remote stores goals as history rows with `is_active` — saving deactivates prior active rows then inserts a new active one.

`Preferences` (key `@trackkal:preferences`): `weightUnit` (`kg|lbs`), `notificationsEnabled`, `mealReminders.{breakfast,lunch,dinner}.{enabled,hour,minute}`, `dynamicAdjustmentEnabled`, `dynamicAdjustmentThreshold` (% — defaults shown below), `lastAdjustmentWeight?`, `smartSuggestEnabled?`, `smartReminderPreferences?`. Defaults when absent: `weightUnit kg`, `notificationsEnabled true`, reminders breakfast 08:00 / lunch 13:00 / dinner 19:00 all disabled, `dynamicAdjustmentEnabled true`, `dynamicAdjustmentThreshold 2`. Loaded local-first: `{...defaults, ...(remotePrefs||{}), ...localPrefs}` so interactive toggles never snap back to the cloud copy. Note: only `weightUnit`, `notificationsEnabled`, and `mealReminders` round-trip to Supabase (`user_preferences`); `dynamicAdjustment*`, `smartSuggest`, and smart-reminder prefs are local-only on write.

`WeightEntry` (key `@trackkal:weightEntries`): `{ date: ISO, weight: kg, id?, updatedAt? }`. `normalizeWeightEntry` coerces `date` to ISO and defaults `id` to the ISO date. Merge is **newer-wins by `updatedAt`** (`mergeWeightEntries`). Clearing history (≤1 entry remaining) resets the dynamic-adjustment baseline.

### Calorie bank config and completed cycles (Premium)

`CalorieBankConfig` (key `@trackkal:calorieBankConfig`):

| Field | Type | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `enabled` | boolean | |
| `cycleStartDay` | `0..6` | 0=Sun … 6=Sat |
| `dailyCapPercent` | `15 \| 20 \| 25` | max % of base daily target bankable/day |
| `spendingCapPercent` | `15 \| 20 \| 25` | max % spendable over/day |
| `enabledDate` | ISO date | when first turned on |
| `pendingDailyCapPercent?` / `pendingSpendingCapPercent?` | `15\|20\|25` | cap changes apply from the **next cycle**, not retroactively |

Config is **seed-only** across devices: the cross-device pull writes the remote config to local *only* when no local config exists (fresh device / evicted cache); it never overwrites an existing local config (it has no `updatedAt` and is hand-toggled). Remotely it lives as a `calorie_bank_config` jsonb column on `user_settings`.

`CalorieBankCompletedCycle` (key `@trackkal:calorieBankCompletedCycles`, **trimmed to last 52**): `startDate`, `endDate`, `weeklyBudget`, `weeklyActual`, `bankUtilization` (%), `expiredCalories`, `daysLogged`, `daysInCycle` (7 or fewer for a partial first cycle), `peakBankBalance`, `capHitDays`, `spendCapHitDays`, `goalType` (`lose|gain|maintain`). Cross-device merge is union by `startDate`.

### Insight unlocks

Key `@trackkal:insightUnlocks` → `Record<insightId, { unlockedAt: ISO; seenAt?: ISO }>`. Read by `loadInsightUnlocks()`; `markInsightSeen(id)` stamps `seenAt`. Every insight card checks `isInsightUnlocked` first (`insightUnlockEngine.ts`); a new insight needs an entry there. Cross-device merge (`mergeUnlocks`) is **monotonic**: keep the **earliest** `unlockedAt` and **any** `seenAt` — an achievement, once unlocked or seen on any device, stays unlocked/seen.

### Supabase schema (`docs/supabase-schema.sql`)

`uuid-ossp` enabled; all PKs are `uuid default uuid_generate_v4()`. A shared `set_updated_at()` trigger stamps `updated_at = now()` on update for most tables.

| Table | Key columns | Soft-delete | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `app_users` | `id` (PK), `auth_user_id` unique, `email` unique, `display_name`, `phone_number`, timestamps | no | **The identity hub.** `food_logs.user_id` etc. reference `app_users.id`, NOT `auth.uid()`. |
| `food_logs` | `id`, `user_id`→app_users, `prompt`, `parsed_payload` jsonb, `logged_date` date, `total_calories/protein/carbs/fat` numeric, timestamps, `deleted_at` | **yes** | The full `MealEntry` is stored in `parsed_payload`. Totals are denormalized via `sumNutrient`. |
| `food_items` | `id`, `food_log_id`→food_logs, name/quantity/macros | no | Optional per-ingredient detail (not currently written by the client). |
| `exercise_logs` | `id`, `user_id`, `prompt`, `exercises_jsonb`, `description`, `duration_minutes`, `calories_burned`, `logged_date`, timestamps, `deleted_at` | **yes** | |
| `weight_entries` | `id`, `user_id`, `logged_date`, `weight_kg`, `notes`, timestamps, `deleted_at` | **yes** | |
| `nutrition_goals` | `id`, `user_id`, `calories_target`, `protein/carbs/fat_target`, profile cols (name, tracking_goal, age, gender, height_cm/feet/inches, current/target_weight_kg, body_goal, activity_rate, activity_level), `is_active` | no | History table; only one `is_active=true` row per user. |
| `engagement_tasks` | `id`, `code` unique, title, description, `reward_entries` | no | Shared reference data. |
| `user_task_status` | `id`, `user_id`, `task_id`, `completed`, unique(user_id, task_id) | no | |
| `push_tokens` | `id`, `user_id`, `expo_token`, `device_info` jsonb, `revoked_at` | revoke via `revoked_at` | unique on `expo_token` for upsert. |
| `push_history` | `id`, `user_id`, `push_token_id`, title, message, `timestamp`, target/success/failure/click counts, `clicked`, `clicked_at` | no | |
| `saved_prompts` | `id`, `user_id`, `prompt`, timestamps | no | |
| `user_preferences` | `id`, `user_id` **unique**, `weight_unit`, `notifications_enabled`, `meal_reminders` jsonb | no | Upsert on `user_id`. |
| `user_settings` | `id`, `user_id` **unique**, `entry_count`, `user_plan`, `device_info` jsonb, (+ `calorie_bank_config` jsonb, added by client upsert) | no | Upsert on `user_id`. |
| `entry_tasks` | `id`, `user_id` unique, `custom_plan_completed`, `registration_completed`, `completed_at` | no | |
| `referral_codes` | `id`, `user_id`, `code` unique, totals | no | Code stored UPPERCASE. |
| `referral_redemptions` | `id`, `referral_code`, `referrer_email`, `referee_email`, `referee_name`, `status`, `meals_logged`, `device_id`, `completed_at` | no | Emails lowercased; **no `user_id`** (keyed by email). |
| `referral_rewards` | `id`, `user_id`, `related_redemption_id`, `earned_at`, `entries_awarded`, `reason` | no | |
| `streak_freezes` | `id`, `user_id` unique, `freezes_available`, `last_reset_date`, `used_on_dates` jsonb | no | Upsert on `user_id`. |
| `grocery_items` | `id`, `user_id`, name, category, `is_checked` | no | |
| `analytics_events` | `id`, `user_id`, `event_name`, `properties` jsonb, `timestamp` | no | Insert-only. |
| `nutrition_library` | `id`, `name` unique, `*_per_100g`, `serving_size_g`, `source` | no | **Shared** (not per-user). Deterministic nutrition cache. |
| `daily_user_metrics` | `id`, `user_id`, `metric_date`, meals/exercise/calories logged, push received/clicked, `streak_active`, unique(user_id, metric_date) | no | Upsert on `user_id,metric_date`. |
| `waitlist` | `id`, `email` unique, `name`, `source` | no | Public insert (landing page). |

Tables the client writes via jsonb-payload upsert that are referenced by `supabaseDataService` but not in the base schema file (created out of band): `insights` (per-row, `payload` jsonb, conflict `id`), `detected_patterns` (one row/user, `payload.patterns`, conflict `user_id`), `weekly_action_plans` (one/user, conflict `user_id`), `insight_unlocks` (conflict `user_id,insight_id`), `daily_summaries` (conflict `user_id,summary_date`), `calorie_bank_completed_cycles` (conflict `id`).

### Row Level Security (`docs/supabase-rls-policies.sql`)

RLS is enabled on every table. The pivot is a `SECURITY DEFINER STABLE` helper:

```sql
CREATE FUNCTION my_app_user_id() RETURNS uuid AS $$
```
