```sql
  SELECT id FROM public.app_users WHERE auth_user_id = auth.uid() LIMIT 1;
$$ LANGUAGE sql SECURITY DEFINER STABLE;
```

| Table(s) | Policy shape |
| --- | --- |
| `app_users` | self only via `auth_user_id = auth.uid()` (select/insert/update/delete) |
| `food_logs`, `food_items` (via parent), `exercise_logs`, `weight_entries`, `nutrition_goals`, `saved_prompts`, `user_preferences`, `user_settings`, `entry_tasks`, `streak_freezes`, `grocery_items`, `analytics_events`, `daily_user_metrics`, `push_tokens`, `push_history`, `referral_rewards`, `user_task_status` | owner only via `user_id = my_app_user_id()` |
| `engagement_tasks`, `referral_codes` (SELECT), `nutrition_library`, `referral_redemptions` | readable/writable by any `auth.role()='authenticated'` user (shared/global data) |
| `referral_codes` (INSERT/UPDATE) | `user_id = my_app_user_id()` |
| `waitlist` | INSERT `WITH CHECK (true)` (anon allowed); SELECT authenticated only |

**The critical, non-obvious fact: `food_logs.user_id` (and all owner-scoped `user_id`s) equal `app_users.id`, not `auth.uid()`.** The link is `app_users.auth_user_id = auth.uid()`, resolved by `my_app_user_id()`. Every query in `supabaseDataService` first calls `getOrCreateUser()` to resolve the `app_users` row, then filters by `user.id`.

### Identity resolution (`getOrCreateUser`)

The session is the source of truth (`accountInfo` may be stale). Resolution order: (1) look up `app_users` by `auth_user_id = currentAuthUid`; (2) fall back to lookup by lowercased `email` (**orphan recovery** for rows whose auth link is missing/stale); (3) if found and stale, update display_name/phone/`auth_user_id`/email; (4) if not found, **upsert on `email`** (`onConflict: 'email'`) to win races where a SELECT missed an existing row instead of failing the unique-email constraint. Emails are always `.trim().toLowerCase()`d.

### Sync engine

**Write path.** Every domain write follows: write AsyncStorage → return → fire-and-forget background sync. If signed in (`accountInfo.supabaseUserId`), call the direct `supabaseDataService` upsert; on failure, `enqueueSyncOperation`. If signed out (no `supabaseUserId` and no `email`), enqueue immediately so it flushes after the next sign-in.

**Sync queue** (`@trackkal:syncQueue`, a `SyncOperation[]`). All read-modify-write goes through `withWriteLock('syncQueue', …)` so enqueue and flush never interleave. `SyncOperation` is a discriminated union over `entity` × `action`:

| entity | actions |
| --- | --- |
| `meal` | upsert, delete |
| `weight` | upsert, delete |
| `goals` | upsert |
| `exercise` | upsert, delete |
| `push_token` | upsert, revoke |
| `push_history` | upsert, update_click |
| `saved_prompt` | upsert, delete |
| `preferences` | upsert |
| `settings` | upsert (entryCount / userPlan / deviceInfo) |
| `entry_tasks` | upsert |
| `referral_code` / `referral_redemption` / `referral_reward` | upsert |
| `streak_freeze` | upsert |
| `analytics_event` | log |

**Flush** (`processSyncQueue`) runs each op via `executeSyncOperation`. It does **not** abort the whole queue on one bad op (no head-of-line blocking): a failing op is retried in place, incrementing a hidden `_attempts`; after `MAX_SYNC_ATTEMPTS = 5` it is dropped with a `console.error`. An op for an unhandled entity throws (so it retries then drops) rather than being silently treated as synced. The queue is flushed from the AppState foreground hook and web `visibilitychange`, and opportunistically inside several `load*` functions.

**Sign-in reconciliation.** On the first `SIGNED_IN` of a session the auth listener runs, in order: `pushDerivedToSupabase()` (one-shot backfill — pushes every locally-cached meal shard, weights, insights, patterns, plan, unlocks, summaries, bank config, cycles, via `Promise.allSettled`), then `pullDerivedFromSupabase()`. The push runs first so the subsequent pull's union loses nothing.

### Conflict resolution (local-first)

`pullDerivedFromSupabase` merges **remote INTO local, local wins**:
- **Insights / patterns / completed cycles:** `unionById` (keyed by `id` / `id` / `startDate`) — local wins on key collision.
- **Daily summaries:** `mergeSummariesByDate` — newer (or tie) local `updatedAt` wins.
- **Weekly action plan:** newer `generatedAt` wins.
- **Insight unlocks:** `mergeUnlocks` — monotonic (earliest unlock, any seen).
- **Calorie bank config:** seed-only (write remote only if no local config).

**Meals** use a richer reconciliation in `_loadMealsInternal`. It unions local shards with `fetchMeals` (remote, `deleted_at IS NULL` only). For each meal:
- In **both** local and remote → keep the one with the newer `touch` (`max(timestamp, updatedAt)`).
- **Local-only and newer than `LAST_MEALS_SYNC_AT`** (or watermark is 0) → pending, keep it; hold the watermark back so a not-yet-synced meal is never dropped.
- **Local-only and older than the watermark** → previously synced, now absent from remote ⇒ deleted on another device ⇒ **drop it.**

After merge it persists changed shards under each day's write lock, re-reading inside the lock to preserve any meal saved during the network fetch. `LAST_MEALS_SYNC_AT` advances to `now()` unless a pending meal exists, in which case it is held at `minPendingTouch − 1`.

### Soft delete

Deletes are **never hard deletes** for synced entities. `deleteMeals` / `deleteWeightEntries` / `deleteExercises` set `deleted_at = now()` and fetches filter `.is('deleted_at', null)`. Critically, upsert row builders (`mealPayloadToRow`, the exercise row builder) **omit `deleted_at` entirely** — sending `deleted_at: null` on a full-day re-upsert would resurrect a meal soft-deleted on another device. Locally, `saveDailyLog` diffs the previous shard against the new list to compute `removedIds`, and `syncMealsToSupabase` soft-deletes them remotely (or queues a `meal/delete` op) so a local deletion does not get merged back in. The one true hard delete is `deleteAllUserData` (account deletion), which `DELETE`s from 15 tables then the `app_users` row.

### Realtime meals (`realtimeMealsService.ts`)

`subscribeMealsForUser(supabaseUserId, onChange)` opens a Supabase channel `food_logs:user:<id>` subscribed to `postgres_changes` (event `*`, schema `public`, table `food_logs`, filter `user_id=eq.<id>`). On any change (including self-fired writes) it calls `invalidateMealsCache()` then `onChange()` (typically a `setMeals(await loadMeals())`). Idempotent per user; `unsubscribeMeals()` tears down on user switch. Requires `food_logs` to be in the `supabase_realtime` publication server-side (`ALTER PUBLICATION supabase_realtime ADD TABLE public.food_logs`).

### PWA cold-open recovery and the sign-out tombstone

On PWA cold open, `@trackkal:accountInfo` is often evicted (iOS Safari ITP) even though the Supabase session is valid. `resolveAccountFromSession()` rebuilds `{email, supabaseUserId}` from `getSession()` and writes it back. It is memoized for `SESSION_FALLBACK_TTL_MS = 4000` and shares an in-flight promise to avoid a write storm across the ~40 callsites of a single cold-open `loadAllData`. A `signedOut` tombstone (set by `markSignedOut()`, cleared on the next real `saveAccountInfo`) prevents the fallback from resurrecting a just-signed-out user from a session that is briefly still valid — important on shared devices.

`loadAccountInfo` treats the cache as source of truth: a remote enrich failure (network/RLS) **never blanks the cache**, so a transient error cannot make a logged-in user appear signed out.

---

What I cut and what to watch:
- I documented the data layer only. The dynamic-adjustment math (200 kcal default, 100/200/300 by pace, 1,200 kcal floor) and the metrics-snapshot derivations live in `dataStorage.ts` but belong to other sections; I included only the storage-relevant pieces.
- **Schema drift risk:** several tables the client reads/writes (`insights`, `detected_patterns`, `weekly_action_plans`, `insight_unlocks`, `daily_summaries`, `calorie_bank_completed_cycles`) and the `user_settings.calorie_bank_config` column are **not** in `docs/supabase-schema.sql`. They were created out of band. The schema file and the RLS file are out of date relative to the code — flagged so the LLM does not assume the SQL docs are exhaustive.
- **Blast radius:** the whole layer keys off `app_users.id ≠ auth.uid()`. Any new table or query that uses `auth.uid()` as `user_id` will silently return zero rows under RLS. The `my_app_user_id()` indirection is the single most important fact in this section.

Relevant files (all absolute): `c:\Users\Hulexo\Downloads\journafied\journafied-app\src\services\dataStorage.ts`, `...\src\services\supabaseDataService.ts`, `...\src\services\realtimeMealsService.ts`, `...\src\types\index.ts`, `...\src\config\featureFlags.ts`, `...\docs\supabase-schema.sql`, `...\docs\supabase-rls-policies.sql`, `...\docs\data-safety.md`.

## 16. Settings and Secondary Screens

---

This section documents `SettingsScreen.tsx` and the secondary screens reached from it: Grocery Suggestions, Integrations, Account, Quick Signup, About, and the Feedback modal. It covers every toggle, control, threshold, copy string, and gating rule, all cited to source.

### Settings architecture overview

`SettingsScreen.tsx` (`src/screens/SettingsScreen.tsx`, ~1416 lines) is the root settings hub. It is not a stack navigator. Every sub screen is a single full height **slide-up modal** animated over the settings list. One `Modal` hosts all panels; the visible panel is chosen by a discriminated `SlideUpType`:

```
'account' | 'notifications' | 'connections' | 'weightUnit' | 'dynamic' | 'smartSuggest'
| 'patternDetection' | 'weeklyOverview' | 'grocery' | 'calorieBank'
```

The panel slides from `SCREEN_HEIGHT` to `0` via `Animated.spring` (`damping: 20, stiffness: 90, overshootClamping: true`). It occupies `SCREEN_HEIGHT * 0.95`; the top `5%` is a tappable backdrop that dismisses. A `PanResponder` drag handle dismisses on drag down past `gs.dy > 100` or fling velocity `gs.vy > 0.5`. Double tap is blocked: `openSlideUp` returns early if `activeSlideUpRef.current !== null`.

Sign in state is reactive, sourced from `UserContext`: `const isSignedIn = !!accountInfo?.email`. Earlier sessions had a stale local boolean bug; this is the fix.

#### Slide-up gating logic (`openSlideUp`)

| Step | Condition | Behavior |
|---|---|---|
| Premium feature requested | `type ∈ ['dynamic','smartSuggest','patternDetection','weeklyOverview','grocery','calorieBank']` and `!isSignedIn` | Alert "Sign In Required" with "Sign In" action that opens the `account` panel |
| Premium feature requested | same set and `plan !== 'premium'` | Calls `onOpenSubscription?.()`, does not open panel |
| `account` requested | `!renderAccountScreen` | Falls back to `onLogin?.()` |
| Otherwise | — | Opens the panel |

Note: the gate here checks `plan !== 'premium'`. The canonical `isPremium` (plan AND signed in AND email, plus the `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` flag) is computed in `HomeScreen` and passed down as the `plan` prop. Settings trusts that prop and only adds the explicit `isSignedIn` check on top.

### Settings list (top to bottom)

Built from `SettingSection` and `SettingItem` (`src/components/SettingsComponents`).

#### Section: Account & Plan

| Item | Icon | Subtitle | Action / Gate |
|---|---|---|---|
| My Account | `user` | "Manage your profile and login" | Opens `account` panel (or `onLogin` fallback) |
| Current Plan | `star` (gold `#EAB308` if premium) | Signed out: "Sign in to manage your plan"; premium: "Premium Plan"; else "Free Plan" | If signed in: button "Manage" (premium, shows alert "You are already on Premium.") or "Upgrade" (calls `onOpenSubscription`). If signed out: row at `opacity 0.5` with a lock icon, no button |
| (Dev) Downgrade to Free | — | — | Only rendered when `plan === 'premium'`; calls `onDowngradeToFree` |

#### Section: App Preferences

Every premium row renders one of two ways: an active `SettingItem` when `plan === 'premium' && isSignedIn`, or a locked variant at `opacity 0.5` (`0.7` for grocery in-progress) with a `shield-lock-outline` right icon and `showChevron={false}`.

| Item | Icon | Premium? | Active subtitle | Locked subtitle |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Notifications | `bell` | No | "Meal reminders & updates" | — |
| Connections | `activity` | No | "Apple Health, Google Fit" | — |
| Weight Unit | `sliders` | No | "Kilograms (kg)" or "Pounds (lbs)" | — |
| Smart Suggest | `zap` | Yes | On: "On · Suggestions on Home"; Off: "Off · Tap to configure" | "Show next meal suggestions on Home" |
| Grocery Suggestions | `shopping-cart` | Yes (+ unlock) | "AI-Powered Lists · Hold to open" | unlocked-not-yet: progress; signed-out: "AI-Powered Lists" |
| Dynamic Adjustments | `trending-up` | Yes | On: ``On · {threshold}% threshold``; Off: "Auto-adjust your plan as your body changes" | "Auto-adjust your plan as your body changes" |
| Calorie Bank | `credit-card` | Yes | On: ``On · Resets every {getDayName(cycleStartDay)}``; Off: "Flexible weekly calorie budgeting" | "Flexible weekly calorie budgeting" |
| Pattern Detection | `eye` | Yes | "Active · Analyzing your eating habits" | "Spot trends in your eating habits" |
| Weekly AI Overview | `bar-chart-2` | Yes | "Active · New insights every Monday" | "Personalized nutrition insights every week" |

Grocery has a third, distinct state for premium signed-in users who have not met the unlock bar: row at `opacity 0.7`, subtitle ``{loggedDays}/5 days · {uniqueFoods}/7 foods to unlock``, and a right pill showing a percent: `Math.round(((min(loggedDays,5) + min(uniqueFoods,7)) / 12) * 100)%`. The unlocked Grocery row opens the explainer panel on press and the full grocery screen on **long press** (`onLongPress={() => onGrocerySuggestions?.()}`).

#### Section: Support & Legal

| Item | Icon | Action |
|---|---|---|
| Help & Support | `help-circle` | Alert "Support content coming soon." |
| How it Works | `book-open` | `onHowItWorks` |
| Contact Us | `mail` | Alert "Contact form coming soon." |
| Privacy Policy | `file-text` | Alert "Privacy Policy" (stub) |
| Terms of Service | `file-text` | Alert "Terms of Service" (stub) |
| About | `info` | Native alert: ``Version {APP_VERSION}\n\nA nutrition and fitness tracking app to help you achieve your health goals.`` (Note: this is an `Alert`, not the standalone `AboutScreen` documented below.) |

#### Section: Data Management

| Item | Icon | Action |
|---|---|---|
| Clear Cache | `trash-2` | `handleClearCache`: confirm dialog, then `AsyncStorage.clear()`, then alert "Data Cleared". Wipes meals, weight, goals, settings. Irreversible. |
| Delete Account | `user-x` | `handleDeleteAccount`: confirm dialog, then `authService.deleteAccount()`. Deletes server data plus device data. Irreversible. |

#### Section: Developer Tools (only when `__DEV__`)

| Item | Action |
|---|---|
| Inject Plateau Data | `dataStorage.debug_injectPlateauData()` then alert "Plateau data injected." (tests Smart Coach) |

#### Version footer

Centered text ``TrackKcal v{APP_VERSION}`` (`APP_VERSION` from `src/constants/appVersion`). This is the live version; do not confuse with the hardcoded "Version 1.0.0" in the separate `AboutScreen`.

### Settings controls in detail

#### Weight Unit panel

Two options: "Kilograms (kg)" and "Pounds (lbs)". Tapping calls `setWeightUnit('kg' | 'lbs')` from `PreferencesContext` then closes. Active option is filled with `theme.colors.primary` and shows a check. Not premium gated.

#### Smart Suggest panel (premium)

A single `Switch`. On toggle it optimistically sets local state and persists `{ ...prefs, smartSuggestEnabled: val }` via `dataStorage.savePreferences`. Defaults **OFF** for new accounts (`useState(false)`, loaded as `prefs?.smartSuggestEnabled === true`). The panel header shows a crown badge. Body is static explainer copy: suggestions appear on Home as a quick-add card, factoring macro targets, remaining calorie budget, and enjoyed foods.

#### Dynamic Adjustments panel (premium)

| Control | Values | Persistence |
|---|---|---|
| Enable switch | on/off | `savePreferences({ ...prefs, dynamicAdjustmentEnabled, dynamicAdjustmentThreshold })` |
| Threshold selector (visible only when enabled) | `[3, 4, 5]` percent | `updateDynamicThreshold(val)` persists `dynamicAdjustmentThreshold` |

Both setters early-return if `plan !== 'premium'`. Default threshold is `5`. Each threshold button shows the absolute weight delta: `currentWeightKg * val / 100`, converted to lbs via `* 2.20462` when `weightUnit === 'lbs'`. Helper copy: "We'll suggest a plan update when your weight changes by {threshold}% (about X kg/lbs)."

The static example (anchored at 100 kg, 2000 kcal):

| Threshold | Triggers at | Target adjusts to | Character |
|---|---|---|---|
| 3% | 97 kg | ~1,940 kcal | "Smaller, more frequent updates" |
| 4% | 96 kg | ~1,900 kcal | "A balanced middle ground" |
| 5% | 95 kg | ~1,800 kcal | "Fewer but bigger updates" |

These example numbers are illustrative copy, not the live adjustment formula.

#### Calorie Bank panel (premium)

The richest panel. The config type is `CalorieBankConfig` (`dataStorage.ts:38`):

```
enabled: boolean
cycleStartDay: 0|1|2|3|4|5|6        // 0=Sun ... 6=Sat
dailyCapPercent: 15|20|25           // max % of base target bankable per day
spendingCapPercent: 15|20|25        // max % of base target spendable over per day
enabledDate: string                 // ISO date when first enabled
pendingDailyCapPercent?: 15|20|25   // queued cap, applies next cycle
```

| Control | Values | Behavior |
|---|---|---|
| Enable switch | on/off | On: optimistic set, then `enableCalorieBank()` (from `calorieBankService`). Off: optimistic clear, then `disableCalorieBank()`. Optimistic default if no prior config: `{ enabled: true, cycleStartDay: 1, dailyCapPercent: 20, spendingCapPercent: 20, enabledDate: today }` |
| Cycle Start Day | day buttons in order `[1,2,3,4,5,6,0]` (Mon first, Sun last), labeled via `getDayName` | Tapping a non-active day shows confirm "Change start day? This starts a new week today...". On confirm: archives the in-progress cycle (`archiveInProgressCycle(summaries, goals)`), then `updateCalorieBankSettings({ cycleStartDay })` |
| Daily Banking Cap | `[15, 20, 25]` percent | Sets **both** `dailyCapPercent` and `spendingCapPercent` to the chosen pct via `updateCalorieBankSettings`. Selected value displayed is `pendingDailyCapPercent ?? dailyCapPercent`. Each button shows `~{Math.round(baseCalorieTarget * pct / 100)} kcal` |

If `pendingDailyCapPercent` differs from the active `dailyCapPercent`, a primary-colored note shows: "New cap applies from your next cycle ({day}). This week keeps its current cap." Cap helper: "The maximum you can bank or spend beyond your daily target in a single day. This prevents extreme restriction or overeating."

Static explainer content (load-bearing for the engine semantics):

- Weekly budget = daily target × 7.
- "Banked" (green `#22C55E`): unused calories transfer to remaining days, raising their targets.
- "Surplus" (red `#EF4444`): over-target calories deduct from remaining days, lowering their targets.
- Three worked examples toggled by `bankExampleTab` (`'lose' | 'maintain' | 'gain'`):

| Tab | Daily target | Weekly budget | Premise |
|---|---|---|---|
| lose | 2,000 | 14,000 | Mon 1,650 → 350 banked, spread ~58/day over 6 days; Sat 2,350 covered by bank; weekly 13,900 under budget |
| maintain | 2,200 | 15,400 | Weekdays ~2,000 saves ~200/day → 1,000 banked; Sat 2,700 (+500) covered; weekly 15,300 |
| gain | 3,000 | 21,000 | Banking reversed: training days +500 banked, rest days 2,625 draw down; weekly lands at 21,000 |

"Good to know" safety notes (these are the user-facing statements of the engine guardrails): daily target never drops below **1,500 kcal (men) / 1,200 kcal (women)**; a skipped logging day is assumed to equal base target with no banking and no penalty; the bank resets to zero on the chosen start day and unused banked calories expire; protein, carbs, and fat scale with the adjusted target by keeping percentages fixed and changing only grams.

#### Notifications and Connections panels

`activeSlideUp === 'notifications'` renders `NotificationSettingsScreen` (documented elsewhere) with `initialPreferences={loadedPreferences}`. `'connections'` renders `IntegrationsScreen` (below). Neither is premium gated.

### IntegrationsScreen

`src/screens/IntegrationsScreen.tsx`. Connects wearables and health apps. Not premium gated. Platform-specific:

| Platform | Card | Subtitle | Toggle handler |
|---|---|---|---|
| iOS (`Platform.OS === 'ios'`) | Apple Health (icon `activity`, `#FF2D55`) | "Syncs with Apple Watch" | `handleToggleAppleHealth` |
| Android (`Platform.OS === 'android'`) | Health Connect (icon `watch`, `#2196F3`) | "Samsung Health, Google Fit, Pixel Watch" | `handleToggleHealthConnect` |

Both call `healthService.init()`. On success: marks connected, sets `lastSync = new Date().toLocaleTimeString()`, success alert. On failure: if `!healthService.isModuleAvailable()` shows a "Development Build Required" alert ("This feature cannot work in Expo Go."); otherwise a generic "Connection Failed" alert. A Sync Status section appears only once connected, showing "Last synced" and a "Sync Now" button that calls `healthService.getData()` and alerts ``Updated data: {steps} steps, {Math.round(calories)} kcal.``

`HealthService` (`src/services/HealthService.ts`) dynamically `require`s `react-native-health` (iOS) and `react-native-health-connect` (Android) inside try/catch so Expo Go does not crash. It requests **read-only** permissions for Steps, ActiveEnergyBurned/ActiveCaloriesBurned, and Distance. `getData` returns `{ steps, calories, distance }`; Android sums records across a same-day `between` time range filter and reads `energy.inKilocalories` / `distance.inMeters`. There is no write/export path. In Expo Go or unlinked builds, `getData` returns `{ steps: 0, calories: 0, distance: 0 }`.

### AccountScreen

`src/screens/AccountScreen.tsx`. Rendered inside the Settings `account` slide-up via the `renderAccountScreen` prop. Two states driven by `authSession`: logged out (auth form) and logged in (profile). `FREE_ENTRY_LIMIT = 20` is defined here.

It seeds an **optimistic fake session** from cached email (`initialAccountInfo?.email`) so the logged-in view paints instantly, then `authService.getSession()` confirms or demotes it to `null` (so a user with a stale cached email but no real session is never stuck on a view they cannot sign out of).

#### Logged-out form (tabs: Sign In / Create Account, controlled by `authMode`)

| Field | Shown in | Validation |
|---|---|---|
| Name | signup only | required (`setNameError`) |
| Email | both | regex `/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/` |
| Password | both | min 6 chars (signup: "Password must be at least 6 characters.") |

- **Sign In** (`handleSignIn`): `authService.signIn(email, password)` (`signInWithPassword`, lowercased). On session, syncs account info from session and reloads.
- **Sign Up** (`handleSignUp`): `authService.signUp(email.toLowerCase(), password)`. If a session returns (email confirmation OFF) the user is signed in immediately and a provisional `AccountInfo` is saved. If `data.user && !data.session` (confirmation ON) only the name is persisted, an alert tells the user to confirm via email, and the tab flips to `signin`.
- **Forgot password** (signin only): opens a modal; `authService.resetPasswordForEmail` sends a reset link. Redirect is the PWA origin on web, else deep link `io.supabase.trackkcal://reset-callback/`.
- **Reset all app data**: `authService.signOut()` then `AsyncStorage.clear()`.
- Includes a **country picker modal** (searchable `COUNTRIES` list, dial codes) and phone parsing (`parseStoredPhone` matches longest dial code first), though phone is not required for auth here.

#### Logged-in profile

- Profile card: avatar initial, name (fallback "User"), email, and a plan badge ("Premium Plan" / "Free Plan"). The plan badge syncs to the `initialPlan` prop passed from HomeScreen (canonical entitlement), not the raw stored plan string.
- Account Stats grid (each `47%` width): Total Entries, Referrals, Current Weight, Goal Weight, Weight Change (green `#22C55E` when positive i.e. loss, sign rendered as `-` for loss), Daily Calorie Goal (`{goals.calories} kcal`). Weights run through `convertWeightToDisplay` and `getWeightUnitLabel`.
- Actions: **Sign Out** (`authService.signOut`, confirm dialog), **Delete Account** (`authService.deleteAccount()` then `AsyncStorage.clear()`, irreversible), **Clear All Local Data** (`handleClearData`: sign out + clear, returns to Home).

This screen also carries a secondary copy of the Dynamic Adjustments toggle/threshold logic (`toggleDynamicAdjustment`, `updateDynamicThreshold`, both premium-gated, default threshold 5), mirroring Settings; the state exists but the visible UI here is centered on auth and stats.

### QuickSignupScreen

`src/screens/QuickSignupScreen.tsx`. Zero-friction onboarding capture. Props: `prefilledName`, `onComplete` (resolves for both success and skip).

- Fields: Name (required), Email (required, regex validated), Mobile (optional). `canSubmit = name && isValidEmail(email) && !submitting`.
- **No password field.** It generates a 24-char random password from `ABC…xyz0123456789!@#$%` and calls `authService.signUp(email.toLowerCase(), randomPassword())`. The user never sees this password; recovery is via password reset later. Stated tradeoff: invisible auth for launch onboarding.
- On `data.session`: saves full `AccountInfo` (name, email, optional phone, `supabaseUserId`) and calls `onComplete`.
- If email already registered: error "That email already has an account. Tap Skip and sign in from Settings." (no sign-in path exists on this screen).
- If `!data.session` (Supabase "Confirm email" is ON): does **not** persist a signed-in identity (avoids creating a ghost premium account with an unrecoverable random password). Saves only the name, alerts the user to confirm, continues as guest. A `__DEV__` warning flags the Supabase misconfiguration.
- **Skip**: confirm dialog warning "Your data will stay on this device only. If you clear your browser or reinstall, you'll lose your plan." then `onComplete`.

### AboutScreen

`src/screens/AboutScreen.tsx`. Standalone static screen (distinct from the Settings "About" alert). Card shows app name "TrackKcal", a **hardcoded "Version 1.0.0"** (note: stale, not wired to `APP_VERSION`), and a description. Links section opens external URLs via `Linking.openURL`:

| Link | URL |
|---|---|
| Privacy Policy | `https://trackkcal.com/privacy.html` |
| Terms of Service | `https://trackkcal.com/terms.html` |

No state, no gating.

### FeedbackModal

`src/components/FeedbackModal.tsx`, backed by `feedbackService` (`src/services/feedbackService.ts`). A `pageSheet` modal. Three category cards (default `general`):

| Key | Label | Icon | Description |
|---|---|---|---|
| bug | Bug | `alert-circle` | "Something broke or behaves wrong" |
| idea | Idea | `zap` | "A feature you wish existed" |
| general | General | `message-circle` | "Anything else on your mind" |

- Message textarea: `maxLength={4000}`, live counter `{length}/4000`. `canSubmit = message.trim().length >= 3 && !submitting`.
- Optional Email field ("if you want a reply").
- On submit: `feedbackService.submit({ message, category, email })`. Success shows a check screen ("Got it" / "Thanks. We read every one.") for 1400 ms then resets and closes. Failure: alert "Could not send".

`feedbackService.submit` validates non-empty and `length <= 4000` (throws "Message is too long." over 4000). It resolves email from input or `accountInfo?.email`, derives `source` (`pwa` / `ios` / `android`), `app_version` from Expo config, and `user_agent` (web only, first 500 chars). Inserts into the Supabase `feedback` table. `user_id` linkage is best-effort, backfilled by a Supabase trigger matching the email to an `app_users` row.

### GrocerySuggestionsScreen and the grocery feature

`src/screens/GrocerySuggestionsScreen.tsx`, with deterministic generator `src/services/GrocerySuggestionService.ts` and the AI layer `src/services/groceryCoachService.ts`.

#### Unlock gate (premium AND earned)

Grocery is premium, and additionally requires an in-app unlock. `dataStorage.checkGroceryUnlockEligibility()` returns `eligible` when **`loggedDays >= 5 && uniqueFoods >= 7`**, where:
- `loggedDays` = count of daily summaries with `entryCount > 0`.
- `uniqueFoods` = size of the set of lowercased, trimmed food names across all logged days.

Once eligible, `setGroceryUnlocked()` persists `@trackkal:groceryUnlocked = 'true'`; a separate `@trackkal:groceryUnlockSeen` flag tracks whether the unlock celebration was shown. The Settings row reflects progress before unlock (`{loggedDays}/5 days · {uniqueFoods}/7 foods`).

#### Generation pipeline (`loadData`)

1. Load or generate `UserMetricsSnapshot` (`getUserMetricsSnapshot` then `generateUserMetricsSnapshot` if absent). If still null: error "Insufficient data. Log a few meals first!".
2. Load active insights.
3. `generateGrocerySuggestions(snapshot, insights, null)` builds the deterministic list.
4. `groceryCoachService.getGroceryCoachExplanation(result, context)` produces the AI narrative (the list itself is never invented by the LLM).

#### Deterministic generator logic (`generateGrocerySuggestions`)

| Constant | Value |
|---|---|
| Base needed categories | always `{protein, carbs, fats, fiber}` |
| Category display order | `protein, fiber, carbs, fats, micronutrients` |
| Junk-replacement threshold | `weeklyTargetKcal * 0.8` (80% buffer) where `weeklyTargetKcal = userGoals.calories * 7` |
| Weight projection constant | `7700 kcal = 1 kg` |
| TDEE estimate | `goal.calories + 500` (lose), `- 500` (gain), unchanged (maintain) |
| Fiber bump on scale-up | `× 1.2` |
| Max user favorites per category | `slice(0, 5)` |

Category mapping tables:
- `INSIGHT_TO_NUTRIENT`: e.g. `'Protein Intake Low' → protein`, `'Weekend Overeating' → fiber` (satiety), `'Carb Overload' → protein`, `'Fat Fatigue' → carbs`.
- `WEAKNESS_TO_NUTRIENT`: `protein→protein`, `fiber→fiber`, `carbs→carbs`, `fats→fats`, `vitamins/iron/calcium→micronutrients`.
- `getCategoryForFood`: keyword heuristics (e.g. chicken/beef/egg/tofu/tuna→protein; bean/oat/berry/broccoli→fiber; rice/potato/bread/pasta→carbs; avocado/nut/oil/butter→fats; spinach/kale/pepper/carrot→micronutrients).

It only uses foods the user has actually logged (no default foods are injected into the list; `DEFAULT_FOODS` exists but is unused in the current path). Processed items are filtered out even when favorited via `PROCESSED_INDICATORS` (`fried, chip, cake, cookie, candy, soda, ice cream, biscuit, donut, pastry, chocolate, sweet, glazed, breaded, battered`).

Quantity/macro defaults per category (`QUANTITY_DEFAULTS`, per 1-week base quantity):

| Category | Qty | Unit | kcal | P | C | F |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| protein | 1 | kg | 1650 | 310 | 0 | 36 |
| fiber | 500 | g | 170 | 14 | 33 | 2 |
| carbs | 500 | g | 650 | 13 | 140 | 2 |
| fats | 1 | pack | 1200 | 40 | 40 | 106 |
| micronutrients | 300 | g | 70 | 9 | 11 | 1 |

Per-item overrides (`ITEM_QUANTITY_OVERRIDES`) include eggs (12 count, 840 kcal), avocado (3 count, 720), banana (1 bunch, 600), apple (6 count, 570), olive oil (1 bottle, 2000), canned tuna (3 cans, 400), milk (2 L, 1000), greek yogurt (1 kg, 590).

**Junk-replacement scaling**: if `currentListKcal < threshold`, the deficit is distributed across protein/carbs/fats by the user's own macro ratios (`g.protein*4 / calories`, etc., normalized; fallback `0.3/0.4/0.3`), scaling each item's quantity and macros linearly. `replacedJunkCalories` is set to that deficit; the UI shows the swap banner only when `replacedJunkCalories > 200`. Items are deduped by `normalizeFoodName` (collapses egg/chicken/rice/bread variants).

**Summary** returns `weeklyTotal {p,c,f,kcal}`, `replacedJunkCalories` (floored at 0), `projectedWeightLossKg = ((tdee*7) - weeklyTotal.kcal) / 7700`, and `maintenanceCalibration = tdee`.

#### AI coach layer (`groceryCoachService`)

| Property | Value |
|---|---|
| Model | `gpt-4o-mini` |
| Temperature | `0.5` |
| Max tokens | `450` |
| Response format | `json_schema`, `name: 'grocery_coach'`, `strict: true` |
| `call_type` | `'grocery-coach'` |
| Path | `invokeAI` (proxy only) |

Inputs are sanitized with `sanitizeObjectForAI` (food names are user-controlled; injection guard). The schema returns `{ title, summary, itemExplanations[] }` where `itemExplanations` is an array of `{name, explanation}` (converted to a dict in app). Guardrails in the system prompt: do not add/remove foods, do not invent micronutrient data, no medical advice, only explain the provided list. A plateau hypothesis is gently surfaced (phrased as "might be") when consistency > 75%, intake ≈ target, and weight is stable. On any failure it returns `null` and the screen falls back to showing `groceryData.primaryFocus`.

#### Grocery screen UI

- Header: back (`chevron-down`), title "Grocery List" with `{checked}/{total} items checked` subtitle, and a PDF share button.
- **Duration toggle**: 1 Week / 2 Weeks (`durationWeeks ∈ {1,2}`). All quantities, macros, kcal, and projected loss multiply by `durationWeeks` at render time.
- AI Insight card (or `primaryFocus` fallback).
- Items grouped by category, render priority `['protein','fiber','micronutrients','fats','carbs']`. Category colors: protein `#6366F1`, fiber `#10B981`, carbs `#F59E0B`, fats `#EC4899`, micronutrients `#8B5CF6`. Each item is a checkbox row (strike-through when checked, `#10B981`), shows scaled qty/unit, a kcal pill, `P/C/F` grams, a `★` if `reason === 'user_favorite'`, and the AI per-item reason when present.
- **Plan Impact** summary: big Total kcal (`weeklyTotal.kcal * weeks`), big kg expected (`projectedWeightLossKg * weeks`, green if loss else `#F59E0B`), macro pills, and a swap banner ("Swapped ~X kcal of processed food...") only when `replacedJunkCalories > 200`.
- **PDF export** (`expo-print` + `expo-sharing`): builds inline HTML grouped by category (priority `protein, fiber, micronutrients, fats, carbs`), each row name + `qty × weeks unit`, footer "Generated by TrackKcal". Shared as `application/pdf`.
- Disclaimer: "Suggestions are based on your nutrition data and are for informational purposes only."

### Completeness notes

- **Cut for scope**: `NotificationSettingsScreen` (rendered from the `notifications` slide-up) is documented in its own section, not here.
- **Worth flagging (stale/inconsistent)**: `AboutScreen` hardcodes "Version 1.0.0" while the rest of the app uses `APP_VERSION`. Settings has a Privacy/Terms that show stub alerts, while `AboutScreen` links to real `trackkcal.com` URLs. Two parallel implementations of Dynamic Adjustments persistence exist (SettingsScreen and AccountScreen) writing the same `dynamicAdjustmentEnabled`/`dynamicAdjustmentThreshold` keys. `DEFAULT_FOODS` in the grocery generator is defined but unused.
- **Blast radius**: "Clear Cache", "Delete Account", and "Clear All Local Data" all call `AsyncStorage.clear()` and are irreversible; the calorie-bank Cycle Start Day change archives the in-progress week. None visually tested by me in this pass.

## 17. Current State, Known Limitations and Roadmap

### Pre-launch status

TrackKcal is pre-launch, targeting a Q2 2026 public release. No build has shipped to the Google Play Store or App Store yet. `app.json` carries `android.versionCode: 1` and Expo `version: "1.0.0"` (the OTA runtime version, deliberately frozen so OTA updates keep reaching installed builds). The store-facing version has never been incremented. The release gate is `docs/RELEASE.md`, whose checklist is mostly unchecked: `npm test` is still a TODO ("add once automated test suite is available"), the `.env` Supabase-keys check is unchecked, and "Manual smoke test on a physical Android device" is unchecked.

### Version constants

There are two independent version numbers. Do not conflate them.

| Constant | File | Current value | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|
| `APP_VERSION` | `src/constants/appVersion.ts` | `'1.3.6'` | Display version in Settings. Bumped on every commit so you can tell which build is on a given PWA/APK. |
| `expo.version` | `app.json` | `'1.0.0'` | Drives the EAS Update `runtimeVersion` (policy `appVersion`). Must stay stable or OTA stops reaching installed builds. |
| `android.versionCode` | `app.json` | `1` | Play Store build counter. Never incremented (no store release yet). |

The latest commit is `7161d74 gate every nutrition insight behind its own unlock (v1.3.6)`. Note: project memory still records "current live version v1.3.4 on both APK and PWA"; the code is two commits ahead (v1.3.5 nutrition snapshot fix, v1.3.6 nutrition insight gating), so v1.3.5/v1.3.6 may not yet be pushed to both distribution targets.

### Dual distribution

The app ships to two targets in parallel, from one codebase. They must be deployed sequentially, never together, because both `eas update` and `expo export -p web` write to `dist/` and will clobber each other mid-upload.

| Target | Mechanism | Channel / project | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| Native APK | EAS Update (OTA) | `preview` channel (`eas.json` → `build.preview`, `distribution: "internal"`, `buildType: "apk"`) | Push with `npx eas-cli@latest update --branch preview`. Preview build sets `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=4096` and `SENTRY_DISABLE_AUTO_UPLOAD=true`. |
| PWA | `expo export -p web` then Vercel | Vercel project `trackkcal-pwa` (alias `trackkcal-pwa.vercel.app`) | Web output is `single` (`app.json` web.output), Metro bundler, standalone display, theme `#FBF9F4`. |
| Native store build | EAS `production` profile | `production` channel, `buildType: "app-bundle"`, `distribution: "store"` | Defined but not exercised; no store submission has happened. |

Two EAS gotchas are load-bearing and live in the deploy runbook:
1. Plain `tsc` stack-overflows on this project. Typecheck with `node --stack-size=8000 ./node_modules/typescript/lib/tsc.js --noEmit`. A clean run still exits non-zero with only the `supabase/functions/ai-proxy` Deno errors, which are expected.
2. The Windows `hermesc.exe` bundler crashes (`ENOMEM` / code 3765269347) when free RAM is low (this dev machine has 8 GB). Web export is unaffected because web does not use Hermes bytecode. Low-RAM workaround is a prebuilt upload with `--skip-bundler`, which loses source maps and so produces minified Sentry traces until a full build is re-run.

### FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH posture

`src/config/featureFlags.ts` sets `export const FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH = true`. During launch this grants premium features to every signed-in user, with no paywall. The architectural invariant still holds: the downstream `isPremium` check requires a `premium` plan AND a signed-in account with an email, so signed-out users get nothing. The flag flips to `false` when paid tiers and RevenueCat go live. This is also why conversion is currently unmeasurable: per `docs/product/METRICS.md`, free-to-paid conversion "is masked by the launch flag, so it is unmeasurable until real payments ship." `docs/product/STRATEGY.md` flags the free/paid line as the biggest open decision: "it is currently a launch flag, not a decision."

The only other feature flag is `featureFlags.grocerySuggestions`, gated to an admin allowlist: emails `admin@trackkcal.com`, `hulexo@trackkcal.com`, `test@trackkcal.com`, or Supabase user id `admin-user-id`. Default is `false`, so grocery suggestions are effectively admin-only / off for normal users.

### Disabled and stubbed features (verified in code)

| Item | Status | Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| Free 3-meals/day limit | DISABLED pre-launch | `HomeScreen.canAddEntry()` is hardcoded `return true` with `// TODO: Re-enable daily limit (3 meals/day for free users) before launch`. The "Daily Limit Reached" alert copy ("Free plan is limited to 3 meals per day…") still exists in both text and photo paths but is unreachable. |
| Real in-app purchases (RevenueCat) | NOT BUILT | `handleSubscribe(plan)` in HomeScreen just calls `setUserPlan('premium')` + `dataStorage.saveUserPlan('premium')` and closes the modal. No StoreKit/Play Billing. "Restore purchases" is a label only. Doc §16.4 confirms purchasing is simulated. |
| Google / Apple OAuth | NOT WIRED | `AccountWallModal.tsx` renders both OAuth buttons `disabled` at `opacity: 0.5` with copy "Sign in with Google — coming soon" / "Sign in with Apple — coming soon". `src/config/env.ts` has empty `GOOGLE_OAUTH` client-id slots pulled from env. Auth is email-OTP only (`authService.signInWithOtp` / `verifyOtp`, 6-digit code). |
| Resend / SMTP for auth email | NOT CONFIGURED | OTP emails go through Supabase's built-in email service. Doc §16.5: "No real email/SMTP service… rate limits and deliverability limitations." Roadmap lists SMTP as not-yet-built. |
| Referral reward push notification | PLACEHOLDER | `notificationService.sendReferralRewardNotification` comments "this is a placeholder" and only fires a local notification; real push needs a backend to map emails → push tokens. |
| Help & Support / Contact Us | PLACEHOLDER | `SettingsScreen` shows `Alert.alert('Help', 'Support content coming soon.')` and `'Contact form coming soon.'` |
| Grocery list default foods | LEAKY | `GrocerySuggestionService.ts` `DEFAULT_FOODS` fallbacks still suggest foods the user never logged; the "restrict to logged foods only" change was discussed, not finished (doc §16.3). |
| Exercise section | VESTIGIAL | `ExerciseLogSection` and exercise state remain for non-banking users even though Calorie Bank supersedes it (doc §16.2). |

### Crash and error monitoring

Sentry is wired and live for React Native: `App.tsx` calls `Sentry.init` with a hardcoded DSN (`o4511453446012928…/4511453482516560`), `Sentry.mobileReplayIntegration()` and `Sentry.feedbackIntegration()`, and the app is wrapped in `Sentry.wrap`. Metro uses `getSentryExpoConfig`. The `@sentry/react-native/expo` plugin points at org `trackkcal`, project `react-native`. Caveat: the preview profile sets `SENTRY_DISABLE_AUTO_UPLOAD=true`, and the low-RAM `--skip-bundler` deploy path produces minified stack traces.

### The hardening campaign (what has been done)

Kunaal is running a section-by-section launch bug-fix and hardening campaign. Method per section: a multi-agent audit (parallel investigators by dimension → adversarial verification of each finding → synthesis), then fixes shipped in waves, each wave a bumped `APP_VERSION` pushed to both the APK (EAS preview) and the PWA (Vercel).

Sections closed so far, with the version ranges that delivered them:

| Section | Versions | What was hardened |
|---|---|---|
| Auth & Session (12) | v1.1.x | sign-out resurrection, silent delete-account failure, five auth/session P1s, sign-out hang, calorie flash, wall re-nag, stale preferences |
| Data Sync & Offline (13) | v1.2.0 – v1.2.2 | local-first pull (stop reverting local data), queue/meal-loader locking (stop queue stalls), stop dropping unsynced meals, keep newer edits, fix delete resurrection |
| Home & Core Logging (1) | v1.2.3 – v1.2.7 | the only P0 (day-switch mid-analysis wiping the original day's meals), write-amplification (#16), photo path aligned to text path, set-goals prompt instead of fake targets for new users, home not asserting unproven success |
| Calorie Bank (engine + cards + settings) | v1.2.8 – v1.3.4 | audit found 13 bugs + 9 improvements. Fixed: gain-goal redistribution inversion, utilization drift, simplified the bank card to Food/Exercise/Remaining (killed 5 card bugs), re-enable wipe, premium flicker, swipe-blank, archival rebuild (settle all completed cycles + gap cycles), cap "apply from next cycle", start-day archiving + warnings, coach awareness of the bank, use-it-before-you-lose-it nudge + recap, honest weekly card, accessibility labels, foreground recompute |
| Nutrition Analysis (in progress) | v1.3.5 – v1.3.6 | nutrition snapshot feeding the AI wrong averages (v1.3.5); gate every nutrition insight behind its own unlock (v1.3.6) |

Remaining tier-A target: Subscription/Premium/Paywall. Tier B: Weight Tracker, AI Coach, Set Goals/Onboarding, Settings. Tier C: Referrals, Notifications, Grocery, Integrations, AI prompts/proxy.

Two Calorie Bank issues were deferred on purpose (not regressions): bug 7, where "In Bank" can exceed the realizable amount late in a cycle (covered by the nudge/recap; a display change risks confusion); and a rare edge where a pending cap change plus the app closed for 2+ full cycles archives those cycles under the old cap. Three Section-1 items were also left intentionally: the PWA-only account-wall flash on cache eviction (parked), background pattern-detection possibly missing a run on cold start if `isPremium` is not hydrated (safe direction, no data loss), and the account-wall nag firing on the blended meal+exercise count (copy fixed to "N times", trigger left as-is).

### Known limitations and rough edges

These are genuine, code-grounded constraints an extender should expect.

| # | Limitation | Source |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | No automated tests. All testing is manual. Biggest single gap. | doc §16.1 |
| 2 | Shipped fixes from v1.2.3 onward are verified against code but several were never run by Kunaal on a real device (the PWA could not accept photos at the time and there was no APK on hand). Pending manual tests are tracked for v1.2.3/v1.2.4/v1.2.5. The native app is the real test surface. | memory `pending-manual-tests` |
| 3 | Image analysis does not compress photos. Full-size base64 is sent to the AI proxy, slow on poor connections. | doc §16.8 |
| 4 | No pagination in meal history. All daily shards load into state; months of data will get slow. | doc §16.9, §18 scaling |
| 5 | Account info can desync between AsyncStorage and the Supabase user record across devices. Merge logic in `loadGoals()` covers goals, not all data types. | doc §16.7 |
| 6 | Calorie bank redistribution recalculates on every render via a `useEffect`. Fast for a 7-day cycle, but wasteful under frequent re-renders. | doc §16.6 |
| 7 | Smart Suggest daily cache keys on `new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]`, which can drift around midnight in non-UTC zones. | doc §16.10 |
| 8 | OTP deliverability is at the mercy of Supabase's built-in email rate limits until a real SMTP/Resend provider is added. This directly throttles signup. | doc §16.5 |
| 9 | OpenAI cost is uncontrolled at scale; the mitigation is the food-analysis/confidence prompt-hash cache, not a budget. At 10K+ users this needs aggressive caching; at 100K, a move off Edge Functions to a dedicated API with rate limiting. | doc §18 scaling |
| 10 | Health integrations (Apple Health, Health Connect) require a native development build; they cannot work in Expo Go, and the connect UI surfaces a "Development Build Required" alert when the native module is absent. | `IntegrationsScreen.tsx`, `HealthService` |

### Roadmap (not yet built)

From `docs/TrackKCal-Complete-Documentation.md` §18 and the decision log (subscription pricing target: AED 89.99/year, AED 24.99/month):

- RevenueCat real in-app purchases (replace the simulated `onSubscribe`)
- OAuth sign-in (Google, Apple) — buttons already stubbed
- SMTP/Resend for reliable auth email
- Data export (CSV/JSON)
- Water tracking
- Barcode scanning (discussed, not implemented)
- Recipe builder (ingredient aggregation, serving-size math)
- Social features (progress sharing, challenges)
- Apple Watch / WearOS companion app
- Home-screen widget for a quick calorie check

Scaling milestones: 1K users — current architecture is fine, may need to leave the Supabase free tier; 10K — OpenAI cost becomes material, cache harder, Sentry already in place; 100K — CDN, image-compression pipeline, meal-history pagination, and a dedicated API server replacing Edge Functions.

Relevant files: `src/config/featureFlags.ts`, `src/config/env.ts`, `src/constants/appVersion.ts`, `app.json`, `eas.json`, `docs/RELEASE.md`, `docs/TrackKCal-Complete-Documentation.md` (§16–§19), `docs/product/{STRATEGY,METRICS}.md`, `src/screens/HomeScreen.tsx` (`canAddEntry`, `handleSubscribe`), `src/screens/SubscriptionScreen.tsx`, `src/components/AccountWallModal.tsx`, `src/services/authService.ts`, `src/services/notificationService.ts`, `App.tsx` (Sentry init).

## 18. Glossary

| Term | Definition |
|---|---|
| `adjusted target` / `adjustedTarget` | Per-day calorie target after the bank redistributes the running balance across remaining days. Computed in pass 2 of `calculateCurrentCycle`: `baseDailyTarget + adjustmentPerDay`, then clamped between `targetFloor` and `targetCeiling`. Past days keep `baseTarget`. `adjustedTodayTarget` is today's value (`src/utils/calorieBankEngine.ts`). |
| `adjustmentPerDay` | The amount added to (or subtracted from) each remaining day's base target. For lose/maintain: `-rawOverspend/remainingDays` when over, `bankBalance/remainingDays` when under. Gain mirrors it on the opposite axis. Drives `adjustedTarget`. |
| `ai-proxy` | The Supabase Edge Function (`supabase/functions/ai-proxy/index.ts`, Deno) that proxies all OpenAI calls. The OpenAI key lives only here as a secret. Invoked via `supabase.functions.invoke('ai-proxy', ...)`. Cancellation propagates client → Edge Function → OpenAI so a timeout never leaves zombie billing. |
| `app_users` vs `auth uid` | Two distinct user identities. `supabaseUserId` = `auth.uid()` (Supabase auth user). `appUserId` = the `app_users` table row id, which is what `food_logs.user_id` holds. Both live on `AccountInfo`. Code must not interchange them. |
| `account wall` / `AccountWallModal` | A modal (`src/components/AccountWallModal.tsx`) shown after a threshold number of logs (`logCount` prop) prompting the anonymous user to continue with email. Creating an account is the gate for premium, since `isPremium` requires a signed-in email. |
| `activityLevel` / `activityRate` | TDEE inputs on `ExtendedGoalData`. `activityLevel` is one of `'sedentary' | 'light' | 'moderate' | 'very'`; `activityRate` is a numeric multiplier. |
| `AccountInfo` | Local account record: `name`, `email`, `phoneNumber`, `supabaseUserId` (auth uid), `appUserId` (app_users id), `passwordHash`, `hasUsedReferralCode`, `premiumUntil`. Stored under `@trackkal:accountInfo` (`src/services/dataStorage.ts`). |
| `AsyncStorage first, Supabase eventual` | Architecture rule: local AsyncStorage is the source of truth and writes return immediately; sync to Supabase happens in the background. UX never blocks on network. |
| `bank balance` / `bankBalance` | Running total of banked minus spent across the cycle, floored at 0 (`if (bankBalance < 0) bankBalance = 0`). For lose/maintain, `bankBalance = totalBanked - totalSpent` (capped quantities). Drives upward redistribution only. |
| `banked` | Calories saved on a past completed day, capped at `dailyCap`. For lose/maintain it is `min(baseTarget - actual, dailyCap)` when under target. For gain it is the capped surplus (over target banks). Never computed for today or future days. |
| `baseDailyTarget` / `baseTarget` | The user's plain daily calorie goal before any banking adjustment: `goals.calories || 2000`. The reference every day is settled against. |
| `BMI` | Body Mass Index insight (`id: 'bmi'`), Weight Tracker. Unlocks at `weightEntries >= 1 && hasHeight`. Computed from height + weight. |
| `calorie bank` / `Calorie Bank` | Premium weekly budget engine. Banks unused calories from past completed days and spends overages, redistributing the balance across remaining days in a 7-day cycle. Never settles today or future days (today is live and unsettled). Engine: `src/utils/calorieBankEngine.ts`. |
| `CalorieBankConfig` | User settings for the bank: `enabled`, `cycleStartDay` (0–6), `dailyCapPercent` (15/20/25), `spendingCapPercent` (15/20/25), `enabledDate` (ISO), plus `pendingDailyCapPercent`/`pendingSpendingCapPercent`. Stored under `@trackkal:calorieBankConfig`. |
| `CalorieBankCompletedCycle` | Archived analytics record for a finished cycle: `weeklyBudget`, `weeklyActual`, `bankUtilization`, `expiredCalories`, `daysLogged`, `daysInCycle`, `peakBankBalance`, `capHitDays`, `spendCapHitDays`, `goalType`. Built by `buildCompletedCycleRecord`. |
| `CalorieBankCycle` | The full computed state of the current cycle returned by `calculateCurrentCycle`: boundaries, `baseDailyTarget`, `weeklyBudget`, `daysInCycle`, `perDayData[]`, `bankBalance`, `remainingBudget`, `remainingDays`, `weeklyActual`, `weeklyLoggedActual`, `adjustedTodayTarget`, `todayMacros`, `goalType`. |
| `CalorieBankDayData` | One day's settled record inside a cycle: `date`, `baseTarget`, `adjustedTarget`, `actual`, `banked`, `spent`, `logged`, `isFuture`, `isToday`, `capHit`, `spendCapHit`. |
| `capHit` / `spendCapHit` | Booleans flagging that a day's banking cap (`difference > dailyCap`) or spending cap (`|difference| > spendingCap`) was reached. Counted as `capHitDays` / `spendCapHitDays` per cycle. |
| `confidence` / confidence level | A food estimate's trustworthiness: `'low' | 'medium' | 'high'` on `ParsedFood` (`src/utils/foodNutrition.ts`), with `confidence_reason`. Set by the food-analysis prompt based on how the user described the food. |
| `confidence badge` / `ConfidenceBadge` | UI badge (`src/components/ConfidenceBadge.tsx`) rendering the food's confidence with a colored dot. For low/medium it can fetch a `ConfidenceHint` via `generateConfidenceHint` telling the user how to raise confidence next time. Hidden when confidence is undefined; no improvement hint shown for `high`. |
| `cycle` | A 7-day calorie-bank window aligned to `cycleStartDay`. The first cycle may be partial (clamped to `enabledDate`), so `daysInCycle` can be fewer than 7. End is always `start + 6` days. |
| `cycleStartDay` | Day of week the cycle resets on: `0=Sun … 6=Sat`. `getCycleStartDate` finds the most recent occurrence on or before the reference date. |
| `DailySummary` | Per-day rollup keyed by `YYYY-MM-DD`: `totalCalories`, `totalProtein/Carbs/Fat`, `entryCount`, `updatedAt`, plus optional micros (`totalFiber`, `totalSugar`, `totalSodium`, `totalVitaminA`, etc.). Stored in the summaries blob `@trackkal:summaries`. Feeds the bank engine and insights. |
| `daysWithData` / `loggedDays` | Count of days with at least one food entry. `loggedDays` is the field on `InsightStats` that gates most Nutrition insight unlocks. |
| `daysInCycle` | Number of days in the current cycle: `differenceInDays(cycleEnd, effectiveCycleStart) + 1`. 7 normally, fewer for a partial first cycle. |
| `day shard` / `dailyLog` | Per-day AsyncStorage key holding that day's meals: `@trackkal:log:${date}` via `STORAGE_KEYS.dailyLog(date)`. Meals are sharded by date so a single day's read-modify-write is isolated (serialized by `withWriteLock`). |
| `deficit-surplus-ai` | Weight insight (`Deficit & Surplus Impact`). AI analysis of how eating affects weight. Unlocks at `calorieAndWeightDays >= 7`. A free-text (non-JSON-schema) prompt. |
| `DetectedPattern` | Premium pattern record: `type` (`'correlation' | 'trigger' | 'outcome'`), `title`, `description` (free sees), `fix` (premium-only advice), `confidence` (0–100, shown only if >70), `dataPoints`, `detectedAt`, `dismissed`. Produced by pattern detection. |
| `effectiveCycleStart` / `enabledDate` | `enabledDate` is when the bank was first turned on (ISO). If it falls after the raw cycle start, it becomes the effective start so days before the bank was on never count. |
| `expiredCalories` | Banked-but-unused calories at cycle reset: `max(0, totalBanked - totalSpent)`. Surfaced in the completed-cycle analytics. |
| `ExtendedGoalData` | The user's full goal/profile: `calories`, macro `%` and grams, `currentWeightKg`, `targetWeightKg`, `age`, `gender`, height fields, `goal` (`'lose' | 'maintain' | 'gain'`), `activityRate`/`activityLevel`, `name`, `dob`, `trackingGoal`. Stored under `@trackkal:goals`. |
| `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` | Launch flag in `src/config/featureFlags.ts`, currently `true`. While true, every signed-in user with email gets premium (no paywall). Set to `false` when paid tiers + RevenueCat go live. Signed-out users are unaffected because the `isPremium` check still requires an email. |
| `featureFlags` | Config object in `src/config/featureFlags.ts`. Currently gates `grocerySuggestions` to admin emails/IDs (`ADMIN_EMAILS`, `ADMIN_IDS`). |
| `gender floor` / `targetFloor` | Lower clamp on an adjusted daily target: `max(baseDailyTarget * 0.70, genderFloor)`, where `genderFloor` is 1200 for female, else 1500. Prevents the bank from ever setting a dangerously low day. |
| `goal-adherence` | First Nutrition insight (`Goal Adherence`), unlocks at `loggedDays >= 2`. Compares daily intake to targets. Historically the canonical unlock-landing example (use `scrollToInsight`). |
| `goalType` / `goal` | Direction of the plan: `'lose' | 'gain' | 'maintain'`. Flips the bank axis: for gain, eating over target banks the surplus and eating under spends it (inverse of lose/maintain). |
| `hashPrompt` | djb2-based hash (`src/utils/promptVersion.ts`) returning a base36 string. Used as a cache-key suffix so editing a prompt's text changes the hash and auto-invalidates stale cached entries. |
| `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS` | The ordered array of all 21 insight definitions in `src/utils/insightUnlockEngine.ts`. Each has `id`, `name`, `description`, `screen`, `icon`, `requirementText`, and a `check(stats)` predicate. |
| `InsightDefinition` | Shape of one insight: `id` (`InsightId`), `name`, `description`, `screen` (`'nutrition' | 'weight'`), `icon` (Feather name), `requirementText` (locked-state copy), `check`. |
| `InsightId` | Union of all insight identifiers (e.g. `'goal-adherence'`, `'macro-split'`, `'calorie-bank'`, `'ai-weekly-insight'`, `'bmi'`, `'weekly-rate'`, `'deficit-surplus-ai'`, `'milestones-records'`). 11 nutrition + 10 weight. |
| `InsightSlot` | Conceptual UI placement of an insight card on the Nutrition Analysis or Weight Tracker screen. Each slot wraps its content in an unlock gate (`isInsightUnlocked`) and shows a locked placeholder with `requirementText` until unlocked. |
| `InsightStats` | The data snapshot fed to every `check`: `loggedDays`, `uniqueFoods`, `weightEntries`, `weightEntrySpanDays`, `hasTargetWeight`, `hasHeight`, `calorieAndWeightDays`, `monthsWithWeightData`, `calorieBankEnabled`. |
| `InsightUnlockRecord` / `InsightUnlocks` | `InsightUnlockRecord` = `{ unlockedAt, seenAt? }`. `InsightUnlocks` = `Record<InsightId, InsightUnlockRecord>`. Stored under `@trackkal:insightUnlocks`. `seenAt` is set when the user dismisses the announcement card. |
| `isInsightUnlocked` | Gate function: `!!unlocks[id]`. Every insight card must call it before rendering. New insights require an entry in `INSIGHT_DEFINITIONS`. |
| `isPlanPremium` | Plan-string-only helper in `dataStorage.ts`: `plan === 'premium'`, or `premiumUntil` in the future. Explicitly NOT an entitlement check; named so nobody mistakes it for `isPremium`. Must be wrapped with the account check. |
| `isPremium` | The canonical entitlement gate (defined in `HomeScreen.tsx`). True only if there is a signed-in account with email AND (`FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH` is on, OR `userPlan === 'premium'`, OR `premiumUntil` is in the future). Never gate on plan alone. |
| `invokeAI` | The single client entry point to OpenAI (`src/services/aiProxyService.ts`). Wraps an `AIRequest` (`model`, `messages`, `temperature`, `max_tokens`, `response_format`, `call_type`, `timeout_ms`, `signal`), routes it through `ai-proxy`, default timeout 60_000 ms, composing caller + timeout abort signals. |
| `json_schema strict` | The `response_format: { type: 'json_schema', strict: true }` mode. All 5 JSON-returning prompts use it. Free-text prompts (Coach, Weekly Insights, Image Vision, Deficit & Surplus) do not. |
| `macro ratio` / `todayMacros` | Macros scaled to the adjusted target: `macroRatio = adjustedTodayTarget / baseDailyTarget`; each macro = `round(goalGrams * macroRatio)`. Keeps protein/carb/fat aligned with a bank-adjusted day. |
| `MealEntry` | One logged meal: `id`, `prompt` (user text), optional AI `summary`, `foods: ParsedFood[]`, `timestamp`, optional `imageUri`, `date`, `userId`, plus loading state (`isLoading`, `loadingState: 'analyzing' | 'done' | 'failed'`). Sharded into day keys. |
| `micro targets` / `MicroTargetSet` | Personalized per-day nutrient goals from age + sex (`src/utils/microTargets.ts`), sourced from NIH DRI/RDA, AHA, FDA Daily Values. Each `MicroTarget` is `{ value, unit ('g'|'mg'|'mcg'), kind ('target'|'limit') }`. Unknown age/sex falls back to adult-male defaults (age 30). |
| `MicroStatus` | Color-coding bucket for a nutrient vs its target: `'deficient'` (<50%), `'low'` (50–80%), `'on_track'` (80–120% of a target or under a limit), `'over'` (120–200%, or over a limit), `'way_over'` (>200%). Computed by `statusFor`/`percentOfTarget`. |
| `micronutrient-balance` | Nutrition insight (`Micronutrients`), unlocks at `loggedDays >= 5`. Vitamins, minerals, omega-3 vs personalized `MicroTargetSet`. |
| `pending cap` / `pendingDailyCapPercent` | A queued cap change (`pendingDailyCapPercent` / `pendingSpendingCapPercent` on `CalorieBankConfig`). Cap changes are not retroactive: the pending value waits until a cycle rollover promotes it to the active cap. |
| `ParsedFood` | One AI-parsed food item: name, macros, optional micros, and `confidence`/`confidence_reason` (`src/utils/foodNutrition.ts`). The unit a `MealEntry` is composed of. |
| `peakBankBalance` | Highest running bank balance reached during a cycle (floored at 0 each step). Recorded in the completed-cycle record. |
| `perDayData` | Array of `CalorieBankDayData` for every day in the cycle. The per-day ledger that all bank displays and aggregates read from. |
| `premiumUntil` | ISO date on `AccountInfo` marking a premium trial/expiry. Premium is active while `new Date(premiumUntil) > now`. One of the three ways `isPremium` can be true. |
| `promptVersion` | The versioning utility (`src/utils/promptVersion.ts`) exposing `hashPrompt`. Tags food-analysis and confidence-hint cache entries so prompt edits silently re-analyze stale entries on next read. |
| `quiet hours` | Smart-reminder window when no notifications fire: default `quietHoursStart: 22`, `quietHoursEnd: 7` (`smartReminderService.ts`). |
| `rawOverspend` | Past-days actual minus past-days expected (`pastDaysActual - pastDaysExpected`). Positive = overate. Used uncapped for downward redistribution (overage reduces future days by the full amount, not the capped `bankBalance`). |
| `remainingBudget` | `weeklyBudget - weeklyActual`, floored at 0. Calories left to spend in the cycle. |
| `remainingDays` | Days from today to cycle end inclusive (`isFuture || isToday` count). Divisor for `adjustmentPerDay`. |
| `sanitizeForAI` / `sanitizeObjectForAI` | Prompt-injection defenses (`src/utils/sanitizeAI.ts`). `sanitizeForAI` strips role-impersonation and override phrases (`ignore previous instructions`, `you are now`, etc.), control chars, collapses whitespace, and caps length (default 2000). `sanitizeObjectForAI` applies it recursively to string fields (default 500 chars/field). All user input must pass through one before any prompt. |
| `settleDay` | The shared per-day settlement function (`calorieBankEngine.ts`). Given base target, actual, goal type, and caps, returns `{ banked, spent, capHit, spendCapHit }`. Used by both the live and archival paths so they cannot drift. |
| `Smart Adjustment` | Premium feature suggesting new calorie/macro targets to prevent plateaus. Surfaced via `SmartAdjustmentBanner` ("Smart Plan Update Available", "Prevent plateaus with new targets") and `SmartAdjustmentModal`. Changes are recorded in `@trackkal:adjustmentHistory`. |
| `Smart Reminder` | AI-timed meal-logging notifications (`src/services/smartReminderService.ts`). Modes include `'smart'` (vs generic). Learns meal-timing patterns; respects quiet hours and per-slot toggles. Premium-gated via `isPlanPremium` + `FREE_PREMIUM_LAUNCH`. Caches in `@trackkal:smartReminder*` keys. |
| `Smart Suggest` | Premium feature proposing a meal to log next, shown in `SmartSuggestBanner` when `smartSuggestEnabled` is on. Returns `{ displayText, loggableText, reasoning }`; the log callback returns true only when a meal was actually logged so the button never falsely claims success. Powered by `generateSmartSuggestion`. |
| `soft-delete` | Deletion strategy where a remote row is marked deleted rather than removed, so a re-synced local copy does not resurrect it. `LAST_MEALS_SYNC_AT` (`@trackkal:lastMealsSyncAt`) lets the app distinguish "local meal pending sync" from "previously synced but now deleted remotely." |
| `spending cap` / `spendingCap` | Max calories a single past day may spend over base: `baseDailyTarget * (spendingCapPercent/100)`, where `spendingCapPercent ∈ {15,20,25}`. `targetCeiling = baseDailyTarget + spendingCap`. |
| `spent` | Capped overage on a past completed day. For lose/maintain it is `min(|baseTarget - actual|, spendingCap)` when over target; for gain, the capped shortfall. |
| `streak freeze` / `StreakFreezeData` | A token that preserves a logging streak across a missed day. `StreakFreezeData` = `{ freezesAvailable (0–2), lastResetDate (month start), usedOnDates[] }`. `checkMissedDaysAndFreeze` (`src/utils/streakLogic.ts`) auto-consumes one for an unlogged yesterday only if a streak was alive on D-2. Stored under `@trackkal:streakFreeze`. |
| `sync queue` / `SyncOperation` | The offline write queue (`@trackkal:syncQueue`). Each `SyncOperation` is a tagged union, e.g. `{ entity: 'meal', action: 'upsert', payload }` or `{ entity: 'meal', action: 'delete', payload: { id } }`. Drained to Supabase in the background; AsyncStorage stays authoritative. |
| `targetCeiling` | Upper clamp on an adjusted daily target: `baseDailyTarget + spendingCap`. An adjusted day can never exceed base plus one day's spending cap. |
| `unlock threshold` | The condition in an insight's `check(stats)` that flips it from locked to unlocked (e.g. `loggedDays >= 3`, `weightEntries >= 5 && weightEntrySpanDays >= 14`, `calorieAndWeightDays >= 7`). The `requirementText` is the human-readable version. |
| `UserMetricsSnapshot` | A precomputed bundle (`@trackkal:userMetricsSnapshot`) of `userGoals` (calories, protein, carbs, fat, goalType) and `averages7Day` (calories, macros, and a full set of micros: fiber, sugar, added sugars, net carbs, saturated/trans/poly/mono fat, sodium, potassium, etc.). Fed to AI prompts so the model reasons over the user's real recent numbers. |
| `utilization` / `bankUtilization` | How much of the banked total was actually used: `min(100, round((totalSpent / totalBanked) * 100))`; 0 if nothing was banked. Surfaced in the Calorie Bank insight and completed-cycle analytics. |
| `WeeklyActionPlan` | Premium weekly plan: `weekStartDate` (Monday ISO) and a list of `actions` (`description`, `rationale`, `completed?`). Stored under `@trackkal:weeklyActionPlan`. |
| `weeklyActual` vs `weeklyLoggedActual` | `weeklyActual` totals all non-future days including unlogged past days assumed at base. `weeklyLoggedActual` counts only days the user actually logged, so an unlogged day's assumed base does not fill the "used" bar in the UI. |
| `weeklyBudget` | Total calories allotted for the cycle: `baseDailyTarget * daysInCycle`. The denominator for budget/remaining displays. |
| `WeightEntry` | One scale reading: `{ date (ISO), weight (kg), id?, updatedAt? }`. Stored under `@trackkal:weightEntries`. Count and span drive Weight Tracker insight unlocks. |
